The Katariah

**The Katariah** is the personal transport vessel of the Emperor, [Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)").

The ship has an exterior (the deck) and two interior zones: *[The Katariah](#The_Katariah)* and the *[Emperor's Quarters](#Emperor.27s_Quarters)*.

It only appears after the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") has been started, anchored off-shore in the mouth of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") near [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Passengers & Crew | | --- | | **[Captain Avidius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Avidius "Skyrim:Captain Avidius")**  **[Emperor Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)")** \* **[Lieutenant Salvarus](/wiki/Skyrim:Lieutenant_Salvarus "Skyrim:Lieutenant Salvarus")**  **[Penitus Oculatus Agents](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Agent "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Agent")**  **[Sailors](/wiki/Skyrim:Sailor "Skyrim:Sailor")** | |

\* This person dies upon the completion of [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")

## Related Quests

- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Windshear

The figurehead of Katariah

Throne area

The main exterior area for the ship is the deck area which can only be accessed from the interior. The initial access point to the ship is via the anchor chain at the stern of the ship leading through the hull into a storeroom in the lower hold. Access to the deck can be made through two exits, one from a ladder near the captain's quarters and one through a door opposite the emperor's quarters. The former of these opens a trapdoor under the forecastle on the main deck and gives the best concealment upon exiting, while the latter leads out onto the main deck beside the stairs leading up to the quarterdeck.

Under the forecastle beside the trapdoor is a long wooden table with a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak and several pieces of cheese on top. The decks have many stacks of crates, barrels and sacks containing provisions. There is a [sailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sailor "Skyrim:Sailor") and five [Penitus Oculatus agents](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Agent "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Agent") on deck, the sailor and one agent are on the main deck, one agent is on the forecastle, two are on the quarterdeck and one is on the poop deck. There are stairs leading up to the forecastle both to the port and starboard of the ship. On the forecastle, on the starboard side is a rowboat provisioned and containing an open crate containing a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), four bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead")—these are all owned and taking them is considered stealing. At the end of the bowsprit is a unique [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar") called [Windshear](/wiki/Skyrim:Windshear "Skyrim:Windshear"). (See the bugs section on that page if it's not there.) The figurehead on the front of the ship appears to be that of an elven maiden.

The main deck has a novice-locked chest beside some crates, two long wooden tables and benches and two rowboats, one provisioned and one empty. The quarter deck has another rowboat that is provisioned and also holds an owned [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"). Beside this rowboat is a table and chairs with a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine and a loaf of bread on top. The poop deck is where the ship's wheel is located and has a throne for the Emperor with a small table beside it, with a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[King](/wiki/Skyrim:King "Skyrim:King")*, a bottle of wine and three [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins on top.

### The Katariah

Storeroom

Entrance to the Katariah is made via the anchor chain that takes you into a large storeroom containing many crates, barrels containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), food sacks and an apprentice-locked chest. Upon entering there is a sailor just leaving the room. Among the crates on the floor, on the port side is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and to the starboard, is a random [potion of light feet](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Light_Feet "Skyrim:Potion of Light Feet") hidden behind a lit lantern, on a barrel. Any noise can alert several sailors and a Penitus Oculatus agent. There are crates, sacks and barrels containing provision throughout the interior. Stairs to the south lead into a wide corridor with a bedroom on the right containing a sailor, three single beds, a table and chairs, a wooden bench and a small bookcase holding five common books and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). On the table is another common book, a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a small coin purse and four gold coins. Leaning against the south wall, next to the wooden bench is an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"). All the beds onboard are unowned. You can hear someone ahead working metal on an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil").

To the east is another open door to a bedroom containing three more single beds, a small table and chair, a wooden bench and a dresser, which has an [Imperial helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet") on top and an Imperial sword on the floor in front of it. The corridor is staggered to the south passing a table and a couple of chairs. Ahead is yet another open door, with a set of shelves before it on the right holding seven common books, a bottle of alto wine and two bottles of wine. As you approach the end of the corridor there is an opening on the right into a dining room containing two sailors and an agent, the room is double height with a balcony around the upper area. Any noise when dealing with these sailors and agent can bring several agents and sailors to investigate. The room at the end of the corridor is another bedroom which contains five single beds, two dressers, a wardrobe, an end table, a table built around a support pillar and a couple of chairs. To the left of the first dresser is a pair of [Imperial boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Boots"), with some cheese on the second. The wardrobe and dressers all contain common [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), while on the end table is a [gold ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Ring") and a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring") and on one of the beds in the southeastern corner is a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe").

The dining room contains many tables and to the north is a counter with a sideboard behind, these hold an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a total of six bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), many pieces of cheese, several loaves of bread, a gourd, four portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), four [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"). On the west wall are two shield plaques each holding an [Imperial shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Shield") and two crossed Imperial swords. To the south is a doorway into another storeroom with a pair of bookcases flanking it. These hold a total of sixteen common books and a random potion of healing. Inside the room are two sideboards and a cupboard. On the sideboards are many more pieces of cheese, a bulb of garlic, a portion of grilled leeks, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a fillet of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* and a couple of loaves of bread. On the floor to the right of the cupboard is a medium coin purse.

The cells

In the dining room, stairs leading up to the balcony overhead are in the northwest corner. There is an expert-locked door near the top of the stairs, with a dresser and chair to the right and to the south is the balcony seen from below with two agents sat on the far side of it facing away from you. Along the west wall are a row of three unlocked cells each containing an unowned bedroll and little else of interest. There is an unlocked door on the north wall that leads into a bedroom containing a sailor as well as a dead sailor and agent. There are four single beds, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), an end table, a long wooden table and several chairs. Behind the lab, on a crate is a random [potion of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"), while on the long table is an apothecary's satchel, a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a portion of grilled leeks, a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a loaf of bread, some cheese and leaning against a chair against the west wall is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute").

Another unlocked door is in the middle of the east wall, the sounds of someone hammering on an anvil appear to be coming from this room. In the room is an agent either using the anvil or a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") with a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") beside these. On the workbench is a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") and on the wall are a total of eight weapon racks holding four Imperial swords and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"). At the northern end of the room is a sideboard with a set of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"), a pair of [Imperial bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers") and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") on top, a pair of [Imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots") on the floor beside it. To the right are shelves holding an [Imperial helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet") and a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), with an [Imperial shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Shield") and a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") on a couple of crates.

On the southern side of the balcony are two tables, where the two agents were sitting, a corridor with cupboards flanking it, the one to the southeast holds a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). The short corridor to the south leads into another storage area with a ladder leading up to the deck of the ship directly in front of you and a door to the right. Around against the north wall is a table with a satchel on top, there is nothing else of interest apart from a few more barrels of ingredients in this area. The door to the right is unlocked and opens into [Captain Avidius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Avidius "Skyrim:Captain Avidius")' room.

Captain Avidius' room

The room contains a double bed in the southwest corner, with a small table beside it and a dresser at the foot of the bed with a pair of random gauntlets and a random [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration") on top, with a lute leaning against the side of it. In front of the dresser, against the south wall is a master-locked chest, while against the north wall is a long wooden table with flute, a small coin purse and three gold coins on top and to the right is a set of shelves holding a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a random potion of healing, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and a flute. Further to the right of these is a wardrobe containing random clothing and a wooden bench. Finally beside the door as you leave are two hooks with a copy of [Katariah master key](/wiki/Skyrim:Katariah_Master_Key "Skyrim:Katariah Master Key"), which opens any and all doors on the ship including the door to the Emperor's quarters. Copies of this key are also carried by Captain Avidius, [Lieutenant Salvarus](/wiki/Skyrim:Lieutenant_Salvarus "Skyrim:Lieutenant Salvarus") and [Emperor Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") himself.

Beyond the expert-locked door is another corridor with a bedroom on the immediate left containing an agent sat in a chair, three single beds, a bookcase holding three common books, a drum and a row of mountain flowers including five [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), five [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and one [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a wardrobe and in a small area to the northeast is a set of shelves holding a medium coin purse with a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") in front.

Opposite this room is an area with a wooden bench, a dresser and chair with an open door beside them. This leads into another bedroom containing two more agents, one of which is normally sleeping. There are four more single beds, an end table, a wardrobe, a dresser, a cupboard holding an iron mace, and a table and chairs in the room. The corridor continues to the north, where there is a door and two corridors heading east and west. Both of these lead around to stairs leading up to another room above. The door opens into a library, Lieutenant Salvarus is standing right behind the door and will spot and attack as soon as you enter. In the middle of the room is a table covered with a tactical map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), an iron dagger and a copy of *[Mixed Unit Tactics](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixed_Unit_Tactics "Skyrim:Mixed Unit Tactics")*. There are a total of six bookcases along the rear wall containing many common books, a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a random empty soul gem, a satchel and an iron dagger, with a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") on the floor to the right of them.

The corridor to the west has a small table with a bottle of alto wine on top beside a wooden bench. The room at the top has two doors, one master-locked leading to the Emperor's quarters and the other leading outside. There are long end tables on either side of the Emperor's door, one of which has a couple of [candlesticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") on top, while the other has a common book and [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") on top. To the right of the door leading outside is a long wooden table with an empty random soul gem, three common books and an apothecary's satchel on top, with two bunches of dried elves ear and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from the ceiling above. To the right is a cupboard and a set of shelves holding a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") and three more common books and to the left of the door outside is another cupboard this one holds four bottles of alto wine, five bottles of wine, a flute and a drum.

### Emperor's Quarters

First room

These consist of two rooms, the first is the Emperor's office and dining area while the second is up a few stairs to the west and are his sleeping quarters. The office is lavishly appointed with several richly woven rugs, many banners hanging from the walls and between the stained glass rear windows and many fancy [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), goblets, bowls, etc around the room. A desk, at which the Emperor himself can be found sat during the quest [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"), is opposite the door with a tactical map of Skyrim on top along with a bottle of wine, several common books and a copy of *[Brothers of Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Brothers_of_Darkness "Skyrim:Brothers of Darkness")*. To the left as you enter the room is a small unit holding two bottles of alto wine, two of wine and two of Nord mead. Next to this is a small table and chair with a common book on the table. Opposite is a small sideboard with a bowl containing [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and in front a low table with a honey nut treat and [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") on top. To the east is a dining table laid for one, with a [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef") steak, two portions of grilled leeks, a bowl of [tomato soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato_Soup "Skyrim:Tomato Soup"), a seared slaughterfish steak, a baked potato, two loaves of bread, a bulb of garlic, a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), and a piece of cheese on top.

Dining area

Around the dining table is a sideboard, a set of shelves holding two bottles of alto wine and one of wine, a narrow table holding two sprigs of snowberries, a bunch of lavender, a red mountain flower and an expert-locked display case containing a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), with a weapon plaque hanging on the wall above holding a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword"). Next to this is a bookcase with eleven common books and copies of *[The Dragon War](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dragon_War "Skyrim:The Dragon War")*, *[The Adabal-a](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Adabal-a "Skyrim:The Adabal-a")* and *[On Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Oblivion "Skyrim:On Oblivion")* on the shelves. Behind the desk along the stern wall are a pair of small wardrobes containing fine clothes, with an adept-locked display case on top containing a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") on the floor to the left, a sideboard with a copy of *[The Rise and Fall of the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Blades "Skyrim:The Rise and Fall of the Blades")* on top and a small unit with several more common books and a bottle of wine on the shelves. Against the west wall to the right of the sleeping quarters is a giant map of Skyrim with a wall shelf above a sideboard with rolls of paper on top holding three common books. An adept-locked door in the port side bulkhead provides access to a narrow outdoor balcony, that makes for a quick getaway after you pay your respects to the Emperor.

Sleeping quarters

The door to the sleeping quarters is expert-locked. The room contains a four-poster double bed coming out of the south wall, with an end table with a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* on top to the left and a sideboard at the foot of the bed with a set of [Emperor's robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Emperor's Robes"), a [gold ruby necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ruby_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Ruby Necklace"), a small coin purse, five gold coins and an open crate containing two gold rings, silver ring and a [flawless ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Ruby "Skyrim:Flawless Ruby") on top. To the left of the bed is a wash basin and sideboard with a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") beside it, while to the right is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes, and a sideboard with an apothecary's satchel, a leveled [potion of glibness](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Glibness "Skyrim:Potion of Glibness"), a leveled potion of healing, a flute and a copy of *[Glories and Laments](/wiki/Skyrim:Glories_and_Laments "Skyrim:Glories and Laments")* on top. Against the northwest wall is a small wardrobe with a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on top and a lute leaning against it, with a long unlocked chest to the right and further to the right of this is a bookcase with a satchel, a unique pair of [gilded wristguards](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilded_Wristguards "Skyrim:Gilded Wristguards"), a random helmet, a couple of candlesticks, six common books and a copy of *[Sovngarde: A Reexamination](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde:_A_Reexamination "Skyrim:Sovngarde: A Reexamination")* on the shelves. Behind the door is a corner shelf with several common books and a random filled soul gem in a holder.

## Notes

- The ship is named after [Empress Katariah](/wiki/Lore:Katariah "Lore:Katariah").

## Bugs

- The Katariah is erroneously flagged as a dungeon; radiant quests choosing it as a target location require the completion of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") questline to retrieve the target object.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- The quest controlling scenes on board the Katariah don't start properly due to a bad story manager node condition.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- One of the Penitus Oculatus agents respawns despite the ship being classed as a "no reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- The ship has no distant LOD, meaning it will pop out of nowhere when you get close.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Some beverages and potions on the ship are mistakenly set as owned.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- The Katariah may partially despawn as you move away from it. This results in shipboard objects apparently floating in midair, and NPCs falling into the water.
- You may find [Lisette](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisette "Skyrim:Lisette") in the ship's mess hall or dead on the deck after [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!").

# Skyrim:The Lady Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

The Lady Stone

**The Lady Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim").

.jpg)

The Lady Stone, when activated

*Those under the sign of [The Lady](/wiki/Lore:The_Lady "Lore:The Lady") regenerate [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") and [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") more quickly.*

Activating the Lady Stone provides the player with a 25% boost to both health and stamina regeneration rates.

## The Lady Stone

It can be found in middle of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), on an island directly north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). There are a few upright stones flanking it and many [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") on the island and around the stones. You will also find many [monarch butterfies](/wiki/Skyrim:Monarch_Butterfly "Skyrim:Monarch Butterfly") and [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") during the day and [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth") and [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") in the evening and at night. Three [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") linger near the island which will attack if they see you. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") can be found on the southwestern end of the island.

## Notes

- The treasure chest for [Treasure Map X](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_X "Skyrim:Treasure Map X") is located underwater just east and slightly north of the stone.
- The [loading screen](/wiki/Skyrim:Loading_Screens#Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Loading Screens") for The Lady Stone implies the stone provides a power rather than a constant effect ability, which is incorrect.

# Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. | **Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").** | |

The Litany of Larceny

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find the [Queen Bee Statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Bee_Statue "Skyrim:Queen Bee Statue") in [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate") and bring it to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory").
2. Find the [Honningbrew Decanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Decanter "Skyrim:Honningbrew Decanter") in [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery").
3. Find the [East Empire Shipping Map](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Shipping_Map "Skyrim:East Empire Shipping Map") in the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
4. Find the [Model Ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Model_Ship "Skyrim:Model Ship") in [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum").
5. Find the [Dwemer Puzzle Cube](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Puzzle_Cube "Skyrim:Dwemer Puzzle Cube") in [Calcelmo's Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo%27s_Laboratory "Skyrim:Calcelmo's Laboratory") within [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").
6. Find the [Bust of the Gray Fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Bust_of_the_Gray_Fox "Skyrim:Bust of the Gray Fox") in [Riftweald Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
7. Find the [Left Eye of the Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Eye_of_the_Falmer "Skyrim:Left Eye of the Falmer") in the Dwemer ruin [Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand").

## Detailed Walkthrough

During the course of the Thieves Guild questline, you may run into one of several unique items in locations relevant to the quests. Picking them up will add a miscellaneous task to take it to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), who will pay a leveled amount of money for the item.

### The Queen Bee Statue

The Queen Bee Statue in Aringoth's quarters

The first trinket that you will likely encounter is the [Queen Bee Statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Bee_Statue "Skyrim:Queen Bee Statue"). It is found on a bedside table in [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth")'s room in [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate"). This location is visited in the Thieves Guild quest [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear"). When picked up, a prompt will tell you to return the item to Delvin Mallory.

### The Honningbrew Decanter

The [Honningbrew Decanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Decanter "Skyrim:Honningbrew Decanter") is located in a room in the upper floor of the [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery"), behind the door which has an expert lock. You will most likely come across it during the quest [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits").

### The East Empire Shipping Map

The [East Empire Shipping Map](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Shipping_Map "Skyrim:East Empire Shipping Map") can be found on a table next to some loot in the Dockmaster's office in the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"). It is easiest to acquire this during the quest [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly"); if you attempt to steal it at any other point, the warehouse may be patrolled by guards, who will attack you on sight if spotted.

### The Model Ship

The [Model Ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Model_Ship "Skyrim:Model Ship") is found on a booby-trapped pedestal in [Snow Veil Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Catacombs "Skyrim:Snow Veil Catacombs"). The pedestal is surrounded by oil, and removal of the ship causes the oil to burst into flame. It is fairly easy to grab the ship near the doorway and retreat to avoid the fire. It is also possible to shoot one of the exploding urns that fall to set off the trap; however, this causes the ship to fly away from the resulting explosion—into a wall, behind a cabinet or even into the room below—making it easy to lose. Another option is to shoot the ship away from the oil on the ground. Be aware that picking up the ship will still trigger the urns. Another option, if you know the Telekinesis spell, is to stand away from the oil and use the spell to retrieve the ship. Another option is to place an item on the pedestal, preventing the trap from activating when you take the ship. The last option would be to use the "Slow Time" shout. Go right up to the pedestal, shout, immediately grab the ship and run away from the oil. Even if you only have the first word of the shout, you will have plenty of time to watch the urns fall to the ground. Of course, you can always set the oil on fire yourself and let it burn up, then take the ship, but the urns will still injure you a bit if you stand too close. Use any flame spell (besides cloak) or the "Fire Breath" shout. You can also use whirlwind sprint, grab the ship, and immediately sprint away from the oil. You visit Snow Veil Catacombs during the quest [Speaking with Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence").

### The Dwemer Puzzle Cube

The [Dwemer Puzzle Cube](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Puzzle_Cube "Skyrim:Dwemer Puzzle Cube") is in [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo")'s Laboratory, which is accessed via the Dwemer Museum in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"). It is found in the large room with the Arcane Enchanter, just before moving on to the balcony. You travel through the laboratory during the quest [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers").

### The Bust of the Gray Fox

The [Bust of the Gray Fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Bust_of_the_Gray_Fox "Skyrim:Bust of the Gray Fox") is found on a table in [Riftweald Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") during the quest [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit"). It is easy to miss as it blends perfectly with the stone behind it, but it's sitting right next to the quest objective.

### The Left Eye of the Falmer

The [Left Eye of the Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Eye_of_the_Falmer "Skyrim:Left Eye of the Falmer") can be taken from Mercer Frey's corpse in the [Irkngthand Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Irkngthand Sanctuary") during the quest [Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted"). After you turn in the Left Eye of the Falmer to Delvin, you can steal it back from its shelf in the Cistern within the Ragged Flagon, and sell it again to Tonilia to double your profit.

### Reward

This is the amount of gold you get each time you turn in an item, except the eye with four times higher reward. The total amount of gold you can accumulate ranges from 50 to 800 gold.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 200 |
| 16-20 | 300 |
| 21-26 | 400 |
| 27-31 | 500 |
| 32-36 | 600 |
| 37-41 | 700 |
| 42+ | 800 |

## Bugs

- It does not matter what order you pick up the items, after picking up the final item the quest will be marked as complete and you will be no longer able to turn any of the items still in your inventory to Delvin Mallory.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes you cannot sell the Left Eye of the Falmer to Delvin.
  - Select the Eye through the console by entering `PRID 000e8efe` . Type `Enable` in the console. The item should now be visible on the shelf. Type `Player.RemoveItem 0001994f 1` to remove the Eye from your inventory if you cannot otherwise do so.
- The quest Hard Answers sometimes triggers when retrieving the Dwemer Puzzle Cube after it has already been completed. **?**
  -  Using the console enter `SetStage TG06 200` . The quest will now move to the completed section of your quest journal. If desired, the duplicate [Nightingale Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Blade "Skyrim:Nightingale Blade") may be removed by entering `Player.RemoveItem 000f6527 1` via the console.
- Sometimes the East Empire Shipping Map will not appear in the East Empire Company Warehouse, even after the associated quest is completed. **?**
- Items that were once on the shelves are now missing or somewhere else in the room.
  - Select the item(s) through the console by entering `PRID X` where X corresponds to the ID referencing the item in question (see list below). Type `RecycleActor` in the console. Repeat as necessary.

:   :   ```
        00019958 Queen Bee Statue
        00019952 Honningbrew Decanter
        00060cc2 East Empire Shipping Map
        0006f266 Model Ship
        0005598c Dwemer Puzzle Cube
        00019954 Bust of the Gray Fox
        0001994f Left Eye of the Falmer
        ```

As of 1.9.32 Official patch IDs are different:

:   :   ```
        e8ef8 Queen Bee Statue
        e8ef9 Honningbrew Decanter
        e8efa East Empire Shipping Map
        e8efb Model Ship
        e8efc Dwemer Puzzle Cube
        e8efd Bust of the Gray Fox
        e8efe Left Eye of the Falmer
        ```

## Quest Stages

| The Litany of Larceny (TGLarceny) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | I've discovered an unusual statue of a queen bee within Goldenglow Estate. I should take it to Delvin Mallory at the Ragged Flagon to determine its true value. *Objective 20:* Return the Queen Bee Statue to Delvin |
| 30 |  | I've discovered an unusual golden decanter inside Honningbrew Meadery. I should take it to Delvin Mallory at the Ragged Flagon to determine its true value. *Objective 30:* Return the Honningbrew Decanter to Delvin |
| 40 |  | I've discovered what appears to be a shipping map for the East Empire Company. I should take it to Delvin Mallory at the Ragged Flagon to determine its true value. *Objective 40:* Return the East Empire Shipping Map to Delvin |
| 50 |  | I've discovered the intricately crafted model of a sailing ship inside Snow Veil Sanctum. I should take it to Delvin Mallory at the Ragged Flagon to determine its true value. *Objective 50:* Return the Ship Model to Delvin |
| 60 |  | I've discovered an curious Dwemer-constructed puzzle cube inside Calcelmo's Quarters in Markarth. I should take it to Delvin Mallory at the Ragged Flagon to determine its true value. *Objective 60:* Return the Dwemer Puzzle Cube to Delvin |
| 70 |  | I've discovered the bust of a man named the Gray Fox inside Mercer Frey's House. I should take it to Delvin Mallory at the Ragged Flagon to determine its true value. *Objective 70:* Return the Bust of the Gray Fox to Delvin |
| 80 |  | I've recovered one of the Eyes of the Falmer from Irkngthand. I should take it to Delvin Mallory at the Ragged Flagon to determine its true value. *Objective 80:* Return the Eye of the Falmer to Delvin |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 25, 35, 45, 55, 65, 75, 85, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGLarceny stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGLarceny`.

# Skyrim:The Lord Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Lord Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Lord+Stone)) | | |

| Occupants | |

| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), Northeast of the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon") | |

The Lord Stone

**The Lord Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim.

.jpg)

The Lord Stone, when activated

Activating The Lord Stone will add 50 points to your [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") rating and 25% [magic resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic"). This makes it easier to reach the [armor rating](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Rating "Skyrim:Armor Rating") and [magic resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") caps. Its effect is generic and useful for characters of all levels and play styles, providing decent all-around protection. [The Atronach Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Atronach_Stone "Skyrim:The Atronach Stone") is more effective at mitigating magic, but comes with a drawback and offers no physical protection.

## The Lord Stone

The Lord Stone is located on top of a stone base with the remains of a large arch on either side of it. It can be reached by following the path that leads past the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"). The path starts to the west of the [Hall of the Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant"). There are several piles of rocks marking the route; some have the remnants of banners hanging from them and flapping in the wind. You'll pass [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") along the path; once you reach a long flight of stone steps cut into the mountain leading up to the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon, turn to face northeast. You'll see the Lord Stone a short distance up a hill.

The Lord Stone is home to a group of three [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), at least one of whom is an archer. There are three unowned bed rolls arranged around a small campfire in front of the standing stone. There is also a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") at the southwest corner of the base of the structure upon which the stone is set. The path near the shrine is home to a leveled animal, which can be an [ice wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"), [ice wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), [snow bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear") or [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"), depending on your level when on the mountain pass.

## Notes

- A [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") with The Lord Stone and [Agent of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Mara "Skyrim:Agent of Mara") power will have a permanent 65% resistance to all magic. This can be achieved straight out of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound") at level 1 with almost no combat involved.
- Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") assigns The Lord Stone to [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") instead.

# Skyrim:The Lost Expedition

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Alethius](/wiki/Skyrim:Alethius "Skyrim:Alethius") (posthumously) |
| Location(s): | [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold reward |
| ID: | dunNchuandZelQst |
| Suggested Level: | 16 |

*"By the Nine I cannot determine the purpose of this tree. It appears to be from the area around Whiterun, but why and how it got here is beyond me."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") and ask to investigate the dig site.
2. Recover [Alethius'](/wiki/Skyrim:Alethius "Skyrim:Alethius") note.
3. Find the expedition members and recover their journals.
4. Re-activate Nchuand-Zel's automated defenses.
5. Speak to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") about the expedition.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Proceed inside [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel") until you encounter [Nimhe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe "Skyrim:Nimhe"). After killing [Nimhe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe "Skyrim:Nimhe"), head up the steps to find the dead body of [Alethius](/wiki/Skyrim:Alethius "Skyrim:Alethius"). Pick up the [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Alethius%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Alethius's Notes") next to his body to begin this quest.

Burn through the webbing behind his body with fire magic to enter [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel"). In the first hallway there is a pressure pad that activates a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap"). Continuing on, you will emerge into a huge open cavern with multiple levels, with [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") standing guard on a few of the connecting walkways. At the end of the large walkway is the entrance to Nchuand-Zel Quarters.

In this zone, you will encounter quite a number of Falmer, usually in groups. After exiting the first corridor, there will be two ways to go: downstairs or straight ahead. Proceed straight ahead first. When you reach a second set of stairs, there is an adept-locked door to the right containing random leveled loot. At the bottom of these stairs is a large group of Falmer (around 4 - 5). Proceed through these corridors until you come across a large door. To the left of this door is a small room with a bunch of Dwemer items. The door leads to a small balcony overlooking Nchuand-Zel, and also contains a chest with random leveled loot. Head back inside Nchuand-Zel Quarters.

### Nchuand-Zel Quarters

Head back to the first set of descending stairs you encountered after coming into the Quarters and proceed down them. You will encounter more Falmer along the way. Head up some stairs, making sure to avoid the rune trap at the top, and you will notice a table to the right against a wall. On this table is *[Stromm's Diary](/wiki/Skyrim:Stromm%27s_Diary "Skyrim:Stromm's Diary")*, which you will need for the quest. After picking this up, you will be tasked to collect three other journals: [Erj's](/wiki/Skyrim:Erj%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Erj's Notes"), [Krag's](/wiki/Skyrim:Krag%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Krag's Journal") and [Staubin's](/wiki/Skyrim:Staubin%27s_Diary "Skyrim:Staubin's Diary"). In the area to the left of this table are the actual Living Quarters, where you will find many Dwemer items, as well as beds you can sleep in. Head back out and past the table until you get to what looks to be a torture room. On the left-hand side of the doorway (as you enter the room) is a lever. Pulling it activates the spike trap on the table next to you. Now head back out to the door where you entered the Quarters from.

Backtrack a short distance until you have to turn right (which faces you towards the entrance of the zone). Instead of turning right, head to the left where a ramp will lead you to a lower level. You will notice the balcony you arrived at earlier when heading down this ramp. At the bottom, there are two ways to go. Heading left leads you to a platform a Falmer is (or was) standing on. Instead, go straight down the next ramp which will lead you to the bottom of the area. An adept level gate on your right holds a chest with random loot. Head down the path away from the gate. The path leads to a body of water, so head in and start swimming around to the left until you see another ramp (underwater) leading to a door, which leads to Nchuand-Zel Armory. Enter it. (Note: It is possible to get here by jumping off any of the bridges you have been traversing, or by jumping off the balcony from earlier).

### Nchuand-Zel Armory

Upon entering the Armory, there are two ways to go: down the corridor or up the stairs. Head through the corridor first. Soon you will come across an adept locked gate, and upon unlocking you will have to go up some stairs. At the top of the stairs is a dead Falmer and [Erj's](/wiki/Skyrim:Erj "Skyrim:Erj") body, along with his diary and a chest containing random loot. The first room to the left at the top of the stairs has nothing of interest, but the second room to the left has an expert-locked gate which leads to a chest with some random loot. Across from that gate is another expert-locked gate with a full set of [Dwarven armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armor "Skyrim:Dwarven Armor"). Upon approaching the next gate, a Falmer appears and a [Dwarven Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") awakens and does battle with it. The next gate has nothing of interest and after that is another corridor. The pressure plate ahead of you will activate a spear trap behind you. The next pressure plate up the stairs activates a [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") behind you. After this, there will be two ways to go. Head right. A Falmer is keeping watch ahead of you. Just ahead of him are the stairs you saw when first entering this area (heading through the corridor instead of the steps guarantees you will avoid the traps should you stand on a pressure plate). Head back and go the other way, which brings you to a door leading to Nchuand-Zel.

Upon going through the door, you will immediately come across [Krag's](/wiki/Skyrim:Krag "Skyrim:Krag") body and his journal. Head up the ramp (past an [Imperial soldier's](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") corpse) which brings you to the final zone: Nchuand-Zel Control. The rocky ramp to the right of the door serves as a shortcut back to the entrance of the ruin.

### Nchuand-Zel Control

After entering the door, continue through the corridor, encountering more Falmer along the way. A pressure plate just before the upwards ramp activates an [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"), so either avoid it or wait until it finishes. At the end of the corridor at the top of the ramp are two more Falmer; you will want to attack the one on the right first as it magic-based in combat. The other has both a bow and a sword. The pressure plate in the middle of this corridor activates a spike trap from the ceiling. Be careful of this if you have a follower, as he or she is likely to trigger this trap; even if your follower is essential/permanent, the spikes can kill him or her if they are still going while he/she is crouched. At the end of the corridor, turn left and you will see [Staubin's](/wiki/Skyrim:Staubin "Skyrim:Staubin") body and his journal, along with a damaged Dwarven Spider. Picking up the final journal grants you a new objective: Re-activate Nchuand-Zel's defenses.

Head past the body and up the steps where you will encounter some Dwarven constructs. At first, there should only be a few Dwarven Spider Workers, but fighting them awakens a couple of Dwarven Spheres. Fighting these can draw the attention of a Falmer, if it was not defeated before the Spheres turned their focus towards you. Continue to the end and you will reach a room with a table and a chest. On top of the table is a leveled healing potion, a Falmer Bow, and a lever. Pulling the lever completes the objective and opens up the gate behind you, so head through. Through the gate and at the end of the corridor is a chest. Now just jump off the bridge to end up back at the entrance door.

Upon exiting, you will see a Dwarven automaton fighting a Falmer. This is actually happening all throughout the ruin. Feel free to stay and join the fight, or just head up the ramp to the left and back to the entrance of Nchuand-Zel. Head back to Understone Keep and talk to Calcelmo to receive your reward and finish the quest. Your arrow may point back to the Armory at this point; see "Bugs".

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Bugs

- If you collect Krag's journal before you get the quest, you won't be prompted for getting Krag's journal, but you can still complete the quest.
- After pulling the lever at the end of the quest, the quest arrow may point to the armory. If it does, just head back to Calcelmo and the quest arrow should reset itself when you exit Nchuand-Zel.
- If you take a follower with you, that follower will not be able to take the "short cut" with you back to Nchuand-Zel's entrance after you reactivate the defenses, as NPCs cannot jump down off the ledge overlooking the exit path. The follower will run back to the upper armory door instead, trying to reach you the long way around.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - A workaround is to jump into the water and the follower will follow. It is then possible to climb the spiral ramp back to the exit level.
  - Alternatively, before jumping down onto the exit path yourself, order your follower to wait at the end of the ledge. You can then use the weakest form of the Unrelenting Force shout to push your follower over the edge and onto the main path. Be careful not to use Unrelenting Force's full power or you are likely to send your follower flying into the water.
  - You could also part ways with your follower before jumping off the ledge. They should be back home upon exiting.
- You may not be able to get through the webbing behind Alethius.
  - Move the body further from the webbing and try again.
  - Use concentration spells like Flames on the webbing.
- In patched versions of the game, reading any of the journals when they are on the ground will automatically give you a copy of them. If you then choose to "Take" the journal, you will end up with two copies. The quest can still be completed as normal, and both copies can be dropped after it is completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- [Nimhe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe "Skyrim:Nimhe") may respawn in the time it takes you to complete this quest and return to the excavation site; this does not affect the quest so you can just run past her.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- After killing [Nimhe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe "Skyrim:Nimhe"), you may not be able to cut through the entrance to the chambers beyond (webbing treated as solid object). You may need to launch an earlier saved game. **?**
  - The game may be treating your swings as hitting Alesius' body. Try dragging him further away from the webbing or using fire spells.
- If you happen to read and pick up any or all of the three journals before Stromm's, the game may not remember this, even though they are now in your inventory, and you will be unable to complete the quest normally: that is, without console commands.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Lost Expedition (dunNchuandZelQst) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |

Hopefully they're still alive. *Objective 20:* Recover Erj's journal  *Objective 30:* Recover Krag's journal  *Objective 40:* Recover Staubs' *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* journal |
| 50 |  | It appears the entire party was wiped out trying to reactivate the city's defenses. I need to find the lever Staubs *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* mentioned and activate it. *Objective 50:* Re-activate Nchuand-Zel's automated defenses |
| 100 |  | I've successfully activated the city's remaining automatons. They should be more then *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* capable of driving the remaining Falmer out. I should see if anyone is looking for the expedition. *Objective 100:* Find someone who knows about the expedition. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunNchuandZelQst stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunNchuandZelQst`.

# Skyrim:The Lost Library

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Locate a huge collection of powerful spell tomes.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | None |
| Location(s): | [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave") |
| Reward: | 16 [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories_Items#Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories Items") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE014\_SpellPack\_StartupQuest |
| Added by: | [Arcane Accessories](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories") |

The Ancient Tome Chest

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest no longer appears in your journal following the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update.

1. Travel to [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave").
2. Locate the Ancient Tome Chest within.

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Note: This quest was originally added to your journal upon installing the [Arcane Accessories](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), this quest no longer appears in your journal. Nevertheless, the rewards can still be obtained by finding the lost library yourself.**

The quest involves travelling to [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") to locate a long-lost archive of spell tomes. The cave is filled with [warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") enemies. The quest marker will lead you to an "Ancient Tome Chest" in a reading area found roughly halfway through the dungeon. For more precise directions, see the [dungeon walkthrough](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave#Hob.27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave"). Open the chest to complete the quest.

The chest contains all 16 [new spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories_Items#Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories Items") added by the Creation. Reading these will teach you the following spells:

:   |  |  |
    | --- | --- |
    | - *[Unbounded Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbounded_Flames "Skyrim:Unbounded Flames")* - *[Unbounded Freezing](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbounded_Freezing "Skyrim:Unbounded Freezing")* - *[Unbounded Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbounded_Storms "Skyrim:Unbounded Storms")* - *[Paralysis Rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Rune "Skyrim:Paralysis Rune")* - *[Pride of Hirstaang](/wiki/Skyrim:Pride_of_Hirstaang "Skyrim:Pride of Hirstaang")* - *[Elemental Flare](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Flare "Skyrim:Elemental Flare")* - *[Elemental Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Bolt "Skyrim:Elemental Bolt")* - *[Elemental Burst](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Burst "Skyrim:Elemental Burst")* | - *[Elemental Blast](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Blast "Skyrim:Elemental Blast")* - *[Orum's Aquatic Escape](/wiki/Skyrim:Orum%27s_Aquatic_Escape "Skyrim:Orum's Aquatic Escape")* - *[Fenrik's Welcome](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrik%27s_Welcome "Skyrim:Fenrik's Welcome")* - *[Mara's Wrath](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Wrath "Skyrim:Mara's Wrath")* - *[Choking Grasp](/wiki/Skyrim:Choking_Grasp "Skyrim:Choking Grasp")* - *[Strangulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Strangulation "Skyrim:Strangulation")* - *[Hangman's Noose](/wiki/Skyrim:Hangman%27s_Noose "Skyrim:Hangman's Noose")* - *[Touch of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Touch_of_Death "Skyrim:Touch of Death")* |

The spells obtained from these tomes are very powerful, as they use far less [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") than anything available in the base game with the same effect. If gameplay balance is a concern, you should note that you are not required to read or even take the tomes in order to complete the quest.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE014_SpellPack_StartupQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE014_SpellPack_StartupQuest`.

# Skyrim:The Lost Man's Reprieve

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Inn: The Lost Man's Reprieve ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Lost+Man%27s+Reprieve)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| HelgenExterior03, HelgenExterior07 | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") | |

The Lost Man's Reprieve

**The Lost Man's Reprieve** is a [tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") in [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") run and owned by [Vilod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilod "Skyrim:Vilod") that is destroyed at the start of the game.

You first see this building during the game's introductory sequence as you step down from the carriage that brought you to Helgen. It is the building directly behind [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") as he marks off the names of the prisoners on his list.

## Related Quests

- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.

## Walkthrough

This is the second structure you enter after [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") [interrupts your beheading](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"). Climbing up the stairs of the tower fortification, the dragon explodes through the side of the tower. You are urged to jump into the building below through the hole in its roof. It has two floors.

The tavern after the dragon attack

On the upper floor are two non-interactive beds, two set of shelves holding clutter, one of which has been knocked over, one table with an overturned chair, three food barrels, and five loose bottles of [mead with juniper berry](/wiki/Skyrim:Mead_with_Juniper_Berry "Skyrim:Mead with Juniper Berry"). Since your hands are still bound when you enter the house, there can be no interaction with surrounding items. There are no steps or ladder to the ground floor, and you must jump down from the east end through a large hole in the floor. The ground floor contains two tables with over-turned chairs, one wardrobe, one end table and one double bed. The building has several openings you can enter through; a northern door and several holes in the northern and eastern walls. You exit this building and join Hadvar or [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") for the remainder of the first quest.

Upon returning, you will find at least four [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") have occupied this southern end of Helgen after the town has been abandoned, three in the tavern and one at the top of the tower you initially escaped through. If you enter from the north, you'll find additional enemies. The building can be approached directly from the mountains to the south of it. On the large wooden table you will find a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and one of [strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), as well as a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). You can sleep in the double bed on the ground floor if you have defeated all the bandits in the area, including the one at the top of the tower. You can also then fast travel directly from the building.

## Notes

- During the initial quest, Unbound, Ralof mentions Vilod, who makes [mead with juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Mead_with_Juniper_Berry "Skyrim:Mead with Juniper Berry"). You can find these on the second floor. If they are not there, return after traveling for at least a day and check again. The bottles respawn every 10 days.
- The building can serve as a "home", since it has two safe containers and a bed, if you do not mind disposing of the respawning bandits.
  - However, when the bandits spawn inside, there is a chance they may be carrying anything you placed in the containers, including weapons.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:The_Lost_Man%27s_Reprieve)*]
- This building is unnamed and features no tavern sign. However, an [unused cell](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells "Skyrim:Test Cells") with the internal name `HelgenTheLostMansReprieve` uses tavern music, suggesting it may relate to this building.

## Bugs

- As the special mead bottles weren't properly enabled in the game data, they don't appear as you pass through the destroyed building during the introductory sequence.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- The double bed inside is inexplicably owned by the `RiverwoodAlvorsHouseFaction`, so you cannot sleep in it straight away.
  - Finishing the quest [Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm") or talking to [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor") will result in a disposition boost with him, which will allow you to use it properly.

# Skyrim:The Lost Paladin

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Find and claim the [Sword of Heroes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chrysamere_(item) "Skyrim:Chrysamere (item)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") |
| Reward: | [Chrysamere](/wiki/Skyrim:Chrysamere_(item) "Skyrim:Chrysamere (item)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE007\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Chrysamere](/wiki/Skyrim:Chrysamere "Skyrim:Chrysamere") |

The Lost Paladin, the previous wielder of Chrysamere

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Travel to [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost").
2. Defeat the [Lost Paladin](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Paladin "Skyrim:Lost Paladin") and take [Chrysamere](/wiki/Skyrim:Chrysamere_(item) "Skyrim:Chrysamere (item)").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Face the Paladin in battle

**Note: This quest was originally added to your journal upon installing the [Chrysamere](/wiki/Skyrim:Chrysamere "Skyrim:Chrysamere") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), this quest no longer appears in your journal. Nevertheless, the reward can still be obtained by finding the artifact yourself.**

This is a non-journal quest that takes place at [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost"). You will likely need to navigate the entirety of the dungeon in order to reach the quest objective. Alternatively, it is possible to jump up onto the high outcropping to the left of the battlements, and use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to land on the battlements.

When you reach the Forelhost Battlements, you'll find the [Lost Paladin](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Paladin "Skyrim:Lost Paladin") in front of the [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") wielding [Chrysamere](/wiki/Skyrim:Chrysamere_(item) "Skyrim:Chrysamere (item)"). You will be able to take the blade once you kill the ghost. Be advised that you may also have to fight [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir") if you are completing the quest [Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult") at the same time.

### Taking the Shortcut

It isn't necessary to navigate all the way through Forelhost to get to the upper Battlements. In fact, this is not recommended because it can start another side quest entitled Siege on the Dragon Cult which can make the final battle more difficult as noted above. It usually starts by speaking with Captain Valmir, whose campsite can be seen in the courtyard just outside the dungeon's main entrance, but sometimes there are different triggers. If the quest is initiated it may cause the Lost Paladin to fail to appear once on the Battlements, sometimes even if the quest is completed. In order to skip the dungeon entirely, simply begin jumping up the incline next to the Forelhost Battlements before entering the courtyard and you can eventually work your way up to the top, where the ghost will be waiting near the Word Wall.

## Notes

- Prior to the Anniversary Edition update, you would receive this quest upon installing the Chrysamere Creation (or upon exiting [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") on a new character). You would then be directed to Forelhost to face the Lost Paladin.

## Bugs

- Your journal will repeatedly update with the current quest objective each time you enter a new section of Forelhost.
  - This bug is fixed by the Anniversary Edition update. The quest no longer provides any journal entries or quest markers.
- The ghost will sometimes not appear at all.
  - This seems to be due to a conflict of some sort with the Siege on the Dragon Cult quest. If you have not done the quest yet, either do not start it, or reload a save where you have not started it. Avoid Captain Valmir and climb up to the battlements. This may require clever use of jumping/horses/Whirlwind Sprint. The ghost should properly spawn in front of the word wall.
- The Paladin does not have [protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Protected_NPCs "Skyrim:Protected NPCs") status. He may be killed early, and not by you, if a [Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") (especially a higher-level dragon such as [Ancient](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon#Ancient_Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon")) attacks you outside Forelhost and then switches targets. Presumably you have to hurry to the battlements and loot his ghostly remains before the area resets. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The Lost Paladin (ccBGSSSE007\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | I've heard a rumor about the location of the Lost Paladin, the last warrior to wield Chrysamere. *Objective 0:* Find the Lost Paladin  *Objective 1:* Find the Lost Paladin  *Objective 2:* Find the Lost Paladin  *Objective 3:* Find the Lost Paladin  *Objective 4:* Find the Lost Paladin |
| 1000 | ☑ | I fought the ghost of the Lost Paladin and claimed Chrysamere for myself. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE007_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE007_Quest`.
