# Skyrim:The Lover's Requital

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") locate his former [fiancée](/wiki/Skyrim:Svidi "Skyrim:Svidi"), so he can kill her.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail"),  [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn") |
| Reward: | [Sibbi's Stash Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Sibbi.27s_Stash_Key "Skyrim:Keys"), randomly generated loot |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar")) =-1 ([Lynly Star-Sung](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung")) if intimidate her with the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") installed =1 ([Lynly Star-Sung](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung")) if lie to Sibbi about Lynly |
| ID: | FreeformRiften02 |

[Lynly Star-Sung](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung") is secretly in hiding.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") in [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail").
2. Locate [Svidi](/wiki/Skyrim:Svidi "Skyrim:Svidi") and talk to her.
3. Tell Sibbi the truth or lie to him.

### A Murderer in the Jail?

Sibbi is planning to take action!

If you enter the [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail"), you will come across [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") residing in one of the jail cells. You may ask him how he ended up in jail, he will respond with: *"Look, we all have our flaws; mine is that women can't get enough of me. So I had this little affair going on while I was betrothed to a beautiful girl named Svidi. Well, she finds out and she tells her brother, Wulfur. Then her brother attacks me with a knife... I mean, I had to defend myself"*

Now, he is very angry about that girl. *"I'd do anything to have that whore's head on a platter."* All he needs to know is where she is. If you can help him find his fiancee, he promises you'll be well compensated. You may ask him for more information about Svidi. He will respond with: *"She was a young woman... buxom, with long flowing black hair. She used to sing the most lovely songs to me when we were courting. I've never heard a voice so beautiful. All that talent will go to waste when I'm finished with her."*

### A Bard in the Inn?

According to Sibbi's description, you may find such a woman in the [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn") in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). Now, she is a [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard "Skyrim:Bard") under the name of [Lynly Star-Sung](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung"). You may tell her that you know she is Svidi, she will initially deny it. *"No, I'm sorry. You must have me mistaken for someone else. I've never even heard that name before."* You can now choose to persuade or intimidate her with your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skills.

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| You have nothing to fear from me. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Please, I beg you, don't tell Sibbi where I am. He'll kill me! | **Passed**: Return to Sibbi |
| **Failed**: I'm sorry, I don't know what you're talking about. | **Failed**: Nothing |
| Stop lying or I'll beat it out of you! **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Please, I beg you, don't tell Sibbi where I am. He'll kill me! | **Passed**: Return to Sibbi |
| **Failed**: I've been hurt worse before. | **Failed**: Nothing |
| Never mind. My mistake. | I should say so. I'd be careful in the future before you confront someone without all of the facts! | Nothing |

If you are successful she will continue: *"Sibbi's been spreading lies about me, you must hear me out."*

You may ask Svidi to tell you her side of the story, she will reply with: *"Sibbi and I were to be married. We were supposed to be happy together forever. Then I found that wretched poetry from [Svana](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield"). When I confronted Sibbi about it, he threatened to kill me. I was scared so I told my brother Wulfur. He went to talk to Sibbi for me and... and... Sibbi killed him. My brother wasn't even armed! When I heard what Sibbi did, I fled. Now you've found me, and you're going to tell him where I am."*

### A Choice in Your Hand

Return to Sibbi and tell him you have got some information about Svidi. He will be very glad. *"Good, good. Just point me in the right direction and I'll do the rest."* At this point, you will have to make a decision: tell him the truth or lie to him.

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| She's in Ivarstead using the name Lynly. | Ivarstead? So close to Riften? She's an even bigger fool than I thought. |
| She's made her way east into Morrowind. | So, the whore thinks the Black-Briar reach ends at the border of Skyrim, eh? She'll soon discover her mistake. |
| Never mind. I was mistaken. | You idiot. You came all the way down here for that? |

Whichever option you choose between the first two, Svidi will not be killed, and Sibbi will give you his [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Sibbi.27s_Stash_Key "Skyrim:Keys") to a long chest found in the basement (at the bottom of the stairs) of the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery") in Riften, saying *"You've done me a great service, my friend. Allow me to compensate you for the information."* The chest will always contain one random weapon, two poisons, and some gold, along with the [Prowler's Profit](/wiki/Skyrim:Prowler%27s_Profit "Skyrim:Prowler's Profit") gems, if applicable. Sibbi's gratitude will also allow you to take any low-value items from the meadery.

## Notes

- Sibbi's chest is non-respawning, so its contents will be determined on your first visit to the meadery and won't change after that.
- Lynly Star-Sung remains alive all the time even if you tell Sibbi the truth.

## Bugs

- Despite the fact that Sibbi says that Lynly Star-Sung has dark hair, her hair is blonde instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, addresses this issue. Lynly now has black hair to comply with Sibbi's description.
- Killing Lynly will fail the quest, despite Sibbi having dialogue afterwards for when you do. This is caused by the `defaultsetstagealias` script attached to her alias.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.
- The game incorrectly runs the speechcraft check against Lynly herself rather than you, making it impossible to pass without the [Amulet of Articulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Articulation#Amulet_of_Articulation "Skyrim:Amulet of Articulation").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you intimidate Lynly, she does not appropriately harbor bitterness towards you due to the relationship values not being adjusted.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes when you go to talk to Sibbi after speaking with Lynly, you can't engage in conversation through the bars, even though there is a pointer over his head and he is up close. You might need to pick the lock and go into his cell. **?**

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften02`.

# Skyrim:The Lover Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Lover Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Lover+Stone)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DoomstoneReach01 | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")  North of [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine") | |

The Lover Stone

**The Lover Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim").

It is situated to the east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), and just north of [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine"). Approach from the west, as the east side is a cliff.

It makes all [skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") improve 15% faster. If you have The Lover Stone active, you cannot gain [resting bonuses](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping "Skyrim:Sleeping") in the original version of the game. This makes it a useful choice for users with [lycanthropy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"), since [werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") cannot gain any benefit from sleeping to begin with.

## The Lover Stone

.jpg)

The Lover Stone, when activated

There is a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") nearby that you will encounter as you approach the stone and several [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") trees in the area. It overlooks the road that passes [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine") on the edge of a cliff face next to a stream that tumbles as a waterfall to join the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") below. Either side of the stone are several upright stones in a semi-circle.

## Notes

- The [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown")([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")) makes it possible to obtain both resting bonuses and the combined benefits of [The Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones") with this one.
  - If you combine the Aetherial Crown with The Guardian Stones and this one, you'll benefit with the blessing of this Stone and the blessing of the Guardian Stone you combine it with. You'll only be able to maximize the benefits of one of the Guardian Stones, though.

# Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") |
| Location(s): | [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave"), [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair")) =1 ([Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard")) |
| ID: | MS06Start |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened"), [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened"), [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute") | | |

Welcome to [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Varnius Junius](/wiki/Skyrim:Varnius_Junius "Skyrim:Varnius Junius") or [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") or [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") or [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
2. Travel to [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
3. Stop the ritual to summon [Potema](/wiki/Lore:Potema "Lore:Potema").
4. Return to Falk Firebeard.

### The Messenger

In [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), the [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpulus_Vinius "Skyrim:Corpulus Vinius") and residing [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisette "Skyrim:Lisette") at the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") will all tell you about a scared [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") resident who recently arrived to ask [Jarl Elisif](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") for help. They will not reveal anything else, so head to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), where you will witness [Varnius Junius](/wiki/Skyrim:Varnius_Junius "Skyrim:Varnius Junius") trying to convince Elisif that the inexplicable disappearances and strange occurrences near [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") should be taken seriously. While Elisif tries her best to calm the near hysterical Varnius, her [court wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") and [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") will both disregard the claims:

"*Haafingar's people will always be safe under my rule.*"

**Varnius**: *"I swear to you, unnatural magics are coming from that cave! There are strange noises and lights! We need someone to investigate!"*
**Elisif**: *"Then we will immediately send out a legion to scour the cave and secure the town. Haafingar's people will always be safe under my rule."*
**Varnius**: *"Th...thank you, my Jarl thank you."*
**Sybille**: *"Your eminence, my scrying has suggested nothing in the area. Dragon Bridge is under imperial control. This is likely superstitious nonsense."*
**Falk**: *"Perhaps a more... tempered reaction... might be called for?"*
**Elisif**: *"Oh. Yes, of course you are right. Falk, tell [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") I said to assign a few extra soldiers to Dragon Bridge."*
**Varnius**: *"Thank you, Jarl Elisif. But about the cave..."*
**Falk**: *"I will have someone take care of the cave as well Varnius, you can rest easy. You're dismissed."*

After the court has acknowledged his claims, Varnius Junius will be relieved and leave the castle, unaware that nobody plans on doing anything to solve his problem. Speak to Varnius Junius or Elisif the Fair or Sybille Stentor, either will lead you to Falk Firebeard, who will admit he thinks Varnius is overreacting and that he has his hands full dealing with the recent murder of [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"), the grieving Elisif, and the ongoing war. Offer to take a look at Wolfskull Cave for him, and he will gladly accept.

### Wolfskull Cave

Wolfskull Cave is located due west of Solitude and north of the [Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia"). As you arrive, two [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") will guard the entrance, hinting at darker things to come. Enter the cave and proceed through the first chamber. Before long, you will be attacked by hordes of leveled [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"), all keen on protecting their secret. As you progress, leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and more skeletons will attack. In the third chamber, you will arrive at a pit, and will have no choice but jump in. Take the northern tunnel and enter [Wolfskull Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Ruins "Skyrim:Wolfskull Ruins").

*"We summon Potema!"*

As you enter, it quickly becomes clear that something is very wrong in the cave; blue beams of light spear across the room and chanting voices can be heard:

**[Ritual Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Ritual_Master "Skyrim:Ritual Master")**: *"Wolf Queen. Hear our call and awaken. We summon Potema!"*
**Necromancers**: *"We summon Potema!"*
**Ritual Master**: *"Long have you slept the dreamless sleep of death, Potema. No longer. Hear us Wolf Queen! We Summon You!"*
**Necromancers**: *"We summon Potema!"*

Take a look from the ledge and you'll notice that the blue lights all lead to the same platform, high above ground level. Backtrack a bit and locate the tunnel leading west. The chamber ahead is covered in [oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"), so use it to your advantage against the patrolling necromancer.

### The Wolf Queen

Back in the main chamber, there are stairs leading further down and enemies will attack. Fight your way to ground level and enter the ruin where a set of stairs will lead back up. As you make your way upstairs, it becomes apparent that the necromancer's ritual is about to go wrong, as [Potema](/wiki/Lore:Potema "Lore:Potema") will shout:

*"Summoned with words. Bound by blood."*

Potema's escape

**Potema**: *"Yes! Yes! Return me to this realm!"*
**Ritual Master**: *"As our voices summon you the blood of the innocent binds you Wolf Queen!"*
**Necromancers**: *"Summoned with words. Bound by blood."*
**Potema**: *"What! What are you doing?! You fools! You cannot bind me to your wills!"*
**Necromancers**: *"Summoned with words. Bound by blood."*
**Potema**: *"You ants don't have the power to bind me!"*

Keep going up one set of stairs after another, fighting the opposition on your way. As your reach the source of the blue light, the ritual master will speak once again: *"Something is wrong. There is an intruder."* As you climb the tower, an additional four necromancers will attack. At the top, you will find the ritual master busy performing the ritual to revive Potema. There is only one way to stop her. When she is dead, the blue light will disappear through a hole in the ceiling and everything will be quiet. Read the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[The Refugees](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Refugees "Skyrim:The Refugees")* from the altar, then activate the lever to lower the drawbridge. Loot the chest on the other side and follow the path, a shortcut back to the first chamber of Wolfskull Cave.

### Falk Firebeard

Back in the Blue Palace, busy castle steward Falk Firebeard will be curious to know whether you found anything other than [wild animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") in Wolfskull Cave. When you tell him that necromancers tried to resurrect [Potema](/wiki/Lore:Potema "Lore:Potema"), he will be shocked and will ask if you stopped them. At this point, you will have no choice but to tell him you interrupted the ritual and that it is done. He will then explain that you have done Solitude a larger service than you can imagine and reward you with a leveled amount of gold. However, Potema is far from defeated. After you level up at least once and wait a few days, a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") delivers a very concerned [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Letter from Falk Firebeard") from Falk Firebeard, beginning the quest [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened").

## Notes

- Attacking the summoning circle will draw all enemies to you, even ones you missed at the base of the tower.
- Killing the Ritual Master will unbind the Draugr and cause them to attack the Necromancers.
- This quest is also a prerequisite for [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute"), which is required before Elisif will allow you to start the [thane quest for Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar").
- The opening conversation between Varnius and Elisif will not change even if not witnessed until after the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have taken Solitude. Elisif will still mention Captain Aldis, who would have already disappeared from the game, and Sybille Stentor will still claim that Dragon Bridge is under Imperial control.
- This quest changes the contents of [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") while it is active. This makes it impossible to clear Wolfskull Cave, and can also cause conflicts with any radiant quests that happen to send you to the cave, making it impossible to complete those quests. Therefore it is best to complete this quest as quickly as possible after triggering it.

## Bugs

- Falk Firebeard always carries a copy of the [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Letter from Falk Firebeard") which the [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") later gives you in order to begin [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened"). It is possible to [pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") this letter before you even talk to Falk about Wolfskull Cave.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- The quest may at times fail to advance to stage 15 when you enter the court, resulting in [Varnius Junius](/wiki/Skyrim:Varnius_Junius "Skyrim:Varnius Junius") and the rest of the court standing without interacting with each other, and when spoken to, will simply tell you not to interrupt the court. This seems to occur if any of the courtiers leave the Blue Palace before Varnius' audience begins. Jarl Elisif will leave the Blue Palace to take part in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames"), [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude"), [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") and [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), and Erikur will also leave the palace for the latter two, so it is advisable to visit the Blue Palace before beginning any of these quests.
  -  You can use the console command `setstage MS06Start 5` to force Varnius' audience to play out and start the quest.
  -  Or `setstage MS06Start 15` to skip just past his audience and also start the quest.
  - Killing [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") (the only courtier present who is not essential) also seems to remedy this.
- Sometimes the marker for miscellaneous quest "Head to the Solitude Court" isn't removed when you talk with Falk Firebeard or complete "The Man Who Cried Wolf".
  -  You can use the console command `setstage MS06Start 10` to deactivate the marker from miscellaneous quest.

## Quest Stages

| The Man Who Cried Wolf (MS06Start) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 15 |  | A representative from Dragon Bridge has appealed to the court in Solitude for help investigating Wolfskull Cave. Falk Firebeard is looking for someone to look into the issue. |
| 50 |  | A representative from Dragon Bridge has appealed to the court in Solitude for help investigating Wolfskull Cave. Falk Firebeard has asked me to clear out the cave. *Objective 50:* Clear Out Wolfskull Cave |
| 100 |  | I have confronted and stopped a group of necromancers attempting to summon Potema, the Wolf Queen, in Wolfskull Cave. I should return to Falk Firebeard with the news. *Objective 100:* Speak to Falk Firebeard |
| 250 | ☑ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 15:* Ask Falk Firebeard about Wolfskull Cave |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 10, 60, 65, 70, 75, 80, 83, 85, 90, 105, 110, 115.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS06Start stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS06Start`.

# Skyrim:The Midden

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Guild: The Midden ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Midden)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Range: 6-30 |
| Occupants | |
| [Ice Wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [Frostbite Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [Skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [Velehk Sain](/wiki/Skyrim:Velehk_Sain "Skyrim:Velehk Sain") [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") | |

| *[De Rerum Dirennis](/wiki/Skyrim:De_Rerum_Dirennis "Skyrim:De Rerum Dirennis")* | |

| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | |
| Location | |
| [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |

The Midden is located within the depths of the College of Winterhold

**The Midden** is a medium-sized dungeon underneath the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") containing the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") and home to the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain"), a former mage of the college.

There are three entrances: a trapdoor in the northern corner of the College courtyard, another trapdoor at the base of the stairwell in the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"), and through an easy-to-miss cave in the northern face of the rocky outcropping that the College rests upon, being the only way to access the Midden without joining the College. The dungeon contains two sections: *[The Midden](#The_Midden)* and *[The Midden Dark](#The_Midden_Dark)*.

The corridors and rooms are littered with the bones of humans and animals, as well as various containers and plenty of other detritus and clutter. A careful search yields many items that can be used at the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge"), including [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), [torchbug thoraxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax"), [rubies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), brooms, and skulls.

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain")** | |

## Related Quests

- **[Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell")**: Find a [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone") by summoning a daedra and learn more about [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration").
- **[Forgotten Names](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Names "Skyrim:Forgotten Names")**: Summon the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") pirate, [Velehk Sain](/wiki/Skyrim:Velehk_Sain "Skyrim:Velehk Sain").
- **[Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions")**: Find and consult the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").
- **[Illusion Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell")**: Find some books about [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") magic to further your Illusion skills.
- **[Restoration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell")**: Find the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") and learn more about [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic.

### The Midden

Entering the Midden from the courtyard leads into an icy corridor heading northeast. On the left beside a pile of firewood is a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). Opposite these against the other wall is a basket containing a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). Ahead, the corridor opens into a room with a walkway around two sides and a level below with a flight of stairs leading down. The hanging skeleton with the deer head has two rubies for eyes, which can be retrieved using [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") or by disturbing the skeleton and causing it to fall (which risks the rubies falling to random locations). Above, on a shelf just below the ceiling, is a basket containing four [refined moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Moonstone "Skyrim:Refined Moonstone"). On your right are barred openings looking into another room with water falling ahead. On the left the walkway continues past another corridor heading northwest. In the northern corner, on a wooden block, is a cast iron pot containing a [potion of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), and in front of the pot is a patch of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus.

The northwest corridor passes two small alcoves opposite each other. The alcove on the right contains two more patches of white cap, and has a strange idol fashioned from bones and deer antlers. Behind it, on the left, there is a piece of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), with another underneath the basket, buried in the floor. The alcove on the left has a crate with a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") on top, while farther along on the left is another patch of white cap. The corridor ends at a wooden door leading to the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance").

Returning to the two-level room and descending the stairs, the floor below is partially covered in old rugs. There is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") at the bottom of the stairs. There is another barred opening, as well as one that is unbarred. In the room beyond, you can hear an undead creature moving around. A corridor heads northeast from the two-level room. Ahead is a fork in the passageway, with a patch of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") in the middle, an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") leaking from a drain on the right, and a skeleton on the floor. By its outstretched hand is a random enchanted [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). To the right, a short passage leads to an open cell with a bedroll inside, with blood splattered all over the floor and walls, and a chair sitting outside the cell. To the left, the passage ends at the top of a flight of stairs, with an [ice wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") lurking at the bottom. This room has a high vaulted ceiling, with many arches supporting it. The passage continues beyond the arches to the northeast, and after a short distance, turns to the southeast next to a magical light source that lights up as you approach.

Ahead, the passage descends another flight of stairs and then opens into a circular chamber in front of the Atronach Forge, with a passage heading southwest. To the left of the forge is a wardrobe with a small square wooden table in front. On the table is the *[Atronach Forge Manual](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Manual "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Manual")*, two bowls of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), and a ruby. Beside the table is a broom. The forge itself is a raised circular stone with the [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion") daedric symbol carved in the center, a pedestal, an offering box, and a handle on the near side. The passage to the southwest curves around to the south and ends at a closed gate. There is a chamber beyond the gate with [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing down the wall. Against the east wall next to some crates is a bucket containing a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") and two torchbug thoraxes, while against the south wall is a slightly raised section with a patch of white cap and a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") growing on top. There is a ledge on the wall above, holding a salt pile and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), above which is a deer skull fixed to the wall. There is a leather strip and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") on the floor against the north wall, while the passage heads west into the room seen through the barred openings. There is a cart with empty wine bottles in and around it, while to the left a flight of stairs leads up to a walkway that ends under two arches where a leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") archer stands. There is a wooden door to the west on the bottom level, behind which is an L-shaped passage that ends at another door leading to *The Midden Dark*.

### The Midden Dark

Skeletal design at the entrance of the Midden Dark

Beyond the door, a passage heads east for a few paces and then turns north. At the corner is a skeletal design with some [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing to the right. To the north is a large ice chamber, with a natural bridge crossing a lower level below. The chamber is guarded by an ice wraith. Below you on a rock to the left is an unlocked wooden chest. Across the bridge, an ice tunnel enters another chamber, with stairs up on the right and a passage heading northwest. The passage leads to a flight of stairs descending to another chamber, with a wooden door that is locked and indicates it requires a key (however, there is no actual key for the door, which is scripted to open in the course of quests). Beyond is the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain"), whom you can access during the quest [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions"), and again when you come to complete the [Restoration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell").

Returning to the previous chamber, climbing the stairs on the right leads to a passage heading north, before descending another flight of stairs. At the bottom is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") ahead, with a salt pile and a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[De Rerum Dirennis](/wiki/Skyrim:De_Rerum_Dirennis "Skyrim:De Rerum Dirennis")*. To the left is a patch of white cap, and to the right stairs descend into a room containing another white cap and two hostile [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") in a lower level filled with human bones.

To the southeast is a wooden door. Behind the door is a circular ritual chamber with a large black metal gauntlet on a pedestal, central to the quest [Forgotten Names](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Names "Skyrim:Forgotten Names"). The symbol of Oblivion is emblazoned on the palm of the gauntlet. A long wooden table opposite holds the *[Midden Incident Report](/wiki/Skyrim:Midden_Incident_Report "Skyrim:Midden Incident Report")* and the [Investigator's Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Investigator%27s_Key "Skyrim:Investigator's Key"). An alcove to the right features a kettle containing two pieces of [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), and a sample of [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"). Beside this is a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), and on a crate behind is an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"). Opposite the alcove against the wall is a bucket containing a [silver sapphire necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Sapphire_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Sapphire Necklace"). There are several hanging moss growing from the walls, and a ring of [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") high up on ledges around the room.

To the southeast, a corridor leads to the top of more stairs with a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a bloodied [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a salt pile, a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a bulb of garlic, and a loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") all on a cart wheel. At the bottom of the stairs is another passage, which is eventually blocked by thick cobwebs you will have to burn or chop your way through. Ahead in another heavily vaulted section are two leveled [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). Around the area you can find several more white cap fungi, a lootable skeleton, an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"). The passage exits the area heading west, passing into the ice chamber's lower level beneath the bridge, and then outside to the shore beneath the College.

Once through the exit, the player can either reenter the dungeon, or jump down a small cliff to an outdoor cave below. The cave exits near the shoreline underneath the College. It is possible to reenter the Midden Dark through this entrance through a combination of careful jumping and persistence. This is useful for characters wishing to access this area and the Atronach Forge without having to enroll with the College.

## Notes

- The three undead required for the quest [J'zargo's Experiment](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo%27s_Experiment "Skyrim:J'zargo's Experiment") can conveniently be found here (one in the Midden, two in the Midden Dark), provided the quest has been obtained before clearing the dungeon.
- During the [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest, [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") will give you the spell [Summon Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Summon Unbound Dremora") and tell you to go get a [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone"). This is the missing spherical object needed for the most powerful objects the forge can produce.
- Entering the Midden Dark via the cave will also (inexplicably) teleport your most recent horse to town.
- The Midden also [appears](/wiki/Legends:The_Midden "Legends:The Midden") in [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends"), in the [Return to Clockwork City](/wiki/Legends:Return_to_Clockwork_City "Legends:Return to Clockwork City") storyline.

## Bugs

- When in the Midden, the door to the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance") is a wooden door through a wall. But when in the Hall of Countenance, the door to the Midden is a trapdoor under the stairs.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=5438)) The door in the Midden has been replaced with a ladder and trapdoor.
- It is apparently sometimes possible for NPCs to come out the Midden exit at the bottom of the main College spire, and when they do, they become trapped there because there is no ground path back into the area.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.6, addresses this issue. Several navmeshes outside the area have now been adjusted to provide a walking path back up to the College. It's a somewhat roundabout path back, but it'll have to do.

# Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman

## Overview

The Mind of a Madman

**The Mind of a Madman** is the mind of [Pelagius the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Mad "Skyrim:Pelagius the Mad"). It is Pelagius' mind in physical form. It is accessible only through the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing") of the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), and only when the quest [The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness") has begun.

The first area you see after you have been transported contains a long dining table filled with food. On one side, [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath") sits on a throne, and on the other side, [Pelagius the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Mad "Skyrim:Pelagius the Mad") sits in a chair.

The area to the right, known as Pelagius' Confidence, contains nothing except two ghostly figures fighting, [Confidence](/wiki/Skyrim:Confidence_(NPC) "Skyrim:Confidence (NPC)") and [Anger](/wiki/Skyrim:Anger "Skyrim:Anger"). The area straight ahead, known as Pelagius' Night Terrors, contains a bed where [Pelagius the Tormented](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Tormented "Skyrim:Pelagius the Tormented") is sleeping. The area to the left, known as Pelagius' Paranoia, contains an arena where two atronachs are fighting. On both sides of the arena are two stone chairs. The chairs on the opposite side are each occupied by a [Bodyguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodyguard_(Pelagius) "Skyrim:Bodyguard (Pelagius)"), while [Pelagius the Suspicious](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Suspicious "Skyrim:Pelagius the Suspicious") stands between them.

## NPCs Present

| Name |
| --- |
| [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath") |

## Related Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

## Notes

- As the area is a separate worldspace, it is possible to fast travel away after using the quest journal to access the map. However, if you do so, you will be unable to access the skill tree and magic inventory. While it is still possible to equip items through containers, you will lose all items, including quest items, that you were carrying when you entered. Thus, you should not fast travel from this area.
- When you complete the Path of Dreams segment, a chest with a "Search" prompt will appear, though activating it will do nothing.
- None of the items here are owned, thus making them free to take.

## Bugs

- Dragons may appear and possibly kill you, as they cannot land, and you cannot attack them.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:The Mind of Madness

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Daedric.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Daedric.png) | **Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Dervenin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dervenin "Skyrim:Dervenin") |
| Location(s): | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing") of the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), [The Mind of a Madman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman") |
| Reward: | [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack"), set of [Fine Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") |
| ID: | DA15 |

Sheogorath tries to cheer up Pelagius the Mad over a feast

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Investigate a man called [Dervenin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dervenin "Skyrim:Dervenin").
2. Gain access to the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing") of the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").
3. Search for [Dervenin's master](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath") in the Pelagius Wing.
4. Complete the First Trial.
5. Complete the Second Trial.
6. Complete the Third Trial.
7. Escape from [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

### Solitude

*"You'll help me! You help people, right? That's what you do?"*

In [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), you may hear a rumor from innkeepers that a mad beggar is wandering around the streets of the city, distressed over the absence of his master, saying things like: *"Please, take pity on an old madman!"* and *"You! You'll help me! You help people, right? That's what you do?"*

The beggar, named [Dervenin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dervenin "Skyrim:Dervenin"), will plead you to find his master: *"My master has abandoned me! Abandoned his people. And nothing I say can change his mind. Now he refuses to even see me. He says I interrupt his vacation! It's been so many years... Won't you please help?"* He will tell you that his master was "visiting a friend in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")" and further detail that his master "went into the [forbidden wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing") of the palace, to speak with an old friend". He will give you [Pelagius' Hip Bone](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius%27_Hip_Bone "Skyrim:Pelagius' Hip Bone"), required to enter the forbidden wing. You also need to retrieve the key to the wing, either from one of the [cleaning](/wiki/Skyrim:Erdi "Skyrim:Erdi") [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Una "Skyrim:Una") or from [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard"), the steward.

### Blue Palace

Enter the Blue Palace and locate one of the cleaning staff. The key can be obtained from [Erdi](/wiki/Skyrim:Erdi "Skyrim:Erdi") or [Una](/wiki/Skyrim:Una "Skyrim:Una") by discussing the Pelagius Wing with her and telling her that Falk asked you to "look into it". You must pass an easy level, invisible [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade her to give you the key. Alternatively, you can convince [the castle steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") to let you in if you have completed the quest [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf").

If you lack the respective requirement, the final dialogue option will not appear; the NPC will simply exit dialogue.

| Option | Falk Firebeard | Una | Erdi |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I need to get into the Pelagius Wing. | Absolutely not. That wing has been sealed for hundreds of years, and for good reason. They say the ghost of Pelagius the Mad still haunts it. Ghost or not, there are reminders of his dark rule that are best left buried away. | Not on your life. It's dangerous in there, and Falk doesn't even like me and Erdi going in every year to clean out the spiders. | Oh, I'd get in trouble for that. It's not allowed. Besides, it's scary in there! |
| Falk, you know I'll be careful. (**Falk Firebeard**) Falk asked me to check it out. (**Una and Erdi**) | I'll make an exception for you, but do not bring anything out when you leave. Too many dark deeds transpired in those halls... | If you really want to... Just be careful of the ghost! He snuck up on me once and scared me sick. It took a week for me to feel better... | Well... I suppose in that case, it's okay to let you in. But only briefly. Be careful, and come right back! |

Exploring briefly in the wing will show it in a state of disrepair. Further travel will require you to walk through some spider webs before you suddenly find yourself transported into a [strange realm](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman").

### Pelagius' Mind

"It's all you've got."

You will find yourself suddenly wearing a full set of Fine Clothes with your inventory inaccessible and your abilities removed. The scene before you appears to be an extravagant dinner set in the middle of a misty wood and surrounded by stone archways. Two people are sitting at the table, one wearing a distinctive outfit and sitting on a throne, and the other a depressed man. The latter is [Pelagius III](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Mad "Skyrim:Pelagius the Mad") who is complaining of various woes, although he sounds strangely sane, which delights the man across from him. Pelagius will leave after a short conversation during which the other man tries to cheer him up.

Upon further investigation, it then transpires that the other individual is none other than [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath") himself. Tell him that you have a message for him and that he needs to come back from vacation. Sheogorath says he will leave if you can make your way out of Pelagius' mind. He will give you the [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") to help you. There are three arches which lead to three separate trials, all of which must be completed. To the southeast is the Arch of Confidence, to the northeast is the Arch of Night Terrors and to the northwest is the Arch of Paranoia. These trials can be completed in any order.

### Pelagius' Confidence

Pelagius' Anger beating up Pelagius' Confidence

In this scene you will see Pelagius' [Anger](/wiki/Skyrim:Anger "Skyrim:Anger") beating up Pelagius' [Confidence](/wiki/Skyrim:Confidence_(NPC) "Skyrim:Confidence (NPC)"). Confidence doesn't look like he is doing too well, since he is tiny and Anger is huge. Sheogorath wants you to tip the scales. Use the Wabbajack on Anger (casting twice) until he is tiny, and then on Confidence (again casting twice) until he is as big as Anger was. You must act quickly, as Confidence will shrink every time Anger hits him. During the battle, two spectral figures labeled [Self Doubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Self_Doubt "Skyrim:Self Doubt") will appear and begin to spar with each other. They do not seem to serve any purpose other than to get in your way as you attempt to complete the trial.

### Pelagius' Night Terrors

Pelagius with his converted night terrors in the background

You will see a bed in the middle of the forest with Pelagius sleeping on it. Sheogorath tells you that Pelagius has been suffering from night terrors since he was a child, and you are tasked with getting rid of them. Use the Wabbajack on [Pelagius the Tormented](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Tormented "Skyrim:Pelagius the Tormented") to start the sequence, and then use it on each terror in turn as they arrive. After a successful attack with the Wabbajack each will turn into something more innocuous. Do not attack the innocuous creatures; instead, use the Wabbajack on Pelagius again to call the next terror. Repeat this process of zapping Pelagius and then the creatures that appear until he wakes up. Don't take too long in zapping the creatures after they appear, or you will have to start over. In order, the creatures or enemies that appear are:

1. A [wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") will appear (to be turned rather humiliatingly into a goat).
2. A [bandit chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") will then appear, to be turned into a younger version of Pelagius.
3. A [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") will appear. After use of the Wabbajack, it will be turned into one of Pelagius' [sultry maidens](/wiki/Skyrim:Sultry_Maiden "Skyrim:Sultry Maiden"), from his early days.
4. A [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") will appear. It turns into a bonfire after use of the staff.
5. A [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") will appear, to be turned into an inaccessible chest behind the bonfire. (The Dragon Priest may summon an atronach as well, but Wabbajack has no effect on it, so you should ignore it.)

After all of the terrors have been converted, everyone will convene around the bonfire, and Sheogorath will communicate with you and ask you to progress to the next area.

### Pelagius' Paranoia

Pelagius' Paranoia

Through the Arch of Paranoia to the northwest is a small fort-like structure with steps leading up to the edge. In the middle of this structure there is an arena occupied by two fighting Storm Atronachs. Supposedly, one is yours and one is your [opponent's](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Suspicious "Skyrim:Pelagius the Suspicious"), who is sitting opposite you with two other men. You are instructed to use Wabbajack to defeat your enemy. Don't bother zapping the atronachs themselves, as one will respond to the changes the other goes through, making the fight endless. Instead, aim for one of the two [bodyguards](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodyguard_(Pelagius) "Skyrim:Bodyguard (Pelagius)") sitting next to your opponent and Wabbajack them. Both of the men will turn into wolves and attack your opponent, killing him.

### Your Reward

Go back to Sheogorath when you've finished his tasks and tell him you've fixed Pelagius' mind. He will summon Dervenin and return to the [Shivering Isles](/wiki/Lore:Shivering_Isles "Lore:Shivering Isles"), telling you to keep Wabbajack. He mentions his chamberlain, [Haskill](/wiki/Lore:Haskill "Lore:Haskill"), as he prepares to depart, saying, *"Well, I suppose it's back to the Shivering Isles. The trouble Haskill can get into while I'm gone simply boggles the mind..."* You will then be transported back to the Pelagius Wing with all the items and powers you had when you started, as well as your new staff and clothes. Before leaving, move further down the hall and down the stairs to find a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Surfeit of Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Surfeit_of_Thieves "Skyrim:Surfeit of Thieves").*

## Notes

- This quest contains several references to events in [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion") and the [Shivering Isles expansion.](/wiki/Shivering:Shivering_Isles "Shivering:Shivering Isles") See [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scrolls_Historical_References#Oblivion "Skyrim:Elder Scrolls Historical References") for more information.
- The Items, Magic, Map, and Skills keys are disabled during the quest, but the Map can be opened by first going to Quest, then pressing M to show on map, then pressing L to show local. Consequently, it is also impossible to open the chest in the Night Terrors scene. The Favorites menu and hotkeys are also disabled.
  - If you open the menu using the method above (or by pressing X on a highlighted quest, if playing on Xbox 360, or by pressing Square on a highlighted quest, if playing on PS3) you can fast travel out of Pelagius's mind. However, you will be unable to open menus, favorites, or change equipment. You will still be wearing the same outfit as in Pelagius's mind and be holding the Wabbajack.
  - It is also possible to access your inventory while in Pelagius' mind; at the Night Terrors scene after the wolf is turned into a goat, other terrors can kill it. Its body can be "looted", rendering you able to take off your current equipment.
  - If you open your map via your journal, you will be placed north of [Bleakwind Basin](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Basin "Skyrim:Bleakwind Basin").
- During the quest, your Wabbajack will have infinite charges.
- The items on Sheogorath's dining table are unowned, and therefore, free to take.
- Once the quest is complete, the Wabbajack and fine clothes set will remain equipped. Therefore, you'll have to re-equip your weapons and armor manually.
- You cannot pickpocket Sheogorath or Pelagius the Mad, but you can pickpocket Pelagius' Confidence (once Pelagius' Anger is defeated) and Dervenin (once he is summoned).
- When Sheogorath sends Dervenin back to the Shivering Isles, Dervenin's beard remains intact. This doesn't make sense, as beards were banned there.
- The enemies meant to attack Pelagius in the Night Terrors section may attack you, instead.
- Right before you enter Pelagius' mind, you may appear naked for a brief moment.
- Anything you pick up while in Pelagius' mind will transfer with you to the real world once the quest is complete.
- Punching or pickpocketing Dervenin after he is summoned by Sheogorath constitutes a crime and will net you a bounty in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").
- This quest can be done as early as level 1. If your Speech skill is too low to convince the maids to let you into the Pelagius Wing, you can increase the skill with [Fortify Persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Persuasion "Skyrim:Fortify Persuasion") effects. You can get [The Gift of Charity](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gift_of_Charity "Skyrim:The Gift of Charity") bonus from Dervenin by giving him 1 gold before asking him about anything else, and you can get the [Blessing of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Blessing of Dibella") from the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in Solitude. If both are done, your Speech skill will temporarily be at least 35, and that will be enough to convince the maids to let you into the Pelagius Wing.

## Bugs

- The Wabbajack may not auto-equip itself on you once Sheogorath gives you it.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Pelagius's Mind is technically an outdoor area and can spawn dragons.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Exiting the Pelagius Wing during and after the quest can cause the game to crash on PS5 and Xbox Series X.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.342, fixes this bug.
- If you enter Pelagius's Mind while you have the [Stray Dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Stray_Dog "Skyrim:Stray Dog") in your company, the dog won't be in the Wing when you return—other followers such as [Lydia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lydia "Skyrim:Lydia") (human) or [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") (dog) are unaffected.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The game may freeze on transition into Pelagius's Mind. This is probably just a "normal" transition freeze, but it may be caused by the quest-specific behavior that occurs at this point, and may not allow you to continue with the game. It is possible the freeze is caused by having more than 999 items of one kind - likely to be one or more types of arrows - in which case the freeze can be avoided by dumping enough of the offending item(s) to reduce the count to 999 or less, before reaching the transition point to Pelagius's Mind.
- When you complete all the tasks for Sheogorath, he will bid you farewell but you will not actually leave Pelagius' mind.
  - You must exit the dialogue with Sheogorath to trigger a scene that will lead to your leaving.
  - Loading from an earlier save usually fixes this.
- You can regain access to the normal menu by pickpocketing Confidence, read a Black Book, exiting the pickpocket menu, then access the quick menu (Down button in PS4), selecting an item and then exiting. You will then be able to access your inventory permanently.
- If you have a [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") active when you enter Pelagius' Mind, the thrall may be missing when you return. If this happens, check your active effects, and if the thrall is still assigned to you, fast travel may return it to your location. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The Mind of Madness (DA15) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Dervenin wants me to talk to his master about returning from vacation. To do so, I need to gain entrance to the Pelagius Wing of the Blue palace. *Objective 10:* Gain access to the Pelagius Wing of the Blue Palace |
| 45 |  | *Objective 45:* Use the key to gain access to the Pelagius Wing |
| 50 |  | Dervenin wants me to talk to his master about returning from vacation. His master should be somewhere in the Pelagius Wing of the Blue Palace. *Objective 50:* Search for Dervenin's master in the Pelagius Wing |
| 100 |  | Dervenin wants his master Sheogorath to return from vacation. I have tracked Sheogorath and been transported by him in to Pelagius's mind. If I can find a way to home Sheogorath has promised to return home as well. *Objective 100:* Use the Wabbajack to escape from Pelagius's Mind |
| 200 | ☑ | I have helped Dervenin by convincing his master Sheogorath to return from vacation inside the mind of Pelagius. Sheogorath has rewarded me with the Wabbajack for my troubles. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 150:* Escape from the Blue Palace |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 20, 30, 40, 55, 90, 95, 150, 190.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA15 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA15`.

# Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle

## Overview

The Mortar and Pestle

**The Mortar and Pestle** is the alchemy shop in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), between [Brina's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina%27s_House "Skyrim:Brina's House") and [Beitild's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Beitild's House").

It is run by the elderly [Frida](/wiki/Skyrim:Frida "Skyrim:Frida") who also lives above the main trading room.

It contains only one zone, *[The Mortar and Pestle](#Walkthrough)*.

**NOTE**: Like all other stores, The Mortar and Pestle has a number of fixed wares on display scattered around the main trading room. These can be bought from the proprietor Frida and will disappear from the room when purchased. For a list of these special items, see [this section](#Displayed_Merchandise).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Frida](/wiki/Skyrim:Frida "Skyrim:Frida") [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary") |

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

The main trading room is dimly lit and Frida can be found behind the counter every day between 8am and 8pm. Without the displayed merchandise, a lot of beverages reveal themselves. On the shelves of a non-respawning cupboard behind the counter are three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and four bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") along with seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). Atop the counter are three bottles of alto wine and two bottles of wine. Underneath the counter are four additional bottles of wine, a single bottle of alto wine, and a [potion of resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Shock"). There is also a small hidden [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two non-respawning sacks with food, and a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")*. Above the shop counter are two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), some [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), and two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), as well as three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Along the wall next to the cupboard sits a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), a non-respawning chest, and a respawning meat barrel. Underneath the stairs leading to the second floor is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a respawning food barrel.

Frida sleeps in her owned bed on the second floor, where even more beverages sit on some shelves next to a respawning food barrel in the northeastern corner: six bottles of wine and two bottles of alto wine. A dinner table is set with two wedges of [goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") and one [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), with two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on the side. There is also a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and two bottles of alto wine. A non-respawning dresser in the corner holds clothes and on its top sit a few spare ingredients: one [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), one [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), one [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), and one sample each of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm") and [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"). On the other side of the bed are five gold coins on a table and a non-respawning unlocked chest.

## Displayed Merchandise

- The following items are sitting out in the store on counters, shelves, or tables. They can be purchased or taken for free if your [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") with Frida is high enough. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Ingredients**: 3 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), 1 [Ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), 2 [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), 2 [Giant Lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), 1 [Glow Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), 1 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), 3 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), 3 [Spider Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), 1 [Spriggan Sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), 3 [Swamp Fungal Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), 1 [Taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), 2 [Thistle Branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), 2 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), 2 [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), 1 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") - This is the merchandise found in the store's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

## Notes

- The front door has an adept lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:Key to The Mortar and Pestle") to which is carried by Frida.

## Bugs

- The store may be locked during normal business hours and open in the middle of the night when merchant services are unavailable.
  - Successful workarounds may be to gain access to 2nd floor door and wait 24 hours while inside during normal business hours. then go downstairs and attempt to make a purchase

# Skyrim:The North Wind

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Ship: The North Wind ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+North+Wind)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WindhelmDocksExterior01 | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | |

The North Wind

**The North Wind** is a ship docked at the [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") docks.

## People

| Crew Members |
| --- |
| [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") (Captain)  [Dalan Merchad](/wiki/Skyrim:Dalan_Merchad "Skyrim:Dalan Merchad")  [Voldsea Giryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Voldsea_Giryon "Skyrim:Voldsea Giryon") |

## Related Quests

- **[Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master")**: Take care of a runaway crew member. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## The North Wind

Fishing supplies

The vessel has several crates and unusable barrels on deck, along with a couple of chairs. You will find both the captain, [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar"), and [Dalan Merchad](/wiki/Skyrim:Dalan_Merchad "Skyrim:Dalan Merchad") on deck at all times; however, the other member of the crew, [Voldsea Giryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Voldsea_Giryon "Skyrim:Voldsea Giryon"), will be found wandering [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), and will happily speak to you, explaining that she's glad they are laying over in Windhelm for a while, and that she likes to walk when on land to keep her legs strong. Speaking with [Dalan Merchad](/wiki/Skyrim:Dalan_Merchad "Skyrim:Dalan Merchad"), on the other hand, has him complaining and wishing they were underway. The captain will ask you to assist him with a [problem](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master"), and will reward you with a year's salary (a leveled amount of gold) if you accept and complete the quest.
