## Related Quests(†)

- **[Meet the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Meet_the_Family "Skyrim:Meet the Family")**: Speak with some of the members of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") and pick up your gear.
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear")**: Send a message to a former [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") client.
- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.
- **[The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit")**: Break into [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey")'s [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and search for clues.
- **[Trinity Restored](/wiki/Skyrim:Trinity_Restored "Skyrim:Trinity Restored")**: Become one of the Nightingales, [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal")'s guardians.
- **[Under New Management](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_New_Management "Skyrim:Under New Management")**: Become the Guild Master of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

(†) Other Thieves Guild quests exist, but do not require you to enter the Cistern.

### The Ragged Flagon - Cistern

You will initially be taken to the Cistern by [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"). After you meet him in [the Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), he will lead you to a storage cabinet with a false back. Behind the cabinet is a passage with a small bedroom on the right. The bedroom contains two owned beds with an end table between them, two cupboards, a round table with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and an unlocked chest. All items in the Ragged Flagon are flagged as owned, but are easy pickings. The passage behind the cabinet ends at a door that opens into the main headquarters for the Guild, the Cistern.

When you first enter the Cistern, [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") will be awaiting you in the center of the room, with five other thieves present round the room: [Cynric Endell](/wiki/Skyrim:Cynric_Endell "Skyrim:Cynric Endell"), [Niruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Niruin "Skyrim:Niruin"), [Rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Rune "Skyrim:Rune"), [Thrynn](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrynn "Skyrim:Thrynn"), and [Vipir the Fleet](/wiki/Skyrim:Vipir_the_Fleet "Skyrim:Vipir the Fleet"). Other thieves return or arrive as you complete specific quests. [Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)") returns once you have completed the [Stabilized](/wiki/Skyrim:Stabilized "Skyrim:Stabilized") quest for [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr"). [Etienne Rarnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Etienne_Rarnis "Skyrim:Etienne Rarnis") moves here once released from the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"). Finally, two new thieves, [Garthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Garthar "Skyrim:Garthar") and [Ravyn Imyan](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravyn_Imyan "Skyrim:Ravyn Imyan"), join the guild once you have started to return the Guild to its former glory.

The Cistern consists of a large circular chamber with two storm drains emptying from the ceiling high overhead, with waterfalls cascading into a pool under a cross-shaped stone walkway. There are wooden suspension bridges linking each quadrant around the outside. All containers, excluding barrels and the chests within the training room used for practicing lockpicking, are safe for storage. There is a pair of cupboards containing clutter flanking the tunnel leading into the room from the Ragged Flagon. Nine single owned beds, in addition to your bed, come out from the outer walls; seven of the ten beds have unlocked guild chests at the foot of them, all containing minor loot. There are several end tables beside the beds around the room. The first bed on the right when entering from the Ragged Flagon is assigned to you. There are additional pairs of [thieves guild gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Gloves "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Gloves") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Boots "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Boots") on the floor on either side of your bed. Around the room are several bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), wine, and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), along with a few [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") and three copies of *[Shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(book) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (book)")*, which explains the meaning of the different [symbols](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") scattered across Skyrim. Several [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes "Skyrim:Notes") can be found around the room, including ones titled *[East Empire Connection](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Connection "Skyrim:East Empire Connection")*, *[Eyes Open](/wiki/Skyrim:Eyes_Open "Skyrim:Eyes Open")*, and *[No Word Yet](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Word_Yet "Skyrim:No Word Yet")*, all of which give insights into the Guild and/or some of its members.

Opposite the entrance, in an alcove to the southeast, is a pair of double metal doors guarding the Guild's treasure room which require two keys, with a table and a barrel to the left and another cupboard containing clutter to the right. There is a desk farther to the left of the alcove, where Mercer Frey is normally found. On the desk is the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") and two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"). Behind the desk are two sets of shelves; as you acquire certain unique items as part of [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny") quest and sell them to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), they will appear on the shelves or desk. Also, as you complete more side jobs for [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") and Delvin, certain other trophies will begin to fill the shelves. Between the sets of shelves is a blank bust, which is used to display [Barenziahs Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Barenziahs_Crown "Skyrim:Barenziahs Crown") once you collect all twenty-four of the [unusual gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") and recover the crown as part of the [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned") quest. To the right of the alcove is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and a barrel in front of a row of four weapon racks, which hold an [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and a [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and an iron and a steel [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"). To the right of the rack are three archery dummies, where Cynric, Thrynn, and Ravyn Imyan (after he joins) spend hours each day honing their [archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skills.

In the alcove to the southwest is a ladder leading to the concealed cemetery entrance to Riften. To the left of the ladder is a long wooden table with a bottle of wine, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top, and to the right is a cupboard containing clutter. In front of the cupboard is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand, beside another cupboard holding two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), four [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), a bottle of alto wine, and several pieces of cheese. On the opposite side of the Cistern to the northeast is a passage with a long wooden table on the right laid with a bottle of alto wine, a [horker loaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Loaf "Skyrim:Horker Loaf"), two pieces of [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), two loaves of bread, a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"). Beside the table is a cupboard holding two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a bottle of alto wine, and some bread and cheese. To the left of the passage is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). The passage takes two turns before entering a training room - see below for details.

During the Thieves Guild quest [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit"), when you enter the Cistern from the Ragged Flagon, Vex, Delvin, and Brynjolf will be standing by the entrance with their weapons drawn. By the alternative entrance will be Vipir the Fleet and Sapphire, by the passage leading to the training room will be Niriun and Cynric Endell with Rune a short distance behind them, and Thrynn will be in the training room. After both you and [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") explain yourselves, Brynjolf asks Delvin to unlock the treasure room. Once both Delvin and Brynjolf have unlocked the door, you are all able to enter, and find Mercer has emptied all seven treasure chests within. There are a couple small wooden tables in the room with a selection of steel weapons on top, and a food barrel in the corner. The locked vault door remains unlocked, unless you stay away from the Cistern long enough for it to reset, which will reset the doors to locked.

#### Upgrades

As you complete the Thieves Guild reputation quests for Delvin Mallory, the beds are upgraded, while several screens and upgrades around the Cistern are added:

- Completing the first reputation quest adds two new Thieves Guild banners high on the walls on either side of the treasury room. The table to the southwest is laid with two bottles of alto wine, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [pheasant roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), two potatoes, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, and several more loaves of bread and pieces of cheese. Hanging above the table from racks are four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and two whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). A shield plaque is installed above the weapon racks to the right of the treasury room, with a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") and crossed [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword").
- Completing the second reputation quest adds two extra cupboards on either side of the ladder leading to the concealed entrance from the graveyard. Rugs are added throughout the zone, and two more banners are hung from the walls above the passage to the training room.
- Completing the third reputation quest makes a new thief, Garthar, join the Guild. Two more banners are hung from the walls above the concealed entrance.
- Completing the fourth and final reputation quest makes a new thief, Ravyn Imyan, join the Guild. Two final banners are added high above the entrance to the Ragged Flagon.
- After you complete the quest [Darkness Returns](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkness_Returns "Skyrim:Darkness Returns"), a shrine to Nocturnal is installed in the water between the entrance to the Ragged Flagon and the training room. When activated, you will be granted the [Blessing of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessings "Skyrim:Blessings"), a 10-point boost to your [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill, and will be cured of any [diseases](/wiki/Skyrim:Diseases "Skyrim:Diseases") you may have contracted.
- After completing the Thieves Guild questline, a long guild tribute chest appears before the desk. You can unlock this chest with a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribute_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Tribute Chest Key") given to you by Brynjolf and claim the items left as tribute for you.
- Upon completing 125 side quests for Vex and/or Delvin, a [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") is also added.

### Training Room

The training room contains several archery targets (both at ground level and in alcoves high on the walls), practice dummies, many more [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, and five different locked chests, each with a different leveled lock from novice through master. There is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Training_Chests "Skyrim:Training Chests") on the ground in front of the chests, which explains they are for practice use and they reset after a short amount of time. There is also an unlocked guild chest, two cupboards, a table, and an end table against the walls. On these are an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a complete set of thieves guild armor including the [hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Hood "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Hood"), gloves, boots, and [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Armor "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Armor"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Advances in Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Advances_in_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Advances in Lockpicking")*.

## Notes

- There is a "Guild" [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the left of the door to [the Ratway Vaults](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway_Vaults "Skyrim:The Ratway Vaults").
- The vault that [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") breaks into during [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit") cannot be open if locked.

## Bugs

- If any of the guild members see you picking the locks in the training room, they will interrupt you by commenting on it as if you weren't meant to be picking them.
- One of the practice chests in the Cistern doesn't respawn like the others.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. It was replaced with a respawning version of the same chest.
- There is no navmesh up to the base of the Nocturnal shrine that gets built in the Cistern.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- The Cistern has no proper room bounds which can cause issues with the lighting in the cell.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- The lighting may occasionally flicker when you're here.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.342, fixes this bug.

The Ragged Flagon

**The Ragged Flagon** is a [tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") that is part of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)")'s headquarters.

Not your usual tavern

The bar is run by [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man"), but the bouncer, [Dirge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dirge "Skyrim:Dirge"), will take over bartender duties if anything happens to Vekel. [Tonilia](/wiki/Skyrim:Tonilia "Skyrim:Tonilia"), the first Thieves Guild [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)"), is also always found at the bar.

The Flagon is located within [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")'s old sewer network, and can be accessed through [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). After joining the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), quicker access becomes available through the headquarters's secret entrance, which opens from behind the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)") into [the Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern"). When the secret entrance is locked later in the Thieves Guild quest line, access to the bar is still possible through the Ratway.

## Related Quests

- **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
- **[Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows")**: Find [Isabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine"), [Ranmir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") lost love.
- **[Imitation Amnesty](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Amnesty "Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty")**: Help get a convicted prisoner released from jail.
- **[Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear")**: Send a message to a former [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") client.
- **[Meet the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Meet_the_Family "Skyrim:Meet the Family")**: Speak with some of the members of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") and pick up your gear.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(quest) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum"): Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.
- **[Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining")**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") for a [silversmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon").
- **[Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows")**: Remove a rival guild from the picture.
- **[Surgery](/wiki/Skyrim:Surgery "Skyrim:Surgery")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Change your appearance.
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload")**: Frame a [ship's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") captain to get revenge for a [jilted merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur").
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit")**: Break into [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey")'s [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and search for clues.
- **[The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken")**: Meet [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre") inside [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") and learn who he wants assassinated.
- **[Toying With The Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Toying_With_The_Dead "Skyrim:Toying With The Dead")**: Retrieve a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil")'s journals for an interested buyer.
- **[Under New Management](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_New_Management "Skyrim:Under New Management")**: Become the Guild Master of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...")**: Restore the Dark Brotherhood's sanctuary.

**Note:** All [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") Thieves Guild quests have been omitted from the list.

## The Ragged Flagon

The first time you enter will be after navigating [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). Upon entering, you will be in the center of five darkened, dirty alcoves, each containing a selection of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks, barrels, crates, and disused furniture. As you complete each of the Thieves Guild [reputation quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Quests.23Special_Job_Quests.23Reputation_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), these alcoves will be occupied by the additional merchants. In front of you is a circular shallow pool, with a wooden deck opposite and the tavern behind. Following the path around to the right, beyond the fifth alcove is a wooden bridge spanning the water beneath, with a tavern sign hanging from a post on the right. The tavern has three small tables and chairs arranged in front of the counter.

There are cupboards, barrels, sacks, and crates all around the room, as well as the counter in front of the east wall. The innkeeper, [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man"), is found standing behind the counter or sweeping the floor. When first reaching the tavern, you will find [Dirge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dirge "Skyrim:Dirge"), the tavern's bouncer, talking to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") by the counter. Dirge will soon return to his usual position on the far side of the bridge, beside the tavern's sign. On the counter are a few bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). On the tables are loaves of bread, with one of them also having a [horker loaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Loaf "Skyrim:Horker Loaf"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and cheese on top. [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), who is usually found in the Ragged Flagon, is normally at this table. Behind the counter is a simple but deep fireplace, with more shelves and cupboards against the northeast wall. Behind one of the cupboards is a set of shelves holding more bottles of alto wine, [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and Nord mead, with two common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top.

Opposite the counter is a wooden ramp leading up onto the deck. [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") is also usually found in the Ragged Flagon, and is normally found standing to the right of the ramp. On the deck, there is a table on the right with a bottle of alto wine, a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [horse haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), and a loaf of bread on top. If you have [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, behind this table sitting on a bench is [Galathil](/wiki/Skyrim:Galathil "Skyrim:Galathil"), the face sculptor you've probably heard of around [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") or [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). On the left of the deck is a stack of crates, sacks, and barrels, where you will usually find [Tonilia](/wiki/Skyrim:Tonilia "Skyrim:Tonilia"), but she won't deal with you until you have proven yourself to the Thieves Guild by completing [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business"). At the end of the deck is one final table, with an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") on top.

In the southeastern corner is a wooden door that leads into [the Ratway Vaults](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway_Vaults "Skyrim:The Ratway Vaults"), with a storage cabinet on the right that requires a key to open. This will be unlocked by Brynjolf at the end of Taking Care of Business, when he will lead you to [the Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern") to introduce you to [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") and welcome you into the Thieves Guild. During the quest [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat"), you will find [Gissur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gissur "Skyrim:Gissur") sitting and drinking at the first table of the tavern or following you around the room, unless he was killed during the quest [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"). He will try to leave once you receive the information regarding [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern"); however, Vekel will suddenly announce, *"That one, right there, walking out the door! He was one of them asking about that old man you were looking for."* If confronted, Gissur will only rebuff your attempts at conversation. However, he can be attacked and killed with no repercussions, and other Thieves Guild members will join the fight on your side.

During the Thieves Guild quest [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit"), you will find both Vex and Delvin missing, and [Garthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Garthar "Skyrim:Garthar") standing in front of the door leading to the Cistern with his weapon drawn.

### Vekel the Man's Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the bar's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days. The other merchants found in the Ragged Flagon each have their own merchant chests, as detailed on their individual NPC pages. Vekel is the only merchant available in the Ragged Flagon by default, and one of only two if you don't join the Thieves Guild.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

As you complete the Thieves Guild reputation quests, new shopkeepers will move into the alcoves to either side of the doorway leading from the Ratway. Once you have completed all four of the special reputation jobs for Delvin, the main furniture within the tavern will be improved to better quality replacements.

### Galathil's Shop

Galathil's shop is opened by installing the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on. She can change your appearance for the price of 1000 gold, but not your race or gender. If you are a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") she says she cannot do anything for you, as she can only work on the living and being undead doesn't count. Galathil's shop is open by default in the [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition") and [Nintendo Switch version](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch"). Galthil is one of only two merchants available in the Ragged Flagon if you don't join the Thieves Guild.

### Syndus' Shop

Syndus' shop is opened after completing the first reputation quest (see [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Syndus "Skyrim:Syndus") for his standard merchandise). None of the displayed merchandise can be purchased, only stolen.

It is located in the first alcove on the right when entering from the Ratway, and contains a counter, three archery targets, several crates, a rack hanging from the ceiling, and a chair that Syndus seems to spend most of his time sitting in. The items on display include a random enchanted [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and a loaf of bread on the counter. On the ledge along the walls, to the northwest is a leveled bow, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), to the southwest behind the targets is a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), and to the southeast are two bottles of alto wine, two bottles of wine, and a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"). On the ground beside Syndus' chair are a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), while hanging from the rack is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), and a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid").

### Herluin Lothaire's Shop

Herluin Lothaire's shop is opened after completing the second reputation quest (see [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Herluin_Lothaire "Skyrim:Herluin Lothaire") for his standard merchandise). None of the displayed merchandise can be purchased, only stolen.

It is located in the first alcove on the left when entering from the Ratway, with a wooden apothecary's sign hanging from a post to the left of the alcove. It contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), a small sideboard, a wall shelf, a small counter, and a chair. Herluin seems to split his time between working at his alchemy lab and sitting in his chair. The items found on display around the alcove are listed below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

### Arnskar Ember-Master's Shop

Arnskar Ember-Master's shop is opened after completing the third reputation quest (see [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnskar_Ember-Master "Skyrim:Arnskar Ember-Master") for his standard merchandise). None of the displayed merchandise can be purchased, only stolen.

It is located in the second alcove on the left when entering from the Ratway, with a wrought blacksmith's sign hanging from a post above the front of the arch. It contains a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and a small counter. Arnskar spends his time either working at his crafting stations or sitting on the ground in front of the alcove with his legs dangling in the water. On the counter is an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a set of bellows, tongs, and a hammer. An [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), an [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), a bottle of wine, and a [venison chop](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Chop "Skyrim:Venison Chop") on a wooden plate are on the ledge along the walls. Two shield plaques are in the alcove; one holds a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") with two crossed iron greatswords, and the other holds a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield") with two crossed [steel greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword").

### Vanryth Gatharian's Shop

Vanryth Gatharian's shop is opened after completing the fourth reputation quest (see [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Vanryth_Gatharian "Skyrim:Vanryth Gatharian") for his standard merchandise). None of the displayed merchandise can be purchased, only stolen.

It is located in the second alcove on the right when entering from the Ratway, and contains a counter, several crates, a small shelving unit, two food barrels, and a chair that Vanryth seems to spend most of his time sitting in. The items on display include a random enchanted [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor") [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") and enchanted light armor [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") on top of the counter. A [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), a pair of boots, and a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), all light armor, are found on the ledge along the walls, while two [hide shields](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield") are on top of one of the crates and two bottles of wine are on a shelf of the unit.

## Notes

- This is the only tavern you'll find that is located under the ground.
- You cannot invest with any of the merchants here. All except for Vekel and Galathil[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") benefit from the [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader") perk.
- All merchants here are part of the ThievesGuildFaction, and will jump to the Guild's defense if hostilities erupt in the Ragged Flagon, either from you or someone else.
- If you ask [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") where [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") is during [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat"), she will describe the Ragged Flagon as a place "where thieves get drunk and knife each other."
- The sewers that would become The Ragged Flagon appear in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as the [Riften Outlaws Refuge](/wiki/Online:Riften_Outlaws_Refuge "Online:Riften Outlaws Refuge"). The Ragged Flagon also [appears](/wiki/Legends:Ragged_Flagon "Legends:Ragged Flagon") in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*, having been added with the *[Return to Clockwork City](/wiki/Legends:Return_to_Clockwork_City "Legends:Return to Clockwork City")* storyline.

## Bugs

- None of the NPCs ever sleep here, as there are no beds available for them.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. An extra room is added to the zone. This room is to the left of the door leading to the [Ratway Vaults](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway_Vaults "Skyrim:The Ratway Vaults"), and contains beds for the NPCs who live in the Flagon. It will also improve as expected with the guildhall itself.
- The encounter zone for this cell is incorrectly set up causing it not to respawn correctly.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.04, addresses this issue. The location value in the encounter zone is fixed, giving the Ragged Flagon a respawn time of 30 days.
- Some of the light sources here may appear to go out when looked at from an angle.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, addresses this issue. The Ragged Flagon required the placement of room bounds to separate the light sources.

## Maps

- 

  An interior map of the Ragged Flagon

# Skyrim:The Raid

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") to uncover and stop the illegal [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") trade in town.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | FreeformRiften20 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand") | **Next →** [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand") | | → Next | [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand") | | |

Discover a cache of moon sugar and skooma while investigating.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") after completing the [Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand") quest.
2. Report to the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") about the presence of a [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") dealer in town.
3. "Deal" with [Sarthis Idren](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarthis_Idren "Skyrim:Sarthis Idren"), and find evidence to locate his sources.
4. Return to the jarl with the evidence.

### Illegal Trade

After completing the [Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand") quest, you can ask [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") where she obtained her [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). She is not forthcoming with the details, however you can pass an easy-level [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade her to tell you the truth.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I think you owe me one. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Okay, okay, I'll tell you. **Failed**: It's not worth dying over. | | | | **Passed**: Reveal the supplier **Failed**: Nothing |
| Here, does this help? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Okay, okay, I'll tell you. **Failed**: It's got nothing to do with the coin... this is my life we're talking about. | | | | **Passed**: Reveal the supplier **Failed**: Nothing |
| And who says I won't? **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Okay, okay, I'll tell you. **Failed**: You can't threaten me any worse than they have! | | | | **Passed**: Reveal the supplier **Failed**: Nothing |
| Okay, never mind. | Thank you. | | | | Nothing |

At last, she will reveal her supplier as [Sarthis Idren](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarthis_Idren "Skyrim:Sarthis Idren") and his base as [Riften Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Warehouse "Skyrim:Riften Warehouse"). She explains that the warehouse is always locked and that only the jarl has a key.

The next step is to report the presence of a skooma dealer to the jarl. The current jarl in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") will acknowledge Sarthis and his illegal operations. However, the dealer has informants in the town guard because he disappears every time they raid the warehouse. Perhaps, an outsider may be able to surprise Sarthis in the warehouse, and *"'convince' him to close down his operation"*. If you accept the mission, you will be given the [Riften Warehouse Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Warehouse_Key "Skyrim:Riften Warehouse Key") to unlock the warehouse.

### The Raid

The warehouse is located at the southern end of Riften's docks. [Orini Dral](/wiki/Skyrim:Orini_Dral "Skyrim:Orini Dral") is patrolling the warehouse, and will immediately spot you. Sarthis is in the basement and will come rushing upstairs to aid his bodyguard. Orini is a modest opponent, but Sarthis can prove a difficult opponent to defeat.

When they are dead, loot Sarthis' body for [his key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarthis%27s_Key "Skyrim:Sarthis's Key"). Descend the stairs in the northeastern corner, turn around and use the key to unlock the door. On the shelves there are five bowls of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar") and six bottles of skooma. On the table there is another bowl of moon sugar and two bottles of skooma. Inside Sarthis' satchel there is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipment%27s_Ready "Skyrim:Shipment's Ready") with information regarding Sarthis' sources. Make sure to read the note to advance the quest.

### It's Not Over Yet

Return to the jarl with the evidence and news of Sarthis' demise. The jarl will be grateful, saying, *"It's nice to receive good news for a change"*, but will ask you to continue the crusade, which starts the [next quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand").

## Notes

- If Wujeeta dies before you report the skooma dealer to the jarl, you will fail the quest, making it impossible to become thane of the Rift regardless of who the jarl is.
- If Sarthis is killed by anyone other than you, you will fail the quest. The key and the note can still be obtained, but no relevant dialogue option will be available from the jarl to proceed.
- If you manage to sneak past or Calm Orini, you can spare his life. Only Sarthis has to die for the quest to progress.
- This is the second of three required quests that are required to unlock the option to become [Thane of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!"). There are additional requirements noted on that quest page.
- The penultimate objective, "Recover skooma source information", will only register as completed if you read the note, unlike most other objectives of this type which only require you to take a note.
- Despite [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") telling you to deal with Sarthis 'discreetly', stealth is not required to succeed in the quest.

## Bugs

- Even though you were given a key by the jarl, and it is occupied by enemies, you will be considered to be trespassing in the warehouse. If you have a follower they will react as such.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - Due to an engine limitation (see [this discussion](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19602)), the player will still incur an increment in their "Trespasses" stat after reading the note.
  - There is a way to enter without it counting as trespassing. When you open the door, before you enter, immediately open the menu and make a fast travel. You will see that you will still enter the warehouse. Then load the game that was saved by making the fast travel. You will be in front of the door but now it will be open. Turn into a werewolf and access the warehouse. It will no longer count as trespassing.
  - If your follower insists on reporting you for stealing the note, you will need to exit the warehouse to ask them to wait.
- The quest marker may be stuck at "Recover skooma source information" and point to the apothecary's satchel, even after you have killed Sarthis yourself and taken the Shipment's Ready note.
  - Reading the note should advance the quest as normal.

## Quest Stages

| The Raid (FreeformRiften20) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Identify Riften's skooma dealer |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Report Sarthis Idren to the Jarl of Riften |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Enter Riften Warehouse |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Eliminate Sarthis Idren |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Recover skooma source information |
| 200 | ☑ | *(Starts [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"))* |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften20 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften20`.

The Ratway

**The Ratway** is a network of sewer tunnels running beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), and home to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). There are three zones to the Ratway, namely *[The Ratway](#The_Ratway)*, *[The Ratway Vaults](#The_Ratway_Vaults)*, and *[The Ratway Warrens](#The_Ratway_Warrens)*. The entrance to the sewer is below [the Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer"), and the nearest stairs down to the lower level of Riften are beside [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage"). The sewers can also be accessed through [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), after joining the Thieves Guild. The Ratway is used by non-members of the Thieves Guild to access The Ragged Flagon.

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | The Ratway | | --- | | **[Drahff](/wiki/Skyrim:Drahff "Skyrim:Drahff")**  **[Gian the Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Gian_the_Fist "Skyrim:Gian the Fist")**  **[Hewnon Black-Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Hewnon_Black-Skeever "Skyrim:Hewnon Black-Skeever")**  **[Lowlife](/wiki/Skyrim:Lowlife "Skyrim:Lowlife")**  **[Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket_(person) "Skyrim:Pickpocket (person)")** [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim") **[Skritch](/wiki/Skyrim:Skritch "Skyrim:Skritch")** [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim") (skeever) | | | [The Ratway Vaults](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway_Vaults "Skyrim:The Ratway Vaults") | | --- | | **[Lowlifes](/wiki/Skyrim:Lowlife "Skyrim:Lowlife")**  **[Vagrants](/wiki/Skyrim:Vagrant "Skyrim:Vagrant")** | | | [The Ratway Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway_Warrens "Skyrim:The Ratway Warrens") | | --- | | **[Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern")**  **[Hefid the Deaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Hefid_the_Deaf "Skyrim:Hefid the Deaf")**  **[Knjakr](/wiki/Skyrim:Knjakr "Skyrim:Knjakr")**  **[Salvianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvianus "Skyrim:Salvianus")** | |

### Thieves Guild

- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit")**: Break into [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey")'s [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and search for clues.

### Other

- **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
- **[A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Seek out a cursed Tsaesci blade in the Ratway.
- **[Bow to the Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_to_the_Master "Skyrim:Bow to the Master")**: Retrieve a [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin_Llanith "Skyrim:Dravin Llanith")'s stolen bow.
- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.
- **[Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(quest) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum"): Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.
- **[The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken")**: Meet [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre") inside [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") and learn who he wants assassinated.
- **[Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...")**: Restore the Dark Brotherhood's sanctuary.

### The Ratway

At the bottom of the steps from the main entrance is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). Past this there are two alcoves. On the left is a [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing through the grate in the floor. At the end of the tunnel are [Drahff](/wiki/Skyrim:Drahff "Skyrim:Drahff") and [Hewnon Black-Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Hewnon_Black-Skeever "Skyrim:Hewnon Black-Skeever") discussing their decision to move into the Ratway and attack anyone looking to pass. Eliminate them both and continue. To the left of the campfire is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). The next area is a square room with an unowned bedroll and a single piece of bread between the bedroll and the right wall. On the floor opposite the bedroll is an iron mace. From here you can see a raised bridge. The lever to lower the bridge is on the other side, so it is not possible to get to it directly.

You must drop down to the stone floor below, where a wandering [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") makes its home. A darkened tunnel is blocked by an expert-locked gate, while a lit tunnel leads to an apprentice-[trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") wooden door. The trap triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the left side that is easily avoided by simply stepping back.

The next room has an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"), with an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging above. To the left are [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), a woodcutter's axe, and a pair of [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves "Skyrim:Gloves"). Another skeever makes its home in the tunnel on the left.

Through the open door opposite is a small room containing an unowned bedroll in the corner. Shelves hold some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and [cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, and a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). Three [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") are inaccessible in (or under) a pot, while a fourth may be blown out of the room by burning the oil slick outside. The gold can be accessed by moving the pot.

Through the closed door awaits [Gian the Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Gian_the_Fist "Skyrim:Gian the Fist"), who wears the unique [Gloves of the Pugilist](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves_of_the_Pugilist "Skyrim:Gloves of the Pugilist"). He has a very high detection level, making it nearly impossible to sneak up to him. He sits at the far side of the room beside his bedroll. Just inside the door are five [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). The room contains a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), an unowned hay pile in the corner, and four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") scattered on the ground. In an alcove is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a leveled random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), with a second leveled poison on the floor to its left.

The next room has a leveled potion of [health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") on the sill of a round grate at the foot of the stairs. On the third step from the top of the stairs, on the left-hand side, is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") from behind you. With the [Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [Skritch](/wiki/Skyrim:Skritch "Skyrim:Skritch")'s cage can be found next to the stairs. With the [Dawnfang & Duskfang](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang") Creation installed, the entrance to [the Guardian Vault](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Vault "Skyrim:The Guardian Vault") is in the southern corner, through a sewer grate.

Through the locked grated door at the top of the stairs is a small naturally lit room, with vegetation growing in the center including a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and roots hanging down from the ceiling all around the room. There is an executioner's block with an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") driven into it near two hanging moss hanging down. With the [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") Creation installed, the entrance to [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(place) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (place)") can be found behind a gate in this room. Butterflies are sometimes found here.

Continuing through the next tunnel, you will come upon a [Lowlife](/wiki/Skyrim:Lowlife "Skyrim:Lowlife") who is facing away from you. On the table is a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)")*, a loaf of bread, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). There are two tunnels to the north. The left-hand tunnel leads to the raised bridge seen previously from the other side and its associated lever. The right-hand tunnel leads to the expert-locked gate seen previously. The door to the east leads to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").

During the quest [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat"), [Shavari](/wiki/Skyrim:Shavari "Skyrim:Shavari") will be seen around town, and will be waiting for you as soon as you enter the Ratway.

### The Ratway Vaults

You can get to the vaults through The Ragged Flagon; the door is to the right of the bar. Alternatively, they can also be entered through the hole in Riftweald Manor marked with a "Danger" shadowmark in which you will drop into an alcove on the top floor near the Ragged Flagon door. The door from the Ragged Flagon itself opens to a large three-floored room. The darkened path heads to the left and passes two small alcoves before exiting to the east into a tunnel. At the end of the tunnel where it enters a room, there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers two [swinging maces](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") from the ceiling straight ahead. In the left-hand corner of the room is an unowned bed with a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead)#Nord3 "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") lying on top. There is a campfire opposite the entrance, with three blocks of wood for seats, a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack, and three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") beside it; three [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") are nearby. Through a wooden door is another tunnel heading south. By a barred window on the right are a lit brazier and a chair, and leaning against the bars is a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"). Above the brazier is a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid") and some [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam").

Following the path around the pillar and the next corner, there are two alcoves to the left. The second alcove has no floor and an oil lantern that can be knocked down onto an oil slick on the floor of the level below. The tunnel then turns west and at the end turns north, leading into the first room on the next level down from the initial entrance. There is a [Vagrant](/wiki/Skyrim:Vagrant "Skyrim:Vagrant") patrolling along the path. Complete the circle and continue going under the entrance. The passage continues into a room in darkness. The room contains an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") with a pair of random enchanted [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), three [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in the hay behind the anvil. There is a lit tunnel heading west opposite the workbench, with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") on the ground. The room after this is guarded by another Vagrant who uses a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") at the top of two flights of stairs and a [Lowlife](/wiki/Skyrim:Lowlife "Skyrim:Lowlife") by a table at the bottom. The room contains a long wooden table and chairs in the middle of the room with a random enchanted [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), three small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), one large coin purse, six loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a loaf of bread, and two miniature [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), one unlocked and the other apprentice-locked, both containing minor loot. Under the stairs, against the north wall are two sets of shelves holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") among a lot of clutter and an apprentice-locked chest to the right. Painted on the wall above is the "Loot" shadowmark. The chest contains [Dravin's bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Dravin's Bow") among its loot, a unique bow stolen from [Dravin Llanith](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin_Llanith "Skyrim:Dravin Llanith"), the owner of [Merryfair Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Merryfair_Farm "Skyrim:Merryfair Farm") just outside [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") to the north. He and his wife were recently robbed; speaking to him will initiate a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_to_the_Master "Skyrim:Bow to the Master") to recover the bow from thieves in the Ratway. A short tunnel leads south from here to an overgrown corner section of the tunnel that contains a skeever. The tunnel eventually opens up to the first room again, this time on the bottom floor. There is an open gate opposite, and barred windows line the east wall. On the ground is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), while against the north wall is a straw bale with a couple food sacks nearby. Beyond the open gate on the ground is a small oil slick below the oil lantern seen in the tunnel above (if the slick hadn't previously been burned away by dropping the lantern from above). Against the south wall, behind more bars is a random [Fortify Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Health "Skyrim:Fortify Health") [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on the ground, and to the left is a short tunnel leading down some stairs to a door that opens into the Ratway Warrens.

During the quest A Cornered Rat, two [Thalmor soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Soldier "Skyrim:Thalmor Soldier") and a [Thalmor wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Wizard "Skyrim:Thalmor Wizard") will be found in the Vaults, with the wizard opposite the entrance, and the soldiers each on one of the floors below.

### The Ratway Warrens

You enter into a darkened tunnel with an apprentice-locked gate on your right and a lit room behind. At the end, the tunnel turns west and ends in an open doorway into the same room. In front is a flight of stone stairs leading up to a ledge above, with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the ground at the bottom. On your right is some wooden scaffolding, while on the left is a straw bale, and beyond that a wooden door. This opens into a small room containing [Salvianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvianus "Skyrim:Salvianus"), a mad, retired [Imperial soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") who fought in the Great War. He is normally found sitting on a chair eating [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). He rambles, and doesn't seem to make much sense. There is an unowned bedroll on the ground, and a wooden table at the rear of the room with two leveled [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") (one of [pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Pickpocketing "Skyrim:Potion of Pickpocketing") and the other of [light feet](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Light_Feet "Skyrim:Potion of Light Feet")), an enchanted [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), an [Imperial officer's helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Officer%27s_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Officer's Helmet"), and a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") on top, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") underneath. All of these items are marked as owned, and taking them is considered stealing.

To the right of the stairs, against the north wall is an apprentice-locked door, behind which you can hear a female who also sounds disturbed. Her name is [Hefid the Deaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Hefid_the_Deaf "Skyrim:Hefid the Deaf"), and she is sitting on the ground in the dark facing away from you. She is carrying several items, including a [burned book](/wiki/Skyrim:Burned_Book "Skyrim:Burned Book"), a bucket, a [flawless garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Garnet "Skyrim:Flawless Garnet"), an inkwell, and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). She constantly checks to ensure she hasn't lost any item. You may not be able to interact with her in order to pickpocket or even view the items.

At the top of the stairs is an unlocked gate directly in front, behind which [Knjakr](/wiki/Skyrim:Knjakr "Skyrim:Knjakr"), a mad chef, will attack as soon as you approach, declaring, *"I'm going to eat well tonight, my darling!"* implying he's a cannibal. His apparel consists of a [chef's tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Chef's Tunic"), a [chef's hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat"), and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes"). He is armed with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"). His room has partially caved in, with an unowned bedroll, a table with a piece of random [raw meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") on top, and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") in the small area not covered with earth. To the south is another small room containing an unowned single bed and an empty table behind an unlocked gate. To the left of this room is an alcove with a large square hole in the floor that drops down into Salvianus' room. At the end of the raised walkway is a substantial door with many locks, bolts, and chains. If you try to open the door, a small slot will open, and a man will explain you are not welcome and threaten you. During the quest A Cornered Rat, you discover this to be the door to [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern")'s room. The room is very well stocked and decorated, certainly out of place for the Ratway.

During the quest A Cornered Rat, the only person seen in the Warrens is Salvianus. Everyone else has disappeared. When you reach the heavily-locked door and go through the conversation, eventually Esbern will admit who he is and let you in. His room contains a single bed with a small table beside it holding copies of *[The Dragon Break](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dragon_Break "Skyrim:The Dragon Break")* and *[The Rise and Fall of the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Blades "Skyrim:The Rise and Fall of the Blades")* and a random enchanted [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). A stack of crates beside this table has a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") on top, and at the foot of the bed is an unlocked chest. A dresser can be found opposite with rolls of paper on top. A [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") is leaning against the west wall, with a desk near the same wall with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Fire and Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_and_Darkness "Skyrim:Fire and Darkness")*, and several [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top and piled on the floor beside it. A bookcase behind the desk holds a further eleven common books, as well as copies of *[Magic from the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_from_the_Sky "Skyrim:Magic from the Sky")*, *[The Dragon War](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dragon_War "Skyrim:The Dragon War")*, *[Feyfolken III](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_III "Skyrim:Feyfolken III")*, *[Children of the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Children_of_the_Sky "Skyrim:Children of the Sky")*, and *[The Wolf Queen, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v6 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v6")*, a bottle of Nord mead, a [silver jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Jeweled Necklace"), and twelve loose septims. There is a small set of shelves against the south wall with four more common books, two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and a loaf of bread. There is an end table beside the door, with a common book and a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* on top and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in the corner beside it. An adjacent counter wraps around to the south wall, with a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), two [charred skeever hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), two [skeever tails](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [blue butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), two random potions, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a bottle of Nord mead on top and on the shelves underneath. Hanging above the counter are two whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), and two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear").

When you leave Esbern's room, or if you stay too long, you will be attacked by another [Thalmor soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Soldier "Skyrim:Thalmor Soldier") and [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Wizard "Skyrim:Thalmor Wizard").

## Notes

- The Ratway, the Ratway Vaults, and [the Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") never respawn. However, the Ratway Warrens respawn on a standard ten-day schedule.
- In the Ratway, the skeever is a good climber, and likely has already attacked the Lowlife. You can usually hear this happen soon after entering the initial entrance.
- If you make enough noise in the Ratway entrance, the Lowlife may grab the iron battle axe, deal with the skeever, and rush toward you even before you've jumped beneath the raised bridge.
- There is [cut content](/wiki/Skyrim:Cut_Content "Skyrim:Cut Content") that would have included the ability to persuade Drahff and Hewnon to leave you alone with a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of 50 or better. Instead, both men always attack on sight.
- During [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat"), the only NPC that remains in the Ratway Vaults is the Nord who is alive; all the others are gone, while a few Thalmor are added, the locations of which are on the quest page.
- Riften Guards call the Ratway "the city under the city. Dark, dangerous, and no place for decent folk."
- There are three [shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") found here:
  - A "Guild" shadowmark is on the left side of the ground before the gated door to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). It's marked for being the headquarters of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
  - A "Loot" shadowmark is above the chest in the northwest room of the Ratway Vaults.
  - A "Danger" shadowmark can be seen after going through [Riftweald Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and before dropping down into the Ratway Vaults.
- In [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends"), there is a reference to the Ratway, with a card named [Ratway Prospector](/wiki/Legends:Ratway Prospector).

## Bugs

- Drahff and Hewnon Black-Skeever's corpses may remain in the Ratway indefinitely.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. They were missing the dead body cleanup script.
- The leveled potions in the Ratway often fall through the floor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The enchanted gauntlets in the Ratway Vaults sometimes fall through the table.

# Skyrim:The Reach
