Part of the Reach

**The Reach** is a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in western [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), with [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") as its capital. It is initially affiliated with the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), but can be captured by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") after completing [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)") and [The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)"). It can also change sides as part of negotiations during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").

The terrain is very mountainous, containing the [Druadach Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Mountains "Skyrim:Druadach Mountains"). The far eastern edge of the hold from [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt") in the north to [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") in the south is more hilly. The mighty [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") and several smaller tributaries originate here.

The Reach is home to the native [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), who will attack any outsiders on sight.

Map of the Reach

Markarth, the hold capital

## Flora and Fauna

The most characteristic flora are the [juniper berry bushes](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") which are native to the Reach. [Hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"), more common to caves, also seems to thrive there. [Mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") and sparse populations of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Mountain Flower") are to be found throughout the hold but in the northeast the flowers can be quite common.

## Places

All locations in the Reach with individual map markers are listed. There are a few places without map markers listed for their significance.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")** — A major city in the southwest of Skyrim near the border of [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), and the capital of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Markarth)
-  **[Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep")** — An ancient Dwarven keep built into the mountainside, used as a palace by the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Understone+Keep)
-  **[Markarth Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Markarth Stables")** — A [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") located outside [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), opposite the entrance. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Markarth+Stables)

### Farms, Towns, and Settlements including Orc Strongholds and Inns

-  **[Cliffside Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Cliffside_Retreat "Skyrim:Cliffside Retreat")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") south of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cliffside+Retreat)
-  **[Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal")** — A prosperous [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") in the southwest of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dushnikh+Yal)
-  **[Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim") — A Nordic hall player home in the Reach, north of [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hendraheim+%28CC%29)
-  **[Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten")** — A mining [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in the northern Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthwasten)
-  **[Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur")** — An [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") in the far northwest of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and north of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur)
-  **[Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn")** — A remote inn in the Reach where [Tiber Septim](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim") once stayed. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Old+Hroldan+Inn)
-  **[Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm")** — A small farm east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Salvius+Farm)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt")** — A small [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave south of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Redoubt)
-  **[Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire")** — A large [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire)
-  **[Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp")** — A large [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire)
-  **[Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in the Reach, located south of [Bthardamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Bthardamz "Skyrim:Bthardamz") and west of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Reach Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in the Reach, located west of [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat") and northeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Stormcloak+Camp)

### Caves

-  **[Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") along the banks of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
-  **[Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bruca%27s+Leap+Redoubt)
-  **[Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") containing [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkfall+Cave+%28DG%29)
-  **[Gloomreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloomreach "Skyrim:Gloomreach")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") in the Reach containing [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") and [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gloomreach)
-  **[Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") and connected underground cellar northeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and invading [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Liar%27s+Retreat)
-  **[Purewater Run](/wiki/Skyrim:Purewater_Run "Skyrim:Purewater Run")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Purewater+Run)
-  **[Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachcliff+Cave)
-  **[Reachwater Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwater_Rock "Skyrim:Reachwater Rock")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwater+Rock)
-  **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rebel%27s+Cairn)
-  **[Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") and two exterior camps east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Red+Eagle+Redoubt)
-  **[Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons") — A large [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt") containing mercenaries, [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"), [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"), and [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Runoff+Caverns+%28CC%29)

### Dragon Lairs

-  **[Dragontooth Crater](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragontooth_Crater "Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater")** — A [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") north-northwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragontooth+Crater)

### Mines

- **[Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")** — A medium-sized [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and forced-labor [prison camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Jails "Skyrim:Jails") in southern [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cidhna+Mine)
-  **[Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine")** — A small [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") east-northeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") initially containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kolskeggr+Mine)
-  **[Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine")** — A small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Left+Hand+Mine)
-  **[Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole")** — A small [moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone "Skyrim:Moonstone") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") initially containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Soljund%27s+Sinkhole)

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic

-  **[Arkngthamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Arkngthamz "Skyrim:Arkngthamz")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southeast of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arkngthamz+%28DG%29)
-  **[Bthardamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Bthardamz "Skyrim:Bthardamz")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west-northwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [Afflicted](/wiki/Skyrim:Afflicted "Skyrim:Afflicted") and [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bthardamz)
-  **[Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt")** — A large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deepwood+Redoubt)
-  **[Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dustman%27s+Cairn)[†](#intnote_1)
-  **[Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout")** — A small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") south of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Four+Skull+Lookout)
-  **[Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag+Rock+Redoubt)
-  **[Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag%27s+End)
-  **[Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt")** — A massive [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") inhabited by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valley+Redoubt)
- **[Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") accessed from inside [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nchuand-Zel)
-  **[Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Otar the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar_the_Mad "Skyrim:Otar the Mad"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ragnvald)
-  **[Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie")** — A small [Dwarven](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") tower east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwind+Eyrie)
-  **[Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valthume)

[†](#note_1)Only technically located in the Reach.

### Standing Stones and Daedric Shrines

-  **[The Lover Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover_Stone "Skyrim:The Lover Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Lover+Stone)
-  **[Shrine to Peryite](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_to_Peryite "Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite")** — The [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+to+Peryite)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") inhabited by [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") and [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), located northwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") on an outcrop of rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakwind+Bluff)
-  **[Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Tower+Redoubt)
-  **[Cradle Stone Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradle_Stone_Tower "Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") west of [Bard's Leap Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit") containing a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cradle+Stone+Tower)
-  **[Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") inhabited by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), located south-southwest of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), just above [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Crone+Rock)
-  **[Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard")** — A large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") initially occupied by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Sungard)
-  **[Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing the warlock [Kornalus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kornalus "Skyrim:Kornalus") and his enchanted [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Harmugstahl)
-  **[Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined [Nordic towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") southeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sundered+Towers)

### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

-  **[Bard's Leap Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit")** — A wooden plank at the very top of [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bard%27s+Leap+Summit)
-  **[Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing")** — An ancient [Dwarven](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") bridge over a weir with structures at either end in the northern part of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deep+Folk+Crossing)
- **[Druadach Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Mountains "Skyrim:Druadach Mountains")** — A mountain range in western [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") serving as a natural barrier to separate [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") from [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock") and [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Mountains)
- **[Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River")** — A river flowing from [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karth+River)
-  **[Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie")** — A small [Dwarven](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") tower east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwind+Eyrie)
-  **[Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple")** — A large mountaintop fort that served as the major [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") temple and outpost in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), now long abandoned and in [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") territory. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sky+Haven+Temple)

### Unmarked Places

- There are three [Dragon Mounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") in the Reach.
  - West of [Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt").
  - West of [The Lover Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover_Stone "Skyrim:The Lover Stone").
  - South of [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp").
- There are three [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") in the Reach.
  - A [Shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrine of Dibella") south of [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn").
  - A [Shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara") south of [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole").
  - A [Shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar") west of [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout").

## The Reach Quests

Quests that are started in or related to the Reach (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").

### Imperial Legion Civil War Quests

- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)")**: Retake [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Stormcloaks Civil War Quests

- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)")**: Blackmail a [Talos worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") into helping the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Daedric Quests

- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").
- **[The Only Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure")**: Slay an apostate [worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Orchendor "Skyrim:Orchendor") for the Daedra Lord [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite").
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.
- **[Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster")**: Assume the identity of the famous [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") in an effort to assassinate the Emperor.
- **[Kill Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Kill Ma'randru-jo")**: Assassinate [Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Ma'randru-jo") to complete a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") contract.
- **[Locate the Assassin of Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Locate_the_Assassin_of_Old "Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old")**: Find the Dark Brotherhood [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin").

### Thieves Guild

- **[Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers")**: Help translate [Gallus's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining")**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") for a [silversmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon").
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

### Side Quests

- **[Evil in Waiting](/wiki/Skyrim:Evil_in_Waiting "Skyrim:Evil in Waiting")**: Seal away an [ancient evil](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)").
- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").
- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").
- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!
- **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")**: Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").

### Dawnguard Quests

- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Search for the Dwemer's [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge").
- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

### Creation Club Quests

- **[Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put a stop to two bandit gangs wielding strange otherworldly equipment.
- **[Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor"): Investigate rumors of a ghost that haunts the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").
- **[Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(quest) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim"): Earn the deed to an [ancient Nordic hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)").
- **[If I had a Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:If_I_had_a_Hammer "Skyrim:If I had a Hammer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer"): Steal a legendary hammer of the gods.
- **[My Pet Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab"): Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").
- **[Relics of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Relics_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Relics of the Crusader")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader"): Reclaim the holy relics of Pelinal Whitestrake.

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests are located in the Reach. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#The_Reach "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

## Bugs

- Manually mining ore in Cidhna Mine can make it impossible to serve your sentence here properly.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- The guard at Soljund's Sinkhole will always be an Empire-affiliated Reach Hold Guard, due to `SoljundSinkholeLocation` missing keywords for changing the garrison if the Stormcloaks take the Reach.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- The Imperial guard who patrols near Salvius Farm is called "Markarth City Guard", even though he isn't in the city.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The guard is now called "Reach Hold Guard".
- Due to the fact that [Ramati](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati "Skyrim:Ramati"), [Mani](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani "Skyrim:Mani"), and [Sudi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi "Skyrim:Sudi") at [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse") are part of the Reach crime faction, should you resurrect and re-kill them, then you could theoretically receive a bounty here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.

---
source_url: "https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless"

entity_type: "quest"
namespace: "Skyrim"
retrieved_at: "2026-05-04T23:44:36.670881+00:00"
tags: ["MetaTemplate-Load", "Skyrim-Creation Club-Quests", "Skyrim-Dead Man's Dread", "Skyrim-Quests", "Skyrim-Quests with Incorrectly Named Images", "Skyrim-SRQRP-Requires Final Review", "Skyrim-Unconfirmed Bugs"]

# Skyrim:The Restless

## Overview

This article is about the quest. For the book, see [The Restless (book)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless_(book) "Skyrim:The Restless (book)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Search for an ancient pirate ship.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | *[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless_(book) "Skyrim:The Restless (book)")* |
| Location(s): | [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever"), [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon"), [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear"), [Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle") |
| Reward: | [Blackwater Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackwater_Blade "Skyrim:Blackwater Blade"), [Cyrus' Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Boots "Skyrim:Cyrus' Boots"), [Cyrus' Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Clothes "Skyrim:Cyrus' Clothes"), [Cyrus' Sabre](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Sabre "Skyrim:Cyrus' Sabre"); Access to *[Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread_(place) "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread (place)")* |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE031\_QUEST |
| Added by: | [Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") |

Pirate loot awaits

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless_(book) "Skyrim:The Restless (book)")* at [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever").
2. Gain access to the cell in [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon") by whatever means necessary and read *[Kevon's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Kevon%27s_Note "Skyrim:Kevon's Note")*. Take the map.
3. Travel to [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear") and find the boat to [Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle").
4. Enter [Blackbone Isle Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto") and take [Cyrus' Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Boots "Skyrim:Cyrus' Boots"), [Cyrus' Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Clothes "Skyrim:Cyrus' Clothes"), and [Cyrus' Sabre](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Sabre "Skyrim:Cyrus' Sabre").
5. Fight your way back out to the boat.

### A Pirate's Life

To begin this quest, you will need to go to [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). On one of the tables inside, you will find a book titled *[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless_(book) "Skyrim:The Restless (book)")* which describes the later life of [Cyrus](/wiki/Lore:Cyrus "Lore:Cyrus"), the protagonist of *[The Elder Scrolls Adventures: Redguard](/wiki/Redguard:Redguard "Redguard:Redguard")*. It mentions [Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle"), a long-lost island in the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts") said to house an ancient treasure. The last person to visit the island reportedly died in the nearby [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") dungeons.

Head to the dungeons in order to figure out how to gain access to the cell containing the pirate's corpse. You can speak to a [Solitude Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") seated outside the cell and pass an easy [Persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill check to convince him to open the cell for you. A starting level character of any race can pass this speech check by activating the [Shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrines") in the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") just outside. Alternatively, you can commit a crime yourself and get thrown in jail, although there are obviously some [disadvantages](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Going_to_Jail "Skyrim:Crime") to using this method. Once inside, you will find the skeletal corpse of [Kevon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kevon "Skyrim:Kevon") next to a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Kevon%27s_Note "Skyrim:Kevon's Note") you need to read. It will reveal that a [map to Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_to_Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Map to Blackbone Isle") can be found beneath a loose brick within the cell wall. Grab it and head for the coast.

### Old Pirate Den

Your next destination after escaping Castle Dour is a coastal shipwreck known as [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear"). Although this location is usually inhabited by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), on this occasion you will encounter a gang of [Blackwater Brigands](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackwater_Brigand "Skyrim:Blackwater Brigand") led by [Celeste](/wiki/Skyrim:Celeste "Skyrim:Celeste"). This encounter will actually add an unnamed miscellaneous objective to your journal directing you to kill Celeste and claim her unique sword, the [Blackwater Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackwater_Blade "Skyrim:Blackwater Blade"). This is secondary to the current quest, but you will likely end up killing Celeste in any case as the brigands are hostile and are guarding the only boat to Blackbone Isle.

Once the threat has been neutralized, activate the small boat to sail to Blackbone Isle. The entirety of the small island consists of a shoreline crawling with [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead"); indeed, you will likely be attacked the minute you arrive. You may explore the island's exterior if you wish, but the quest will direct you to the entrance of [Blackbone Isle Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto") located right next to the boat. The grotto is similarly filled with undead, and houses a well preserved ship named *[Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread_(place) "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread (place)")*. Fight your way through the ship's undead inhabitants until you reach the captain's quarters on the lower level. Here you will find the *[Captain's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Captain's Journal")* explaining the fate of the ship, as well as [Cyrus' Sabre](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Sabre "Skyrim:Cyrus' Sabre") hanging above the desk. Take the sabre, and loot the chest next to the captain's bed to obtain [Cyrus' Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Clothes "Skyrim:Cyrus' Clothes") and [Cyrus' Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Boots "Skyrim:Cyrus' Boots"). All three of these relics of Cyrus need to be taken to progress the quest.

Attempting to leave the ship with your new items, you will quickly discover that angry [Ghost Sailors](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Sailor "Skyrim:Ghost Sailor") have arisen to defend their final resting place. Fight your way back to the entrance and face the [Ghost Captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Captain "Skyrim:Ghost Captain") out on the deck of the ship. With all the spirits defeated, you can safely make your way back to the boat and leave Blackbone Isle.

### A New Player Home

Although the quest formally concludes after making your escape, you will soon receive a [mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate%27s_Note "Skyrim:Pirate's Note") from a "restless soul" via [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier"), advising you to convert *Dead Man's Dread* into a [player home](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses"). Return to the ship via the boat at Orphan's Tear to complete this objective and claim the island as your own. The ship contains several crafting stations and storage containers, as well as multiple copies of the unique [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") items added by the Creation.

You will also find a map inside the ship that can be used for instant [transport](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#Dead_Man.27s_Dread "Skyrim:Transport") to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). You can also unlock the two other markers on the map to allow travel to [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") (technically [Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")) and [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") by first discovering these locations.

## Notes

- Originally, this quest was automatically added to your journal upon installing the [Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). This was updated with the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), and you are now required to locate the book yourself to begin the quest.
- You will only encounter undead in the exterior areas of Blackbone Isle if you have either the [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") or [Plague of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead") [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed. If you have neither Creation installed, the island will instead be inhabited by six harmless [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit").
- The Ghost Captain and the other spirits will not follow you below deck. This can be exploited by running back inside the ship to heal.
- The skeleton of Kevon is in the same cell as the Crumbling Mortar and can still be used to escape if it has never been used beforehand
- Blackbone Isle has a map marker to fast travel to the location but once there you can only leave either via the rowboat or, after claiming the ship with the Pirate's Note, a map on a table aboard the ship will give an additional option to fast travel to four different ports back on Skyrim.

## Bugs

- If you are arrested, the optional objective won't be marked as complete until you move further away from the door than where you start. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The Restless (ccBGSSSE031\_QUEST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've heard stories of lost shipwrecks strewn across the Sea of Ghosts. If I head to the Winking Skeever in Solitude, I may be able to find more information on there *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* whereabouts. *Objective 10:* Browse books at the Winking Skeever |
| 20 |  | I've heard stories of lost shipwrecks strewn across the Sea of Ghosts. At the Winking Skeever in Solitude, I found a lead on a ship said to have traveled to Blackbone Isle. Apparently, the last person to visit the island died in Castle Dour Dungeon. *Objective 20:* Find the pirate's corpse in Castle Dour Dungeon  *Objective 5:* (Optional) Convince the guard to give you access to the jail cell  *Objective 15:* (Optional) Get arrested and go to jail in Solitude |
| 25 |  | At the Winking Skeever in Solitude, I found a lead on a ship said to have traveled to Blackbone Isle. Apparently, the last person to visit the island died in Castle Dour Dungeon. I found his corpse which hinted at the location of a hidden map. *Objective 25:* Examine the loose brick |
| 30 |  | At the Winking Skeever in Solitude, I found a lead on a ship said to have traveled to Blackbone Isle. Apparently, the last person to visit the island died in Castle Dour Dungeon. I found his corpse and the map he hid under a loose brick. I'll need a boat to travel to the location, perhaps I can find a spare at the wreck near Orphan's Tear. *Objective 30:* Find a spare boat and travel to Blackbone Isle |
| 40 |  | After finding the map to Blackbone Isle, I traveled to the remote location using a boat at Orphan's Tear. *Objective 40:* Investigate Blackbone Isle |
| 43 |  | After finding the map to Blackbone Isle, I traveled to the remote location using a boat at Orphan's Tear. After entering a cave, I found Dead Man's Dread docked inside the grotto. |
| 50 |  | After finding the map to Blackbone Isle, I traveled to the remote location using a boat at Orphan's Tear. After entering a cave, I found Dead Man's Dread docked inside the grotto. Inside the ship were two items of note, Cyrus' Sabre and outfit. *Objective 50:* Escape the grotto |
| 100 | ☑ | After finding the map to Blackbone Isle, I traveled to the remote location using a boat at Orphan's Tear. After entering a cave, I found Dead Man's Dread docked inside the grotto. Inside the ship were two items of note, Cyrus' Sabre and outfit, which were protected by guardians of the ship. I managed to escape the grotto with both items. |
| (ccBGSSSE031\_Blackwater) | | |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the Blackwater Brigand Boss |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Retrieve the Blackwater Blade |
| 30 | ☑ |  |
| Restless Home Quest (ccBGSSSE031\_HomeQuest) | | |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Read the pirate's note |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Claim Dead Man's Dread |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - ccBGSSSE031\_QUEST: 0, 1, 4, 5, 15, 39, 44, 45, 60, 70, 80, 90, 200, 1000
  - ccBGSSSE031\_HomeQuest: 5, 30.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE031_QUEST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE031_QUEST`.

# Skyrim:The Restless

## Overview

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless_(book) "Skyrim:The Restless (book)")* at [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever").
2. Gain access to the cell in [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon") by whatever means necessary and read *[Kevon's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Kevon%27s_Note "Skyrim:Kevon's Note")*. Take the map.
3. Travel to [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear") and find the boat to [Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle").
4. Enter [Blackbone Isle Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto") and take [Cyrus' Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Boots "Skyrim:Cyrus' Boots"), [Cyrus' Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Clothes "Skyrim:Cyrus' Clothes"), and [Cyrus' Sabre](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrus%27_Sabre "Skyrim:Cyrus' Sabre").
5. Fight your way back out to the boat.

### A New Player Home

Although the quest formally concludes after making your escape, you will soon receive a [mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate%27s_Note "Skyrim:Pirate's Note") from a "restless soul" via [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier"), advising you to convert *Dead Man's Dread* into a [player home](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses"). You can also unlock the two other markers on the map to allow travel to [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") (technically [Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")) and [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") by first discovering these locations.

## Notes

- Originally, this quest was automatically added to your journal upon installing the [Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). - Blackbone Isle has a map marker to fast travel to the location but once there you can only leave either via the rowboat or, after claiming the ship with the Pirate's Note, a map on a table aboard the ship will give an additional option to fast travel to four different ports back on Skyrim.

- If you are arrested, the optional objective won't be marked as complete until you move further away from the door than where you start. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The Restless (ccBGSSSE031\_QUEST) | | |

| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE031_QUEST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE031_QUEST`.

# Skyrim:The Retching Netch

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

The Retching Netch

**The Retching Netch** is the cornerclub in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is in the marketplace between [Alor House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House") to the northwest and [Glover Mallory's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House") to the southwest. It is the only inn in Raven Rock, and the only one on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

It is owned and operated by [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri"), who sells [food and drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri#Standard_Merchandise "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") and rents out beds for 10 gold. Its interior includes a [ground floor](#Ground_Floor), the [taproom](#Taproom), and the [private rooms](#Private_Rooms).

The establishment earned its name several years ago, when Geldis saw one of his patrons staggering around the docks with a bottle of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma") while naked and singing loudly. A [netch](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch") floated over the [Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark"), and the naked man threw the bottle at it. The bottle broke on the netch, which began to tilt, then eventually vomited.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") [[a]](#intnote_RNDrovas)  [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)")  [Niyya](/wiki/Skyrim:Niyya "Skyrim:Niyya") [[c]](#intnote_RNNiyya)  [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")[[d]](#intnote_RNRalis)  [Slitter](/wiki/Skyrim:Slitter "Skyrim:Slitter")  [Teldryn Sero](/wiki/Skyrim:Teldryn_Sero "Skyrim:Teldryn Sero") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

## Related Quests

- **[Feeding the Addiction](/wiki/Skyrim:Feeding_the_Addiction "Skyrim:Feeding the Addiction")**: Convince an [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") to let a [drunken miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel") get back to the bar.
- **[It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste")**: Distribute [Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to the citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[My Pet Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Nix-Hound "Skyrim:My Pet Nix-Hound")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Nix-Hound"): Buy a tame [nix-hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_(creature) "Skyrim:Nix-Hound (creature)").
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").
- **[Put A Fork In It](/wiki/Skyrim:Put_A_Fork_In_It "Skyrim:Put A Fork In It")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath"): Pass [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath")'s trial to earn his staff.
- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold")**: Save [Councilor Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn") from an assassination plot.
- **[Speak to Ralis Sedarys at Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_to_Ralis_Sedarys_at_Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Speak to Ralis Sedarys at Kolbjorn Barrow")**: Speak to [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys") at [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow").
- **[Visit the hunters at Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Visit_the_hunters_at_Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Visit the hunters at Frostmoon Crag")**: Talk to the hunters at [Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Frostmoon Crag").

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance are three ash yam urns and two [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants. To the right of the entrance are four more scathecraw plants. A [Redoran guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") is posted outside the entrance, which is unlocked.

#### Ground Floor

Retching Netch ground floor

The entrance leads into the upper floor of the establishment. Near the west wall of this small circular room, mercenary-for-hire [Teldryn Sero](/wiki/Skyrim:Teldryn_Sero "Skyrim:Teldryn Sero") can be found at all hours sitting close to the roaring fireplace and the [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") where the cook [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") works. Along the south wall is a small round table holding a bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), while Teldryn's table holds another bottle of shein and a bottle of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"). Along the north wall around Teldryn's table are four food barrels, with three more bottles of shein atop two more small round tables and an unusable barrel. With the [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, the [Fork of Horripilation](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_of_Horripilation "Skyrim:Fork of Horripilation") and a *[Mysterious Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(Staff_of_Sheogorath) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (Staff of Sheogorath)")* can be found pinned to a keg in this room, surrounded by a green glow. In the middle of the room, stairs lead down to the lower floor.

#### Taproom

Retching Netch taproom

At the bottom of the stairs is the spacious taproom, with numerous small round tables for the regulars, as well as two short corridors to the north and west leading to doors to four private rooms reserved for paying or permanent residents. Near the foot of the stairs are two food barrels and two food urns. In the southeast corner is a food barrel standing next to a stack of barrels, six of which are food barrels. To the south behind the bar is a meat barrel, a food barrel, and a fish barrel, two of which have bottles of shein on top, flanking the entrance to a small storage alcove containing three more food barrels in a stack. In the southwest corner are two huge brewing vats, with two food barrels nearby among the two large kegs by the west corridor. In the northwest corner are two more large kegs, another food barrel, and a set of shelves holding five bottles of shein and copies of all three volumes of *[History of Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock")*. To the north are two food barrels and two tables, with the table by the north corridor holding a bottle of shein. In the northeast corner is another table and a food barrel.

In the middle of the room are two tables, with one holding a bottle each of shein and sujamma, and the other holding a bottle of shein. To the south is the bar, where [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") offers his services and [chats](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri#Conversations "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") with the regulars. Two bottles of sujamma and a bottle of shein sit on the bar, while under the counter is an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") and a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Next to the bar on the floor is an open box containing three bottles of shein and two bottles of sujamma.

#### Private Rooms

Retching Netch room for rent

The west corridor connects to two rooms. The room you can rent is to the south, and is filled with goodies for the paying customer, including two chests containing minor loot, two ingredient urns, a food barrel, a food urn, and a large amount of food. In the northeast corner, the food barrel and an unusable barrel have a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and two [eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") on top. To the right of these barrels and opposite the single bed is a set of shelves holding two baskets containing two bowls of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar"), a wooden bowl containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), two bottles of shein, a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), an [ash yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"), two eidar cheese wheels, a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and a copy of *[The Reclamations](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reclamations "Skyrim:The Reclamations")*. To the right of the set of shelves is a small round table holding another ash yam, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). Lastly, a small table along the south wall holds three ash yams, another sliced goat cheese, and a large coin purse. The small neighboring room to the west belongs to Drovas Relvi, and features his owned single bed, an ash yam urn, an open box containing three more ash yams, and a small round table holding a bottle of sujamma.

The north corridor connects to two rooms. Both rooms are sparsely decorated, and the second room is apprentice-locked. The first room belongs to Geldis Sadri, and features his owned single bed with a chest at its foot, a small round table holding a loaf of bread, an ash yam, and a bottle of shein, and a set of shelves holding two bottles of shein and a copy of the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)")-related tome *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*. The second room belongs to [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)"), and features his owned single bed with a chest at its foot, a small round table holding a loaf of bread and a bottle of shein, and a set of shelves holding another bottle of shein and copies of both volumes of *[The Red Year](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year "Skyrim:The Red Year")*. On the floor outside Mogrul's room is the owned bedroll used by his lackey [Slitter](/wiki/Skyrim:Slitter "Skyrim:Slitter").

## Notes

- The bed you can rent here is the only bed in Solstheim that grants the [Well Rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Rested "Skyrim:Well Rested") bonus.
- Redoran guards may occasionally remark on this inn, stating: *"They serve the best Sujamma I've ever tasted over at the Retching Netch. Worth every coin."*

## Bugs

- The East Empire Company strongbox here can be unlocked with the inn [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Retching_Netch_Key "Skyrim:Retching Netch Key") carried by Geldis.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") is finished and the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") has been cleansed, Drovas's sleep package may still have him trying to sleep at the Retching Netch, even though he won't work here anymore.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:The Rift

## Overview
