| Location | |
| Southeast part of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") | |

The Rift's aspen forests

**The Rift** is a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in southeast [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), with its capital in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It is initially affiliated with the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), but can be captured by the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") after completing [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)") and [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)"). It can also change sides as part of negotiations during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").

The Rift is the southernmost of Skyrim's holds, sitting on a massive plateau in the southeastern corner of the province. The Rift borders both [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), and is separated from the rest of the world by steep cliffs and mountains, including the [Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains"), the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains"), and the legendary [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"). It holds two large lakes as well as autumnal deciduous forests.

In addition to its capital in Riften, the Rift also houses the settlements of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") and [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone").

Map of the Rift

Riften, the hold capital

## Flora and Fauna

The Rift is particularly distinctive for its high number of aspen trees, with white bark and leaves in autumnal hues. For those looking for alchemy ingredients, the Rift contains all variants of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Mountain Flower"), as well as the native [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") and the [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"). The Rift is also the only place to find wild [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") plants.

As for the fauna the most notable is the rich population of [fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Fish "Skyrim:Fish") and [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") in [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich"), which fuel the economy of Riften.

## Places

All locations in the Rift with individual map markers are listed. There are a few places without map markers listed for their significance.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")** — A major city in the southeast of Skyrim near the borders of [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), and the capital of the Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riften)
-  **[Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep")** — A castle located at the southern end of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistveil+Keep)
-  **[Riften Docks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Docks "Skyrim:Riften Docks")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") — An extensive dock located on the western side of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Riften+Docks+%28CC%29)
-  **[Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables")** — A [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") outside the northern entrance to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riften+Stables)
-  **[Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)")** — The headquarters of [the Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") located with the sewers beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), known as [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Thieves+Guild)

### Farms, Towns, and Settlements including Orc Strongholds and Inns

-  **[Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alchemist%27s+Shack)
-  **[Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge")** — A large remote building east of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Black-Briar+Lodge)
-  **[Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") southeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Froki%27s+Shack)
-  **[Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate")** — A [honey farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercenary_(Goldenglow) "Skyrim:Mercenary (Goldenglow)"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the farm's owner [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Goldenglow+Estate)
-  **[Heartwood Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Heartwood_Mill "Skyrim:Heartwood Mill")** — A struggling lumber mill on the shores of [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich"), west of [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Heartwood+Mill)
-  **[Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead")** — A milling [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in the western Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ivarstead)
-  **[Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur")** — An accursed [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") beset by [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") in the southeast of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), west-southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Largashbur)
-  **[Merryfair Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Merryfair_Farm "Skyrim:Merryfair Farm")** — A poor, small farm northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), owned and run by [Dravin Llanith](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin_Llanith "Skyrim:Dravin Llanith") and his wife [Synda Llanith](/wiki/Skyrim:Synda_Llanith "Skyrim:Synda Llanith"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Merryfair+Farm)
-  **[Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm")** — A farm east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") that cultivates [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sarethi+Farm)
-  **[Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone")** — A mining [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in the northern Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shor%27s+Stone)
-  **[Snow-Shod Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Farm "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Farm")** — A small farm south of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") that is owned by [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snow-Shod+Farm)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Last Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Vigil "Skyrim:Last Vigil")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") northeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Last+Vigil+%28DB%29)
-  **[Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in the Rift, located south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") and west of the [Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Rift Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in the Rift, located northeast of [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm") and west of [Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Stormcloak+Camp)

### Caves

-  **[Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Boulderfall+Cave)
-  **[Broken Helm Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") in the southeast corner of The Rift containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Helm+Hollow)
-  **[Clearspring Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Cave "Skyrim:Clearspring Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing a [troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearspring+Cave)
-  **[Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Crystaldrift+Cave)
-  **[Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southwest of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+Pass)
-  **[Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fallowstone+Cave)
-  **[Gromm's Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Gromm%27s_Pass "Skyrim:Gromm's Pass")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") located in the Rift, south of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gromm%27s+Pass+%28CC%29)
-  **[Honeystrand Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeystrand_Cave "Skyrim:Honeystrand Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Honeystrand+Cave)
-  **[Nightingale Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Hall "Skyrim:Nightingale Hall")** — The home of the [Nightingales](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales "Skyrim:Nightingales") between Riften and [the Shadow Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shadow_Stone "Skyrim:The Shadow Stone"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nightingale+Hall)
-  **[Pinepeak Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinepeak_Cavern "Skyrim:Pinepeak Cavern")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinepeak+Cavern)
-  **[Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redwater+Den+%28DG%29)
-  **[Ruunvald Excavation](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Excavation "Skyrim:Ruunvald Excavation")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [Vigilants](/wiki/Skyrim:Charmed_Vigilant "Skyrim:Charmed Vigilant") charmed by the conjurer [Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne "Skyrim:Minorne"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruunvald+Excavation+%28DG%29)
-  **[Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave")** — A large [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tolvald%27s+Cave)

### Dragon Lairs

-  **[Autumnwatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnwatch_Tower "Skyrim:Autumnwatch Tower")** — A [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnwatch+Tower)
-  **[Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook")** — A [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Tongue+Overlook)
-  **[Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit")** — A mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") northwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Summit)

### Mines

-  **[Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine")** — A small [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") east-northeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Prospect+Mine)
-  **[Northwind Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Mine "Skyrim:Northwind Mine")** — A small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") northwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Mine)
- **[Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine")** — A small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in western [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") initially containing [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redbelly+Mine)

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic

-  **[Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angarvunde)
-  **[Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point")** — A small outdoor [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and, after [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arcwind+Point)
-  **[Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel")** — A medium-sized [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Avanchnzel)
-  **[Champion's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Champion's Rest")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra "Skyrim:Umbra") — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") located in the Rift, east of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Champion%27s+Rest+%28CC%29)
-  **[Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dragon Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cultist "Skyrim:Dragon Cultist"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forelhost)
-  **[Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the draugr [Sigdis Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigdis_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Sigdis Gauldurson"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Geirmund%27s+Hall)
-  **[Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shroud+Hearth+Barrow)

### Standing Stones and Daedric Shrines

-  **[The Shadow Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shadow_Stone "Skyrim:The Shadow Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim, [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Shadow+Stone)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darklight+Tower)
-  **[Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Faldar%27s+Tooth)
-  **[Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") which serves as the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)")'s base of operations. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dawnguard+%28DG%29)
-  **[Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall")** — A large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north-northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Greenwall)
-  **[Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") east-northeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") disguised as guards. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nilheim)
-  **[Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower")** — A small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Watchtower)
-  **[Shor's Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Watchtower "Skyrim:Shor's Watchtower")** — A small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") north-northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shor%27s+Watchtower)
-  **[Stendarr's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Stendarr's Beacon")** — A small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stendarr%27s+Beacon)
-  **[Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Treva%27s+Watch)

### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

The Velothi Mountains viewed from Stendarr's Beacon

-  **[Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing")** — A circular glade inhabited by a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") and its attending [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnshade+Clearing)
-  **[Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn")** — A small mountain pool on the cliff overlooking [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), due east of [Snapleg Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Snapleg_Cave "Skyrim:Snapleg Cave") and west of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearspring+Tarn)
- **[Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River")** — A river connecting [Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir") to the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+River)
-  **[Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove")** — A grove accessed through [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave") containing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") whose tribe has defiled a shrine of [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Grove)
- **[Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the southern border of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jerall+Mountains)
- **[Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir")** — A lake in the western Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Geir)
- **[Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich")** — A lake in the eastern Rift, immediately southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Honrich)
-  **[Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Bthalft)
-  **[Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in the mountains southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing a [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother") and [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Rkund)
- **[Treva River](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva_River "Skyrim:Treva River")** — A river in the center of the Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Treva+River)
- **[Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the eastern border of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Velothi+Mountains)

### Unmarked Places

- There are three [Dragon Mounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") in the Rift.
  - Northeast of [Autumnwatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnwatch_Tower "Skyrim:Autumnwatch Tower").
  - West of [Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing").
  - North of [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook").
- There are two [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") in the Rift.
  - A [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") southwest of [Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack").
  - A [Shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar") west of [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave").

## The Rift Quests

Quests that are started in or related to the Rift (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").
- **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").

### Imperial Legion Civil War Quests

- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)")**: Take [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Daedric Quests

- **[The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")**: Help lift the curse placed on the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") by [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").
- **[Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi")**: Kill a hapless [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi") in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").

### Thieves Guild

- All [primary quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") except for [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers"), as well as the special jobs, either originate or terminate here.

### Side Quests including Divine Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").
- **[Infiltration](/wiki/Skyrim:Infiltration "Skyrim:Infiltration")**: Help [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") take back [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch").
- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").
- **[Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")**: Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").
- **[Repentance](/wiki/Skyrim:Repentance "Skyrim:Repentance")**: Help [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") prevent her mother [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") from transforming into a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").
- **[A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots")**: Go where a [famous alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") could not in order to aid ground-breaking research.
- **[Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult")**: Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") to recover his mask for [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir").
- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

### Dawnguard Quests

- Dawnguard Main Questline
  - **[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Speak with the leader of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").
  - **[Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find out what the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan") are looking for.
  - **[Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Choose your side!
  - **[Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
  - **[Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Explore [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar").
  - **[Unseen Visions](/wiki/Skyrim:Unseen_Visions "Skyrim:Unseen Visions")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Perform a ceremony to read the Elder Scroll.

- Dawnguard Side Quests (all start here, several take place exclusively in the Rift)
  - **[Ancient Technology](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Technology "Skyrim:Ancient Technology")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Retrieve Dwemer schematics to improve technology for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Bolstering the Ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") and recruit him into the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").
  - **[Cleansing Light](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_Light "Skyrim:Cleansing Light")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the boss of a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") lair. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Destroying the Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroying_the_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Destroying the Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") leaders.
  - **[Hide and Seek](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(quest) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (quest)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") masquerading as a citizen. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Rescue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue "Skyrim:Rescue")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Rescue a victim from [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- **[A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Seek out a cursed Tsaesci blade in the Ratway.
- **[Vile Whispers](/wiki/Skyrim:Vile_Whispers "Skyrim:Vile Whispers")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra "Skyrim:Umbra"): A [malevolent Daedric entity](/wiki/Lore:Umbra "Lore:Umbra") long thought destroyed has resurfaced in the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains").

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests are located in the Rift. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#The_Rift "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

## Notes

- The Rift also [appears](/wiki/Online:The_Rift "Online:The Rift") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").
- Unlike in most other Holds, a good number of residents in the settlements here have leveled weapons instead of fixed ones.

## Bugs

- Although Fort Dawnguard is located here, crimes committed there may earn you a bounty in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") instead. **?**

# Skyrim:The Rising Dead

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **A group of [Necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") plan to summon an army of [zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Zombie "Skyrim:Zombie").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Anonymous Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Anonymous_Letter_(Plague_of_the_Dead) "Skyrim:Anonymous Letter (Plague of the Dead)") |
| Location(s): | Ritual site north of [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=31270&y=-99871&zoom=17&legacy=true) |
| Reward: | [*Spell Tome: Conjure Zombie*](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Zombie"), [*Spell Tome: Conjure Foul Zombie*](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Foul_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Foul Zombie") (level 11+) |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE003\_ZombieQuestStartEncounter |
| Required Level: | 5 |
| Suggested Level: | 11 |
| Added by: | [Plague of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead") |

An ancient evil has been summoned to Skyrim

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Reach level 5 and read the [anonymous letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Anonymous_Letter_(Plague_of_the_Dead) "Skyrim:Anonymous Letter (Plague of the Dead)").
2. Travel to the ritual site north of [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum").
3. Find and read the [*Necromancer's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Journal_(Plague_of_the_Dead) "Skyrim:Necromancer's Journal (Plague of the Dead)") to complete the quest.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The Ritual Site

After reaching level 5, a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will approach you and deliver an [anonymous letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Anonymous_Letter_(Plague_of_the_Dead) "Skyrim:Anonymous Letter (Plague of the Dead)"). Read the letter to learn that a group of [Necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") plan to perform an ancient, dangerous summoning ritual to conjure an army of [zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Zombie "Skyrim:Zombie"). The ritual site is located high in the mountains southeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), just north of [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=31270&y=-99871&zoom=17&legacy=true).

Once you arrive at the ritual site, you will find a group of decomposing zombies standing over the bodies of the slain Necromancers. Clearly the ritual was successful, but the Necromancers lost control of their summoned undead. Defeat the zombies and approach the body of the Necromancer marked by the quest marker. He will be holding a leveled spell tome ([*Spell Tome: Conjure Zombie*](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Zombie") for lower levels, or [*Spell Tome: Conjure Foul Zombie*](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Foul_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Foul Zombie") for levels 11+) as well as a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Journal_(Plague_of_the_Dead) "Skyrim:Necromancer's Journal (Plague of the Dead)"). Read the journal to complete the quest and learn of the consequences of the ritual. You can also loot the area for two additional copies of *Spell Tome: Conjure Zombie*.

Following the conclusion of the quest, you will have a chance to encounter [zombie horde](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Zombie_Attack "Skyrim:World Interactions") world interactions randomly in the wilderness.

## Notes

- At release, this quest had no level requirement and the anonymous letter would be automatically added to your inventory upon installation. This was changed in [Patch 1.6](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch#Version_1.6 "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch") with the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition").
- The unmarked location "[The Headless Skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Falkreath#The_Headless_Skeleton "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Falkreath")" can also be found here, with it being next to the pine tree.

## Quest Stages

| The Rising Dead (ccBGSSSE003\_ZombieQuestStartEncounter) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've found an urgent anonymous letter. I should read it and see what it's regarding. *Objective :* Read the Anonymous Letter |
| 20 |  | I've received an anonymous letter asking me to help stop a group of Necromancers who are planning to raise an army of Zombies. I should investigate the ritual site. *Objective :* Investigate the Ritual Site |
| 30 |  | Read the Necromancer's Journal *Objective :* Read the Necromancer's Journal |
| 40 | ☑ | I found the Necromancer's ritual site, but it's too late. I also found a journal detailing what transpired here. They appear to have already conjured the risen dead, possibly across all of Skyrim. I'll need to be vigilant, especially during the late night hours. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE003_ZombieQuestStartEncounter stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE003_ZombieQuestStartEncounter`.

# Skyrim:The Ritual Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

The Ritual Stone

**The Ritual Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim, located east of Whiterun. It is located to the east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") by the roadside, above the entrance to [Graywinter Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Graywinter_Watch "Skyrim:Graywinter Watch").

*"Once a day, those under the sign of The Ritual can reanimate nearby corpses to fight for them."*

Activating the Ritual Stone grants you [the power](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers#The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:Powers") to [raise corpses](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate") to fight for you for about one hour of in-game time. The power also allows you to raise some corpses that can usually not be reanimated, such as [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") or [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). Horses cannot be raised with the Ritual Stone power. Bodies raised by the Ritual Stone do not turn to ash after the effect expires and there is no limit to the number of corpses you can reanimate.

## The Ritual Stone

.jpg)

The Ritual Stone, when activated

The stone is on a rock outcrop between the road leading east from [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"). A path leads from the road, around the outcrop as it climbs and passes under several squared off arches. At the top is a hostile, leveled [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") who will attack as soon as they are aware of you. They are standing beside the standing stone and will raise two [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") to help them with the fight, one of these is an archer and the other uses a one-handed [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). A circle of candles surrounds the stone and a few paces to the southeast is a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower").

## Notes

- If you reanimate a corpse and make it follow you to a location with more corpses (or NPCs that you can kill), you can end up with a large number of reanimated followers.
- The Ritual Stone power spreads out in a sphere several feet wide around the player when cast, reanimating any npcs or creatures within its radius.
- The Ritual Stone power works on corpses up to level 75. This limit can be increased using the [Necromage](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromage_(perk) "Skyrim:Necromage (perk)") perk.
- Placing the Ritual Stone power inside the [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") allows you multiple castings by removing and equipping the crown. This can be used to build potentially unlimited armies of undead.
- While the Ritual Stone power is active, the number of summons or raised creatures the player may have at a moment is temporarily increased by 100.
- The Ritual Stone power can be useful for accessing corpses that have fallen out of bounds.
- The Ritual Stone power can be useful for bringing additional followers into the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").
- With the [Necromantic Grimoire](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromantic_Grimoire "Skyrim:Necromantic Grimoire") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, you can find a [Conjure Undying Ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Undying_Ghost "Skyrim:Conjure Undying Ghost") spell tome lying on a rock next to the stone.

# Skyrim:The Sanctuary and the Manufactory

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). | [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Repair a Dwarven ruin and make yourself at home.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | *[Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts%27_Journal,_v1 "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v1")*, [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"), [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") |
| Location(s): | [Frostroot Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostroot_Cave "Skyrim:Frostroot Cave"), [Nchuanthumz](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz") |
| Reward: | New player house |
| ID: | ccAARSSE001ManufactoryControlQuest |
| Added by: | [Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz:_Dwarven_Home "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. To start this quest head to the Frozen Hearth inn within Winterhold.
2. Go inside and into one of the rooms to find [Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts%27_Journal,_v1 "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v1").
3. Head to the [Frostroot Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostroot_Cave "Skyrim:Frostroot Cave") and find the [Nchuanthumz](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz") entrance.
4. Access Nchuanthumz's Manufactory
5. Find the Argonian [Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts")'s body near a control panel. Examine the corpse for clues.
6. Read [Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts%27_Journal,_v2 "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v2").
7. Use one of the two buttons to activate the Dwarven Sphere Overseer.
8. Collect 3 Dwemer Cogs, 3 Dwemer Actuators and a Dwemer Oil.
9. Return to the Dwarven Sphere Overseer and bring the manufactory back online.
10. Collect a Centurion Dynamo Core and use it to construct a Dwarven Spider Renovator.
11. Summon the Dwarven Spider Renovator to clean a section of the house.
12. Wait 24 hours for the renovations to finish. A few rooms will be fully renovated and furnished.
13. Repeat this 2 more times to fully renovate the home.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Go to [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts%27_Journal,_v1 "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v1") is on a table in the left room when facing to the innkeeper, read it to start the quest. Quest maker will direct to [Frostroot Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostroot_Cave "Skyrim:Frostroot Cave"). Head to and enter the cave, fight three bandits and walk along a short way to Nchuanthumz.

Once you enter [Nchuanthumz](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz"), head straight and deal with a few skeevers and three bandits until you reach the lift to Nchuanthumz's Manufactory. Use the lift and then continue straight forward until you reach the corpse of [Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts"), examine the body to find a [Dwemer Actuator](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Actuator "Skyrim:Dwemer Actuator") and his [second journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts%27_Journal,_v2 "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v2").

The journal lists the items required to repair the assembly lines, with the required items being one [Dwarven oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Oil "Skyrim:Dwarven Oil"), three [Dwemer cogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog"), and three Dwemer Actuators. The room already contains everything you need. You should already have one Dwemer Actuator from Artifacts' own inventory; the other two are on the two tables on either side of the room, alongside the cogs and the oil. Collect all the required items and activate the Dwarven Sphere Overseer button. The quest markers will direct you to press either the right or left button to do so.

The Dwarven Sphere Overseer will emerge from the scuttle on the right side of the room. Follow the Dwarven Sphere Overseer and give it the repair parts by interacting with it. You can then activate the manufactory; if you already have a [Centurion Dynamo Core](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core") then you can head straight to the room on the left, however if you don't have one, go to the room on the west side of the manufactory to find a destroyed Dwarven Centurion Master, whose body has a core on it.

Place the Centurion Dynamo Core into the Dynamo Actuator and then activate the button next to it. This will build a Dwarven Spider Renovator, head back to the lift and go back up to Nchuanthumz. There are three sections of the house to clear with the spider, each takes 24 hours once the spider is summoned using one of the levers. Once all three sections are complete, the quest will finish and you will have a fully furnished Dwarven house.

# Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [75.84.209.125](/wiki/Special:Contributions/75.84.209.125 "Special:Contributions/75.84.209.125"), checked by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help a necromancer escape from [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:Selveni Nethri") |
| Location(s): | [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | dunSouthfringeQST |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

*"Please, cut me down!"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find [Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:Selveni Nethri") trapped in webs in [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") and cut her down.
2. Help her escape the cave.

### Caught in a Web

When exploring [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") you will find a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") named [Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:Selveni Nethri") trapped in a spider's web. Obviously she is frantic to escape and pleads with you to cut her down.

### A Cursed Necromancer

Apparently Selveni's dealings as a necromancer resulted in her daughter being taken from her and sent to the [orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Selveni had gone to Riften to see if she could get her daughter out, but learned her daughter had already been moved. When she returned to the coven, [Bashnag](/wiki/Skyrim:Bashnag "Skyrim:Bashnag") accused her of trying to sell him out to the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). She was cursed and chased off. Because of the curse she has been weakened and can't cast a spell to save her life. She isn't able to escape the Sanctum until the way out is safe, and she is desperate to locate her missing daughter.

### Clear the Way

You have probably already faced the many resident [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") on your way in. While it isn't necessary to kill Bashnag and all his fellow [spellswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)") to ensure her safety, the quest will fail if Selveni dies before escaping. Let her know when the way out is clear. She will thank you and move along the path in the spider area to get out of the cave by herself. When she has exited the cave, the quest will be completed. There is no follow-up to this quest, as Selveni's daughter does not appear anywhere in Skyrim and Selveni herself disappears for good once she is out of your sight.

## Notes

- There are numerous internal references that show many changes to this quest. Originally, it took place in [Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave") (which is also referred to as Boulderfall *Pass*), and Selveni was to be a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf"), rather than a necromancer.
  - An unused message internally known as `dunSouthfringeQuestObjective` also refers to this, it reads: *"Help Selvani*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Nethri escape Boulderfall Pass."* The name of this particular message "**Pack Animals**", might've originally been the name of the quest (as it isn't actually named in the final game's files), and seemingly referred to Selveni's lycanthropy.

## Bugs

- She may refuse to move after being cut down.
  - Try talking to her until she moves. This might continue past any meaningful conversation, but she should eventually move.
- In many cases, Selveni can get stuck near the entrance. Some things that can be tried to unstick her are:
  - Talk to her.
  - Use your equipment, spell, or shout to get her unstuck, such as [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), a [Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralyze_(effect) "Skyrim:Paralyze (effect)") spell, or blocks.
  - Use the wait feature for one hour.
  - Leaving and reentering the location may also work. In that case, she will disappear from the cave, and the journal will update the quest as completed. You may be forced to go back to [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") after a long time roaming other places to solve this quest with this method, though.
  - Hitting her with an arrow may also help push her towards the entrance. However, do not use a powerful bow and arrow combination or you will risk killing her.
- Selveni may even escape but the quest journal indicates that it never completed.
- This quest is set up as a Miscellaneous quest but increments the Side Quests achievement when it isn't supposed to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunSouthfringeQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunSouthfringeQST`.

# Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer

## Overview

The Scorched Hammer

**The Scorched Hammer** is the home of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")'s blacksmith, [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") and his adopted son [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer"), who he has been training in [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"). If anything happens to Balimund, Asbjorn will take over running the shop. Otherwise, Asbjorn spends most of his time inside the Scorched Hammer.

Balimund

It is located to the west of the main market place, between the canal below and the exit to the docks.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Smithing (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Smithing (Expert)") (Blacksmith)  [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") (Apprentice) |

## Related Quests

- **[Stoking the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoking_the_Flames "Skyrim:Stoking the Flames")**: Find 10 [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") to restore [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund")'s forge.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

To the right of the entrance, outside the building is a [blacksmith's forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") and [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") claims that his forge is unique because he fuels it with [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") (although [his supply is low](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoking_the_Flames "Skyrim:Stoking the Flames")). However, items created at his forge do not have any special properties. Balimund spends most of the day working at the forge, but does frequently take a lunch break inside his house, but also works quite late in the evening.

### The Scorched Hammer

Balimund's home

The first room you enter has a fireplace against the south wall, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and two chairs pulled up close to the fire. This is where [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer") spends most of his days, unless Balimund has died in which case he takes over the running of the forge and shop outside. To the left of the fireplace is a small square wooden table, which holds two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Quite_Pleased "Skyrim:Quite Pleased") from [Harrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrald "Skyrim:Harrald") stating that he's convinced everyone in the [keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") and guard to use Balimund's services for any blacksmithing required. There are two chairs at the table and hanging above from the ceiling are two garlic braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). In the southwest corner, to the right of the fireplace are three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood").

The doorway to the west enters a corridor with a flight of stairs down to the cellar on the right and two doors one to the south and the other opposite to the north. The door to the south leads to [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer")'s bedroom which consists of a single owned bed in the northeast, with an end table holding a copy of *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")* beside it, a wall shelf holding a bottle of alto wine above and a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") against the west wall.

The door to the north opens into [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund")'s bedroom and consists of a dresser holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") right by the door, with a safe with a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Armorer's Challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Armorer%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:The Armorer's Challenge")* on the floor between the safe and dresser and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top of the safe. There is also a wall shelf above the dresser holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe with a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword") on top and around the corner against the east wall is an unowned single bed, with a chair beside it.

There is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel by the top of the stairs down to the cellar. At the bottom of the stairs, on the left are several food barrels and a few bales of straw. Under the stairs is a pile of firewood. To the south is a doorway to a storage area with a grindstone in front of you and behind that two wall shelves holding fifteen [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), four [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot") and two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"). To the right of these are a set of shelves holding two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), four leather strips and three pieces of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather"). Against the west wall, by the shelves is a tanning rack and in an alcove to the right is a long wooden table and chair. On the table is the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), a bottle of wine, a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two leather strips and an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"). To the east is a food storeroom containing two food barrels, a basket of [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and cabbages, a cupboard holding clutter and a set of shelves holding several potatoes, a cabbage, a couple of loaves of bread and several pieces of cheese. Hanging from the ceiling are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a garlic braid, two bunches of elves ear and a bunch of frost mirriam.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the blacksmith's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| 1 | Complete leveled set of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") (unmatched, unenchanted; [Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Armor "Skyrim:Glass Armor") is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (one of each type incl. [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") except [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"); unenchanted; Ebony is best possible) |  |

## Notes

- Completing Balimund's quest [Stoking the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoking_the_Flames "Skyrim:Stoking the Flames") allows you to freely take all low-valued items in the building and to sleep in Balimund's bed, but not Asbjorn's.
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the entrance door.

The Sea Squall

**The Sea Squall** is a ship docked in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar")'s Northstar Port.

## Residents

| Crew |
| --- |
| [Captain Wayfinder](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder")  [Guthrum](/wiki/Skyrim:Guthrum "Skyrim:Guthrum")  [Ravam Verethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravam_Verethi "Skyrim:Ravam Verethi") |

## Related Quests

- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## The Sea Squall

The boat is docked at the end of a jetty opposite the entrance to [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine"). There are several crates and barrels on deck, along with three chairs that the captain and both sailors seem to spend most of their time sitting on.

## Notes

- Dawnstar guards can be seen traversing between the ship and the mine entrance.
-  Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") adds 3 bedrolls to the ship.

# Skyrim:The Serpent Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Serpent Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Serpent+Stone)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Serpentstone_Isle "Lore:Serpentstone Isle")) | | |

| Region | |

The Serpent Stone

**The Serpent Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim.

While the stone is active, the player can use a ranged attack that will [paralyze](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralyze_(effect) "Skyrim:Paralyze (effect)") a target for 5 seconds and also do 25 points of damage. Activating the stone will present the message:

"*Once a day, those under the sign of the Serpent can use a ranged paralyzing poison on opponents.*"

## Related Quests

- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.

## The Serpent Stone

The stone is on **Serpentstone Isle**, directly east of [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and northeast of [Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_The_Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos"). It is guarded by an [ice wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"). The island is fairly empty, apart from a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on the southeastern shore, a couple of [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") plants on the northern shore, and the occasional [snow fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox "Skyrim:Snow Fox"). There are routes up from both the eastern and northern shores, to a square arch atop a short flight of stairs, with the stone standing beyond.

## Gallery

- .jpg)

  The Serpent Stone, when activated
- 

  Serpentstone Isle

## Notes

- A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") can be found along the eastern shore.

# Skyrim:The Shadow Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Shadow Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Shadow+Stone)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") or [Necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DoomstoneFallForest01 | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| South of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") East of [Snow-Shod Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Farm "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Farm") | |

The Shadow Stone

**The Shadow Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim, and is located south of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), east of [Snow-Shod Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Farm "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Farm"), near [Nightingale Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Hall "Skyrim:Nightingale Hall").

.jpg)

The Shadow Stone, when activated

## The Shadow Stone

***Once a day, those under the sign of The Shadow can become [invisible](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(effect) "Skyrim:Invisibility (effect)") for an extended period.***

When nearing the stone care should be taken, as there is a [respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") high leveled [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") or [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") lurking by the stone. As soon as you are detected, they will warn you off, if you don't immediately leave they will attack you. They may be accompanied by multiple hostile [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") who will all attack as soon as you are detected. The stone itself is surrounded by a further nine standing stones that were carved, but show no markings. A few paces to the east, by a fallen piece of masonry is a lootable skeleton with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") laying on the ground beside it.

The power the stone confers is unique in that the [invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(effect) "Skyrim:Invisibility (effect)") effect takes place instantly, instead of having to cast it like you would with an [Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(spell) "Skyrim:Invisibility (spell)") spell, this lack of delay could save you in a tight spot.

## Notes

- The power granted by the Shadow Stone lasts 60 seconds or until canceled.

# Skyrim:The Shill Job

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Place an item as evidence inside a wealthy home.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRDU |

*"Get in, plant the goods and get out. Quiet and neat."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about shill jobs and receive the evidence.
2. Enter the house and put the item into the targeted chest.
3. Report back to Vex for your reward.

### A View to a Shill

After you are a full member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), you will want to start thieving for fun and profit. By now, you will have met [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex"). She handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), shill, [sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sweep_Job "Skyrim:The Sweep Job") and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. In order to earn some gold and help Vex with her goal of restoring the Guild to its former glory, ask her for a shill job. She will inform you that a client has requested someone be taken out. Unlike the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), the guild does this by planting evidence in their home and tipping off the guard.

### The Plant

Vex will give you a stolen item that needs to be placed as evidence. The item is a randomly-selected [gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") or unenchanted piece of [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry") ([circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Circlet "Skyrim:Circlet"), [necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace "Skyrim:Necklace"), or [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring "Skyrim:Ring")); see [Leveled Lists](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Thieves_Guild_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") for full details. The item is identical to a standard item, except that "Stolen" has been added to its name.

The quest can send you to any wealthy house, which amounts to twenty-nine possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |

House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead
