House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You need to enter the selected house undetected and find the designated chest. Open the chest and place the stolen item in it. Although there may be multiple containers in the house, only the chest indicated by your quest marker will work; if you attempt to put the stolen item into the wrong container, you will be told that you can't remove the item from your inventory. If you are sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, you will fail the quest. Getting caught in the house or killing anyone living in the house will also result in failing the quest. You are not responsible for tipping off the guards after placing the evidence.

Once you have planted the evidence, return to Vex for a leveled gold reward.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- Even if you complete the job successfully, there are no obvious repercussions for the person you have framed. They do not go to jail or otherwise become inaccessible.
- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- Despite the Stolen indication in the item's name, the item given to you will not be flagged as stolen.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun, namely [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") and [Severio Pelagia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Severio_Pelagia%27s_House "Skyrim:Severio Pelagia's House"). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
-  The chest you must plant the Stolen Flawless Ruby in Uthgerd's home may already contain a Flawless Ruby. If you steal the contents before planting the Stolen Flawless Ruby and already have a stolen flawless ruby in your inventory, it does not register that you have planted the one given to you by Vex. Placing the ruby in the chest that is labeled Stolen Flawless Ruby does nothing in regards to completing the quest objective, and taking it back out simply adds it to your already existing inventory of flawless rubies. If you autosave on travel, just reload the Uthgerd's House save and place your current flawless ruby inventory into another container or drop on the ground.
- The "stolen item" might disappear from your inventory for no obvious reasons and you'll be unable to complete the quest.
  - To fix this, use `setstage tgrdu 10` in the console and it will take the quest back to the stage that Vex gave your character the item.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish). This will give you a different item as evidence.
  - The item disappearing may be due to the item being a gem, and the stolen gem being used to smith a piece of jewelry.
- These quests don't remove the planted evidence from the target chest when you finish them.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Shill Job (TGRDU) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Plant the <Alias=Evidence> in <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> |
| 20 |  | I've been told to plant the <Alias=Evidence> in <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City>. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. |
|  | I've planted the <Alias=Evidence> in <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City>. |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Vex |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRDU stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRDU`.

# Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Meet [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre") inside [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") and learn who he wants assassinated.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") |
| Location(s): | [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | DB04a |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark"), and then after completing that quest kill the target of [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Kill Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild"), [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius"), [Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern") and/or [Kill Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk") | **Next →** [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") | | |

[Rexus](/wiki/Skyrim:Rexus "Skyrim:Rexus") hands over an Amulet

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Meet [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre") inside [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud").
2. Take his letter and amulet to Astrid.
3. Take the amulet to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory").
4. Return to Astrid with the [letter of credit](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_of_Credit "Skyrim:Letter of Credit").

### The Prodigal Returns

When you last left the Dark Brotherhood sanctuary, Astrid was still in turmoil regarding your sudden promotion to Listener, and the ensuing duties the role required. Once you have fulfilled any of the contracts [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") gave you after completing [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark") ([Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild"), [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius"), [Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern"), [Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk")), go back to the sanctuary. Astrid will approach you and tell you that she has finished thinking. She agrees that it would be madness to just ignore the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")'s demands and tells you to travel to Volunruud to meet with [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre").

### The Stars Aligned

When you enter Volunruud, a skeleton sits in a small alcove immediately to your left. It will attack you as you pass, so conduct a preemptive strike while it slumbers, or sneak past it. Near the skeleton are [Heddic's Volunruud notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Heddic%27s_Volunruud_Notes "Skyrim:Heddic's Volunruud Notes"); reading them will start [Volunruud's dungeon quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Silenced_Tongues "Skyrim:Silenced Tongues"). Completing the quest gives you a word of [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper"), a useful [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") for assassins, but the quest is not necessary to meet Motierre.
After the skeleton, the first room is straight ahead. There are three paths, but the one you want is the leftmost one. Open the door and you'll find the client waiting with [Rexus](/wiki/Skyrim:Rexus "Skyrim:Rexus"), his bodyguard. Motierre will be impressed and a bit unnerved that you have arrived. He informs you that he has multiple targets in mind, all culminating in a shocking end--the assassination of the Emperor. The bodyguard will then give you two items: a valuable [jeweled amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Amulet "Skyrim:Jeweled Amulet") "to cover expenses" and a [sealed letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre%27s_Sealed_Letter "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre's Sealed Letter") with further instructions to deliver to Astrid. Return to the sanctuary and deliver these items to Astrid.

### Back at the Sanctuary

When you return, Astrid is anxious to know the goings-on. When you tell her of Motierre's grand design, she will be excited by the prospect of such glory for the Brotherhood and starts with preparations. She wants to study the letter further, but in the meantime, asks you to take the amulet to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), a [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") member located at the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") in the Ratway in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). She wants the amulet appraised and sold, if Mallory is interested.

### The Wheels in Motion

Upon inspecting the amulet, Mallory will inform you that it is a one-of-a-kind item and is only given to members of the [Elder Council](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Council "Lore:Elder Council"). He agrees to purchase it and hands you a [letter of credit](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_of_Credit "Skyrim:Letter of Credit"), which is to be delivered to Astrid—as per their "standard arrangement".

Return to Astrid with the letter. When you explain what Mallory told you about the amulet she will be delighted, musing that Motierre is probably a member of the Elder Council looking to get himself promoted. With that, she is all smiles and action; she informs you that the first step to completing the new directive will be for you to [attend a wedding](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") and assassinate [the bride](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici").

## Notes

- If you read the letter Amaund Motierre gives you inside Volunruud before delivering it to Astrid, she will mention it in conversation after showing it to her, criticizing your actions as "sloppy". This has no effect on the quest other than the additional dialogue.
- You can directly go to Volunruud rather than speaking to Astrid first, but the quest won't start until she talks to you.
- There is a chest in Amaund's chamber within the ruins which is free to loot, containing some leveled valuables and gold.
- If you go to Amaund before getting the quest, the quest will not be altered. If you return to the Sanctuary, Astrid will simply tell you to go to Volunruud before ending the conversation.
- Asking Astrid for more details on the wedding murder will have her speaking like the civil war is still ongoing, even if you've already completed that questline.
- If you are a member of the Thieves Guild when you take the amulet to Mallory, he will ask if the assistance you need is for the guild, prompting you to say it is for the Dark Brotherhood instead.

## Quest Stages

# Skyrim:The Silver Hand

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). | |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor"), one [radiant quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions") | | → Next | [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor") | | |

The meeting in the Underforge

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor").
2. Meet with Skjor at night.
3. Enter the [Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge").
4. Participate in the blood ritual.
5. Talk to [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress").
6. Kill the [werewolf hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").

### A Secret Meeting

After completing another set of radiant quests, the usual job providers will once again point you towards [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor"). Aela will say:
*"Still eager to please. This is good. Skjor may be right about you. He has something special planned for you. Better talk to him."*, while Farkas will say: *"Skjor was looking for you before. Talk to him before doing anything else."*

Skjor turns out to be less talkative than usual and will request a meeting after dark near the Underforge, a secret crypt underneath the smithy of [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"). At night, Skjor will wait for you near the secret entrance, determined to make you a [stronger member](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") of the Companions. He will then open the secret entrance and encourage you to follow.

Inside the Underforge, you will encounter [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") in her lycanthropic form, standing next to an empty fountain. Skjor will introduce her as your 'forebear', and will inform you that this is to be kept secret from Harbinger [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane"), and will then ask if you are prepared. When you are ready, Skjor will cut open Aela's wrist, filling the fountain with her blood. Activate the fountain and receive the [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form") power, which causes you to black out.

### Rampage

You wake up outside the Underforge, now as a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"), where you will find all of Whiterun's residents are now hostile to you. If you head into the streets, citizens will flee and guards will attack you, leaving you no choice but to avoid them or kill them. Due to your beastly appearance, you will not gain a bounty for assaulting anyone. After a certain amount of time, you will black out once again.

The easiest way to avoid unwanted casualties is to simply wait a while after exiting the Underforge, as this causes your werewolf bloodlust to wear off, and the next scene to continue.

Another option is to go back into the Underforge as soon as you've transformed, and use the secret exit that leads you out of the city.

You can also simply avoid any attackers if you do not wish to kill any people in the city, you'll black out regardless of whether you killed anyone or not.

### The Silver Hand

This time, you wake up in the middle of nowhere, with a concerned Aela looking over you. Your gear has been unequipped, but you haven't lost anything; simply re-equip to prepare for battle. Aela will congratulate you on surviving the initiation and inform you that the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"), a group of werewolf hunters, have inhabited [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") and will not hide the fact that they should be slaughtered right away. She also informs you that Skjor already entered the fort. From this point, Aela will act as your follower, dismissing your current follower if you have one. Head west towards the fort. A number of Silver Hand members will guard the exterior area, so dispose of them and enter the fort.

### Gallows Rock

Aela fighting Krev the Skinner

*"The bastards... somehow they managed to kill Skjor."*

The first room is a sealed-off area, so pull the chain next to the severed werewolf head and proceed forward. The fort is buzzing with enemies and werewolves in cages, both living and dead, all seemingly exposed to torture by their captors. Be on the lookout for the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[The Importance of Where](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Importance_of_Where "Skyrim:The Importance of Where")* in the huge southern chamber, the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill book *[The Last Scabbard of Akrash](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash")* near the workbench, as well as several locked and unlocked chests. Aela will comment on the first dead werewolf you find, which is found next to a set of rare [Torture Tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Tools "Skyrim:Torture Tools").

When you reach the northwestern chamber, Aela will rightfully warn you about Silver Hand leader [Krev the Skinner](/wiki/Skyrim:Krev_the_Skinner "Skyrim:Krev the Skinner"), so be prepared. When the chamber is cleared, a worried Aela will run up onto the podium and discover the dead body of [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor"), obviously killed due to his lycanthropy. Once you speak with her, the quest will end and you will have to find your own way out, through the door to the northeast that was previously barred. Three new [radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions") are now available back in [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") and you will have to complete two of them (for Aela) before you can access the next major quest. However, if a certain amount of time has passed, you may only have to do one radiant quest to begin [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor").[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:The_Silver_Hand#Added_note)*]

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked once you speak with [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") after surviving the initiation:

-  **Blood Oath** (10 points/Bronze) — Become a member of [the Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle")

## Notes

- You don't need to wait until nightfall to meet Skjor. If you leave the Companions' compound, enter another building, and exit the building you entered, he will make his way to the entrance to the Underforge by the time you return, and the quest will continue like normal.
- If you sleep before meeting with Skjor and Aela, you will retain the effects of being Rested, Well Rested or Lover's Comfort until time expires. Your beast's blood will prevent you from getting them again unless you cure your lycanthropy after the Companions questline is completed, so do not sleep in any of the many beds in the Silver Hand base.
- If you have [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, this is your first opportunity to start acquiring werewolf perks. If you're in Whiterun, you can kill and feed on guards and citizens for werewolf experience. Guards killed will respawn eventually, but citizens will stay dead.
- Once you enter the Underforge, you can talk to Aela in her beast form. If you have the *Special Edition*, Nintendo Switch version, or *Anniversary Edition*, you can also engage in conversation with Aela in her beast form (you'll hear her voice as well).
- Unless you have the [Ring of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Ring of Hircine"), transforming is not immediately possible during the Gallows Rock section. This is because Beast Form is considered a greater power, thus there is a one day cooldown before you can transform again. Simply waiting 24 hours will refresh this and allow you to use your new gift to fight the Silver Hand.
- Version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") turns Gallows Rock into a no-reset zone, and makes it unclearable during this quest.
- After being killed in this quest, Krev the Skinner will eventually respawn with the rest of the dungeon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, addresses this issue. A generic boss will spawn instead.

## Bugs

- At the end of running around on your rampage through Whiterun, the screen will fade and load the next sequence in the quest. After it finishes loading, the game automatically closes for no reason.
  - Simply restarting the game and trying again should fix this.
- Sometimes, you can transform again after the Rampage stage, but before the Gallows Rock stage, enabling you to fight the Silver Hand in Beast Form and ignoring the 24 hour cooldown.
- Sometimes, you won't go on the rampage through Whiterun and instead skip straight to the part where you are with Aela, although the 24-hour cooldown period is active. **?**
- Skjor always says "Not now. The Underforge, tonight." even if it is nighttime due to either/or dialogue conditions.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3, addresses this issue. Both dialogue conditions have been merged together.

## Quest Stages

| The Silver Hand (C03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | Aela and Skjor want to speak to me about some kind of special mission for the Companions. *Objective 5:* Talk to Skjor |
| 10 |  | Skjor and Aela say they have some sort of special assignment for me. I'm supposed to meet them underneath the Skyforge tonight. *Objective 10:* Meet with Skjor at night |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Enter the Underforge |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Participate in the blood ritual |
| 25 |  | I have ascended to the Circle which leads the Companions, and now share their blood as a werewolf. To celebrate my new status, Skjor and Aela have invited me to attack a Silver Hand camp nearby. *Objective 25:* Talk to Aela |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Kill the werewolf hunters |
| 200 | ☑ | I have ascended to the Circle which leads the Companions, and now share their blood as a werewolf. Aela led me to a Silver Hand stronghold where Skjor fell in battle. She has enlisted me on her quest for revenge. |
|  |  | *(After killing Krev)* *Objective 31:* Talk to Aela |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage C03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest C03`.

# Skyrim:The Spiced Wine

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Convince [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") to hand over some spices.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Evette San](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San "Skyrim:Evette San") |
| Location(s): | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") |
| Reward: | 25 gold and 2 Bottles of [Spiced Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 (Evette) |
| ID: | SolitudeFreeform06 |

Evette needs a shipment of spices for her Spiced Wine.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Evette San](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San "Skyrim:Evette San").
2. Persuade [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") to hand over the goods.
3. Return to Evette.

### The Spiced Wine

[Evette San](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San "Skyrim:Evette San") is a [food vendor](/wiki/Skyrim:Food_Vendor "Skyrim:Food Vendor") who is famous for her [Spiced Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine"). You can find her at her market stall in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") during the day. She may ask you *"You wouldn't have a few minutes to run down to the docks would you?"* If you are willing to help her, she will tell you *"I've got a shipment of Spices the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") is holding up. I need someone to convince them to release it."*

Get out of the city and follow the road down to the harbor area. You can find [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") near the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") during the day. Talk to her about Evette's shipment. Vittoria will say, *"Ah yes. If she wants to pay the two thousand gold tariff than we'll be all set."* At this point, you can try to persuade or bribe Vittoria. You must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade her. You can also pay the 2000 gold tariff for the shipment.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| *"Sure, I'll pay the tariff."* (2000 gold) | *"You will? I mean of course you will. You can tell Evette San her shipment will be brought up to Solitude shortly."* | | | | Return to Evette |
| *"Evette can't afford a tariff. She can barely afford her stand."* **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"I suppose I could make an exception. I do like her spiced wine. Fine, tell Evette San her shipment will be brought up to Solitude shortly."* **Failed**: *"That's not my problem."* | | | | **Passed**: Return to Evette **Failed**: Nothing |
| *"I'm sure we can work something out."* **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: *"That would be acceptable. You can tell Evette San her shipment will be brought up to Solitude shortly."* **Failed**: *"I'm afraid your*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *bargaining without the metal to back it up."* | | | | **Passed**: Return to Evette **Failed**: Nothing |

Return to Evette with the good news and she will be very happy. *"Thank you so much. I swear it's a fight with them every shipment."* Then she will give you two bottles of Spiced Wine for your troubles. You can also take more drinks from her stall freely.

## Notes

- If the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") is completed, this quest will become unavailable.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage SolitudeFreeform06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest SolitudeFreeform06`.

# Skyrim:The Staff of Hasedoki

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dillonn241](/wiki/User:Dillonn241 "User:Dillonn241"), checked by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Locate a legendary staff that's been smuggled into Skyrim.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading the [smuggler's trade notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Smuggler%27s_Trade_Notes "Skyrim:Smuggler's Trade Notes") |
| Location(s): | Bandit camp north of Whiterun, road west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass") |
| Reward: | [Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki (item)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE045\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki") |

A strange Orc is questing for a legendary staff

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Locate and read the *[Smuggler's Trade Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Smuggler%27s_Trade_Notes "Skyrim:Smuggler's Trade Notes")* at the bandit camp west of [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=22032&y=3456&zoom=17&legacy=true).
2. Obtain the *[Smuggler's Ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Smuggler%27s_Ledger "Skyrim:Smuggler's Ledger")* from [Modig Gilgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Modig_Gilgar "Skyrim:Modig Gilgar") at his besieged cart near the [Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-4648&y=-8009).
3. Enter [Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass") and take the [Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki (item)") from [Ivara of Olenveld](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivara_of_Olenveld "Skyrim:Ivara of Olenveld").

### Smuggled Goods

Travel to an [unmarked bandit camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Unmarked_Bandit_and_Forsworn_Camps "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") located beneath a cliff, west of [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=22032&y=3456&zoom=17&legacy=true). Once there, you must deal with the hostile [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and locate the *[Smuggler's Trade Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Smuggler%27s_Trade_Notes "Skyrim:Smuggler's Trade Notes")* (not to be confused with the *[Smugglers' Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Smugglers%27_Note "Skyrim:Smugglers' Note")* located nearby). Reading it will reveal that the smugglers were recently approached by an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") looking to purchase the [Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki (item)"), a legendary artifact which they had recently sold to someone else. The smugglers sold this Orc the location of the buyers, planning to intercept and ambush him. Be wary if you are looting the camp, as opening the nearby chest will cause more bandits to spawn.

[Bonemen](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneman "Skyrim:Boneman") fill the passages of Brittleshin Pass

The ambush site is located along the road west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), next to the ruined house near the [Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-4648&y=-8009). The Orc in question, [Modig Gilgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Modig_Gilgar "Skyrim:Modig Gilgar"), will be found standing over the bodies of multiple bandits. He will turn hostile if you get too close, so you are left with the option to either kill him or pickpocket him to obtain the *[Smuggler's Ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Smuggler%27s_Ledger "Skyrim:Smuggler's Ledger")*. Reading this will reveal the location of the buyers: [Ivara of Olenveld](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivara_of_Olenveld "Skyrim:Ivara of Olenveld") and [Lushak gra-Ragdam](/wiki/Skyrim:Lushak_gra-Ragdam "Skyrim:Lushak gra-Ragdam"), located in [Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass"). Be sure to check Modig's cart for loot, including a copy of *[To Raise the Living](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Raise_the_Living "Skyrim:To Raise the Living")* as well as a container named Modig's Satchel which holds minor loot.

### A Path to the Soul Cairn

You must now venture to [Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass"), and enter either through its north or south entrance. Taking the southern approach will result in marginally fewer enemies to face. The enemies in question are [bonemen](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneman "Skyrim:Boneman"), which appear in addition to the usual undead [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") encountered in Brittleshin Pass.

You will need to make your way to the inner sanctum, where the boss level [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") would usually be present. In his place, you will find Lushak gra-Ragdam and Ivara of Olenveld, two necromancers who will be hostile on sight. Beware Ivara, as she wields the Staff of Hasedoki. She can repeatedly use the staff to immobilize you. Once you've defeated them both, the remaining bonemen will disappear, leaving you free to loot and exit the cave. Lushak carries copies of *[Arkay the Enemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Arkay_the_Enemy "Skyrim:Arkay the Enemy")* and *[The Black Arts On Trial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arts_On_Trial "Skyrim:The Black Arts On Trial")*, the latter being an [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill book. Ivara carries copies of *[The Light and the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Light_and_the_Dark "Skyrim:The Light and the Dark")*, *[Ivara's Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivara%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Ivara's Notes")*, and *[Souls, Black and White](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls,_Black_and_White "Skyrim:Souls, Black and White")*, as well as the Staff itself. Reading her notes will reveal that the two necromancers traveled all the way from the island of [Olenveld](/wiki/Lore:Olenveld "Lore:Olenveld") to open a portal to the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") and offer Hasedoki's soul to earn the favor of the [Ideal Masters](/wiki/Skyrim:Ideal_Master_Crystal "Skyrim:Ideal Master Crystal"). Loot his Staff from Ivara's corpse to end this plot and complete the quest.

The Staff creates a permanent 40-point [ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward "Skyrim:Ward") protection while being held, and when cast it will ragdoll and forcefully knock targets backwards. (This includes you during your fight against Ivara.) If the target then dies within 60 seconds, they will be [soul trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

## Notes

- Ivara, Lushak, and the three bonemen will spawn in Brittleshin Pass as soon as Modig Gilgar is killed or pickpocketed. Reading the ledger is optional. Brittleshin Pass is not reset by this. If you have not cleared it previously, Ivara will kill the necromancer boss, clearing the dungeon.
- Completing the quest will cause Modig Gilgar and his cart to immediately disappear.

## Quest Stages

| The Staff of Hasedoki (ccBGSSSE045\_Quest) | | |

| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

| 10 |  | I've heard rumors of smugglers near Whiterun trading black market items. I should investigate the area to see what I can uncover. *Objective 10:* Investigate the Smuggler's Den |
| 20 |  | I've found a smuggler's note which may provide further information on their transactions. *Objective 20:* Read the smuggler's trade notes |
| 30 |  | I've found a smuggler's note which detailed the sale of a powerful staff to a necromancer somewhere west of Whiterun. While the location was not written in the note, it was apparently sold to an Orc who was interested in obtaining the staff. As the smuggler's planned to ambush and rob the Orc, I should go to the location and find out what happened. *Objective 30:* Go to the site of the ambush |
| 40 |  | On the road west of Whiterun I've encountered a hostile Orc besieged by bandits. It appears conversation is not an option. *Objective 40:* Kill or pickpocket the Orc |

According to the ledger, the current owners of the staff are two necromancers holed up in Brittleshin Pass. *Objective 60:* Find the necromancers in Brittleshin Pass |
| 70 |  | I've killed the necromancer Ivara of Olenveld. |
| 80 |  | I've killed the necromancer Lushak gra-Ragdam. |
| 90 |  | Inside Brittleshin Pass I was attacked by two necromancers, Ivara of Olenveld and Lushak gra-Ragdam. In their possession was the artifact they purchased from the smugglers, the Staff of Hasedoki. *Objective 90:* Retrieve the necromancer's staff |
| 100 |  | Inside Brittleshin Pass I was attacked by two necromancers, Ivara of Olenveld and Lushak gra-Ragdam. In their possession was the artifact they purchased from the smugglers, the Staff of Hasedoki. |
| 200 | ☑ | Inside Brittleshin Pass I was attacked by two necromancers, Ivara of Olenveld and Lushak gra-Ragdam. In their possession was the artifact they purchased from the smugglers, the Staff of Hasedoki. After defeating them both, I retrieved the staff from the body of Ivara. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE045_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE045_Quest`.
